 343:     def add_house(self, target_id: str):
 344:         """Dynamically add a new house to an existing pole or lateral."""
 345:         if target_id not in self.nodes:
 346:             return "Target node not found"
 347: 
 348:         target = self.nodes[target_id]
 349: 
 350:         # Determine next ID
 351:         h_nodes = [nid for nid in self.nodes.keys() if nid.startswith('H') and nid != "HOSP"]
 352:         h_idx = max([int(nid.replace('H', '')) for nid in h_nodes]) + 1 if h_nodes else 0
 353:         new_id = f"H{h_idx}"
 354: 
 355:         # Visual spacing offset
 356:         import random
 357:         offset_y = 50 if target.y < 500 else -50
 358:         offset_x = random.randint(-20, 20)
 359: 
 360:         h = GridNode(
 361:             new_id,
 362:             node_type="house",
 363:             x=target.x + offset_x,
 364:             y=target.y + offset_y
 365:         )
 366:         h.load = random.uniform(0.2, 0.6)
 367:         h.generation = random.uniform(0.1, 0.35)
 368:         h._base_load = h.load
 369:         h._base_generation = h.generation
 370: 
 371:         if h._base_generation >= 0.25:
 372:             h.role = "generation"
 373:         elif h._base_generation >= 0.15:
 374:             h.role = "storage"
 375:         else:
 376:             h.role = "load"
 377: 
 378:         h.label = f"House {h_idx}"
 379:         h.priority = 3
 380: 
 381:         self.nodes[new_id] = h
 382:         self.graph.add_node(new_id)
 383:         self._add_edge(target_id, new_id, capacity=3.0, resistance=0.01)
 384: 
 385:         return f"Added {new_id} to {target_id}"
 386: 
 387:     def _add_edge(self, u: str, v: str, capacity: float = None, resistance: float = None,
 388:                   active: bool = True, switch_type: str = None, is_tie_switch: bool = False,
 389:                   has_switch: bool = False):
 390:         """
 391:         Add a physical line between two nodes.
 392:         switch_type: "sectionalizer" | "tie" | None
 393:         switch_status is derived from `active`: open=False → 'open', True → 'closed'
 394:         has_switch kept for backward compat (True if switch_type is set).
 395:         """
 396: 
 397:         # Interactive constraints logic
 398:         n_u = self.nodes.get(u)
 399:         n_v = self.nodes.get(v)
 400: 
 401:         if not n_u or not n_v:
 402:             raise ValueError(f"Nodes {u} and {v} must exist to connect.")
 403: 
 404:         types = {n_u.node_type, n_v.node_type}
 405: 
 406:         # Hard constraint rules preventing random spaghetti logic
 407:         if "house" in types and "house" in types and len(types) == 1:
 408:             raise ValueError("Houses cannot connect directly to houses.")
 409:         if "generator" in types and "house" in types:
 410:             raise ValueError("Generators cannot feed houses directly (requires transformers).")
 411: 
 412:         # Euclidean Distance calculation
 413:         dx = n_u.x - n_v.x
 414:         dy = n_u.y - n_v.y
 415:         dist = math.hypot(dx, dy)
 416: 
 417:         # Dynamic physical resistance based natively on drawn line length
 418:         if resistance is None:
 419:             resistance = max(0.001, dist * 0.0001)
 420: 
 421:         # Dynamic generic capacity based on distance and type (simplified)
 422:         if capacity is None:
 423:             if "generator" in types: capacity = 30.0
 424:             elif "step_up" in types: capacity = 15.0
 425:             elif "substation" in types: capacity = 15.0
 426:             elif "transformer" in types: capacity = 10.0
 427:             elif "service" in types or "pole" in types: capacity = 5.0
 428:             else: capacity = 2.0
 429: 
 430:         if switch_type is not None:
 431:             has_switch = True   # auto-set for backward compat
 432:         switch_status = "open" if not active else "closed"
 433: 
 434:         edge_attrs = {
 435:             'capacity': capacity, 'resistance': resistance, 'flow': 0.0,
 436:             'active': active, 'has_switch': has_switch, 'is_tie_switch': is_tie_switch,
 437:             'switch_type': switch_type or ("tie" if is_tie_switch else ("sectionalizer" if has_switch else None)),
 438:             'switch_status': switch_status
 439:         }
 440: 
 441:         # FIX: Add edge in ONE direction only (parent → child)
 442:         # Power flows: substation → transformer → pole → house
 443:         # Reverse edge added ONLY for tie switches (controlled bidirectional)
 444:         self.graph.add_edge(u, v, **edge_attrs)
 445: 
 446:         # Tie switches allow reverse flow - add reverse edge only for ties
 447:         if is_tie_switch and active:
 448:             reverse_attrs = edge_attrs.copy()
 449:             reverse_attrs['reverse_tie'] = True  # Mark as reverse tie edge
 450:             self.graph.add_edge(v, u, **reverse_attrs)
 451: 
 452:     def get_downstream_nodes(self, start):
 453:         visited = set()
 454:         stack = [start]
 455: 
 456:         while stack:
 457:             node = stack.pop()
 458: 
 459:             for _, child, data in self.graph.out_edges(node, data=True):
 460:                 if not data.get("active", True):
 461:                     continue
 462: 
 463:                 if child not in visited:
 464:                     visited.add(child)
 465:                     stack.append(child)
 466: 
 467:         return visited
 468: 
 469:     def move_node(self, node_id: str, new_x: float, new_y: float):
 470:         """Updates spatial coordinates and dynamically recalcs edge physics based on stretching."""
 471:         if node_id not in self.nodes:
 472:             raise ValueError(f"Unknown node {node_id}")
 473: 
 474:         node = self.nodes[node_id]
 475:         node.x = new_x
 476:         node.y = new_y
 477: 
 478:         # Update all physical connected line resistances
 479:         for neighbor in self.graph.neighbors(node_id):
 480:             n_neighbor = self.nodes[neighbor]
 481:             dx = node.x - n_neighbor.x
 482:             dy = node.y - n_neighbor.y
 483:             dist = math.hypot(dx, dy)
 484:             # Apply dynamic resistance (0.0001 Ohms per pixel as base metric)
 485:             self.graph[node_id][neighbor]["resistance"] = max(0.001, dist * 0.0001)
 486: 
 487:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 488:     # Per-Timestep Simulation
 489:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 490: 
 491:     def get_time_of_day(self) -> int:
 492:         """Maps simulation timestep → hour of day (0-23) on a 24-step cycle."""
 493:         return self.timestep % 24
 494: 
 495:     def step(self) -> dict:
 496:         """Backward compatibility for existing tests."""
 497:         self.update_generation()
 498:         return self.update_power_flow()
 499: 
 500:     def update_generation(self):
 501:         """Step 1: Calculate generation (solar + wind) and loads."""
 502:         self.timestep += 1
 503: 
 504:         self._handle_reclosers()
 505: 
 506:         self._apply_time_curves()
 507: 
 508:         for node in self.nodes.values():
 509:             node.weather = 0.8 if self.storm_active else 0.0
 510:             if not node.failed and not node.isolated:
 511:                 node.step(dt=1.0, timestep=self.timestep)
 512: 
 513:     def update_power_flow(self) -> dict:
 514:         """Step 3: Physics flow (BFS + voltage) directly after EMS balances."""
 515:         self._simulate_energy_flow()
 516:         self._update_stress()
 517: 
 518:         return self.get_state()
 519: 
 520:     def _handle_reclosers(self):
 521:         """
 522:         Auto-reclose logic for feeder-head distribution reclosers.
 523:         If a recloser tripped (active=False), but it hasn't reached lockout,
 524:         wait `reclose_delay` and then attempt to close it again.
 525:         """
 526:         to_remove = []
 527:         for (u, v), (target_time, attempt_count) in list(self.reclose_queue.items()):
 528:             if self.timestep >= target_time:
 529:                 edge = self.graph[u][v]
 530:                 if attempt_count < edge.get("reclose_max", 3):
 531:                     edge["active"] = True
 532:                     edge["switch_status"] = "closed"
 533:                     edge["reclose_attempts"] = attempt_count + 1
 534:                     self.event_log.append(f"🔄 Recloser {u}─{v} auto-reclosing (attempt {attempt_count+1})...")
 535:                 else:
 536:                     edge["locked_out"] = True
 537:                     self.event_log.append(f"❌ Recloser {u}─{v} locked out permanently.")
 538:                 to_remove.append((u, v))
 539: 
 540:         for k in to_remove:
 541:             self.reclose_queue.pop(k, None)
 542: 
 543:     def _apply_time_curves(self):
 544:         """
 545:         Scale generation according to 24h curves.
 546:         - Houses:       solar curve (SOLAR_CURVE)
 547:         - Wind farms:   wind curve  (WIND_CURVE)
 548:         - Nuclear:      flat baseline (no curve — always available)
 549:         - Solar farms:  SOLAR_CURVE at grid scale
 550:         - Coal:         demand-following, no time curve applied here
 551:         """
 552:         hour         = self.get_time_of_day()
 553:         solar_factor = SOLAR_CURVE[hour]
 554:         wind_factor  = WIND_CURVE[hour]
 555:         load_factor  = LOAD_CURVE[hour]
 556:         storm_boost  = 0.25 if self.storm_active else 0.0
 557: 
 558:         for node in self.nodes.values():
 559:             if node.failed or node.isolated:
 560:                 continue
 561: 
 562:             noise = random.uniform(0.95, 1.05)
 563: 
 564:             # House prosumer solar
 565:             if node.node_type == "house":
 566:                 node.load       = round(node._base_load * (load_factor + storm_boost) * noise, 4)
 567:                 node.generation = round(node._base_generation * solar_factor * noise, 4)
 568: 
 569:             # Wind generator — follows WIND_CURVE
 570:             elif node.node_type == "generator" and node.source_type == "wind":
 571:                 wind_noise = random.uniform(0.88, 1.12)   # winds are more variable
 572:                 storm_penalty = 0.7 if self.storm_active else 1.0
 573:                 node.generation = round(node._base_generation * wind_factor * wind_noise * storm_penalty, 4)
 574: 
 575:             # Nuclear generator — flat baseload, never curves down
 576:             elif node.node_type == "generator" and node.source_type == "nuclear":
 577:                 node.generation = round(node._base_generation * random.uniform(0.98, 1.01), 4)
 578: 
 579:             # Solar farm — same curve as house solar at grid scale
 580:             elif node.source_type == "solar":
 581:                 storm_cut = 0.5 if self.storm_active else 1.0
 582:                 node.generation = round(node._base_generation * solar_factor * noise * storm_cut, 4)
 583: 
 584:             # Coal/conventional generators drift slightly
 585:             elif node.node_type == "generator" and node.source_type == "coal":
 586:                 drift = random.gauss(0, 0.015) - (0.03 if self.storm_active else 0)
 587:                 node.generation = round(max(0.0, min(12.0, node.generation + drift)), 4)
 588: 
 589: 
 590:     def _isolate_fault_segments(self):
 591:         """
 592:         Segment-based isolation: if any node or edge fails within a segment,
 593:         the entire segment is isolated by opening its boundary switches.
 594: 
 595:         A segment is explicitly defined as the set of nodes BETWEEN two switches
 596:         on the network graph (not just the faulted node's immediate neighbors).
 597:         This prevents wrong sections from being isolated.
 598: 
 599:         The identified fault segment is stored in self.last_fault_segment for:
 600:           - Frontend overlay rendering
 601:           - FLISR log transparency
 602:           - Test assertion
 603: 
 604:         IMPORTANT: This method ONLY acts when there is an actual active fault.
 605:         On a healthy grid it returns immediately to prevent stale isolation cascades.
 606:         """
 607:         # ── Early exit if nothing is failed or tripped ────────────────────
 608:         has_failed_nodes  = any(n.failed for n in self.nodes.values())
 609:         has_tripped_cable = any(
 610:             not d.get("active") and not d.get("switch_type")
 611:             for _, _, d in self.graph.edges(data=True)
 612:         )
 613:         if not has_failed_nodes and not has_tripped_cable:
 614:             return   # healthy grid — nothing to isolate
 615: 
 616:         # FIX: Use directed graph for proper fault propagation (downstream only)
 617:         # Build directed segment graph - maintain direction from source to downstream
 618:         segment_graph = nx.DiGraph()
 619: 
 620:         # ── Segment graph: ONLY active non-switch edges in ONE direction ─────────
 621:         # This carves the network into segments bounded by switches.
 622:         # Use ONLY active edges to avoid including broken cables in propagation calc
 623:         SWITCH_TYPES = ("sectionalizer", "recloser", "tie")
 624:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
 625:             # CRITICAL: Only use ACTIVE edges - don't include broken cables
 626:             if not data.get("active", True):
 627:                 continue
 628:             if data.get("switch_type") not in SWITCH_TYPES and not data.get("is_tie_switch"):
 629:                 # Add edge in ONE direction only (parent → child)
 630:                 # descendants(u) will find all nodes that receive power FROM u
 631:                 segment_graph.add_edge(u, v)
 632: 
 633:         for nid in self.nodes:
 634:             segment_graph.add_node(nid)
 635: 
 636:         faulted_segments: set[frozenset] = set()
 637: 
 638:         # ── Detect faults from failed nodes ───────────────────────────────────
 639:         # FIX: Use descendants() to get only DOWNSTREAM nodes (direction of flow)
 640:         # This ensures when LA0_2 fails, only LA0_2 + downstream are affected,
 641:         # NOT LA0_1 (which is upstream)
 642:         for nid, node in self.nodes.items():
 643:             if node.failed:
 644:                 # Get only downstream nodes using get_downstream_nodes (strict direction)
 645:                 downstream = self.get_downstream_nodes(nid)
 646:                 # Include the failed node itself
 647:                 downstream.add(nid)
 648:                 comp = frozenset(downstream)
 649:                 faulted_segments.add(comp)
 650: 
 651:         # ── Detect faults from tripped (non-switch) cables ────────────────────
 652:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
 653:             if not data.get("active") and not data.get("switch_type"):
 654:                 if u in segment_graph:
 655:                     # Tripped cable affects downstream from the break point using directional flow
 656:                     downstream = self.get_downstream_nodes(u)
 657:                     downstream.add(u)
 658:                     comp = frozenset(downstream)
 659:                     faulted_segments.add(comp)
 660: 
 661:         # ── Open boundary switches for all faulted segments ───────────────────
 662:         # Also build the explicit fault segment descriptor.
 663:         all_start_switches: list[str] = []
 664:         all_end_switches:   list[str] = []
 665:         all_affected_nodes: list[str] = []
 666: 
 667:         for comp in faulted_segments:
 668:             boundary_switches: list[tuple[str, str]] = []
 669: 
 670:             for u in comp:
 671:                 for nbr in self.graph.successors(u):
 672:                     if nbr not in comp:
 673:                         edge_data = self.graph[u][nbr]
 674:                         sw_type   = edge_data.get("switch_type")
 675:                         if sw_type in SWITCH_TYPES:
 676:                             if edge_data.get("active", True):
 677:                                 edge_data["active"]        = False
 678:                                 edge_data["switch_status"] = "fault_locked"
 679:                                 boundary_switches.append((u, nbr))
 680:                                 self.event_log.append(
 681:                                     f"🔒 {sw_type.capitalize()} {u}─{nbr} opened to isolate fault segment."
 682:                                 )
 683: 
 684:             # Record the explicit segment descriptor
 685:             if boundary_switches:
 686:                 sw_nodes = [s for pair in boundary_switches for s in pair]
 687:                 all_start_switches.append(boundary_switches[0][0])
 688:                 all_end_switches.append(boundary_switches[-1][1])
 689:                 all_affected_nodes.extend([n for n in comp if n not in sw_nodes])
 690: 
 691:         # ── Persist last fault segment (used by get_state + frontend overlay) ─
 692:         if faulted_segments:
 693:             self.last_fault_segment = {
 694:                 "start_switch":   all_start_switches[0] if all_start_switches else None,
 695:                 "end_switch":     all_end_switches[-1]  if all_end_switches   else None,
 696:                 "affected_nodes": list(set(all_affected_nodes)),
 697:             }
 698:         else:
 699:             # No new faults — keep existing segment until explicitly cleared
 700:             pass
 701: 
 702:     def _simulate_energy_flow(self):
 703:         """
 704:         Backward Sweep Flow Algorithm (proper power flow for radial grids).
 705: 
 706:         Step 1: Compute demand bottom-up (backward sweep)
 707:         Step 2: Distribute power top-down (forward sweep)
 708: 
 709:         This ensures proper flow splitting based on actual load demands,
 710:         not just equal division among children.
 711:         """
 712:         from collections import deque
 713: 
 714:         # -----------------------------
 715:         # 1. RESET FLOW (CRITICAL)
 716:         # -----------------------------
 717:         for u, v in self.graph.edges():
 718:             self.graph[u][v]["flow"] = 0.0
 719:             self.graph[u][v]["source_type"] = None
 720: 
 721:         for node_id, node in self.nodes.items():
 722:             # BATTERY DISCHARGE
 723:             if node.node_type == "battery" and getattr(node, "battery_level", 1.0) > 0.2:
 724:                 node.generation += getattr(node, "discharge_rate", 5.0)
 725:                 node.source_type = "battery"
 726: 
 727:             # SUPERCAPACITOR DISCHARGE
 728:             if node.node_type == "supercap" and getattr(node, "supercap_level", 1.0) > 0.1:
 729:                 node.generation += getattr(node, "discharge_rate", 5.0)
 730:                 node.source_type = "supercap"
 731: 
 732:             # SOLAR
 733:             if node.node_type == "solar" or getattr(node, "source_type", "") == "solar":
 734:                 node.generation = getattr(node, "solar_output", getattr(node, "generation", 5.0))
 735:                 node.source_type = "solar"
 736: 
 737:         # -----------------------------
 738:         # 2. FIND ALL SOURCES (MULTI-SOURCE)
 739:         # -----------------------------
 740:         sources = [
 741:             nid for nid, n in self.nodes.items()
 742:             if not n.failed and n.generation > 0.01
 743:         ]
 744: 
 745:         if not sources:
 746:             return
 747: 
 748:         # -----------------------------
 749:         # 3. BUILD TOPOLOGICAL ORDER (for backward sweep)
 750:         # -----------------------------
 751:         # Get all nodes in proper topological order: sources first, leaves last
 752:         # For power flow: generators -> substation -> transformer -> pole -> house
 753:         #
 754:         # We use a BFS from leaves UP to sources, then reverse to get proper order
 755: 
 756:         # Find all leaf nodes (nodes with no successors = end of feeders)
 757:         leaves = [nid for nid in self.graph.nodes() if not list(self.graph.successors(nid))]
 758: 
 759:         order = []
 760:         visited = set()
 761:         queue = deque(leaves)
 762: 
 763:         while queue:
 764:             node = queue.popleft()
 765:             if node in visited:
 766:                 continue
 767:             visited.add(node)
 768:             order.append(node)
 769: 
 770:             # Add predecessors (parents) to queue - go UP toward sources
 771:             for parent in self.graph.predecessors(node):
 772:                 if parent not in visited:
 773:                     queue.append(parent)
 774: 
 775:         # Reverse to get top-down order (sources first, leaves last)
 776:         order.reverse()
 777: 
 778:         # -----------------------------
 779:         # 4. BACKWARD SWEEP: Compute total demand at each node
 780:         # -----------------------------
 781:         total_demand = {}
 782: 
 783:         for node in order:
 784:             node_obj = self.nodes[node]
 785:             # Node's own load
 786:             node_load = getattr(node_obj, 'load', 0) or 0
 787: 
 788:             # Sum of children's demands (outgoing edges)
 789:             children_demand = 0.0
 790:             for child in self.graph.successors(node):
 791:                 edge = self.graph[node][child]
 792:                 if edge.get("active", True):
 793:                     children_demand += total_demand.get(child, 0.0)
 794: 
 795:             total_demand[node] = node_load + children_demand
 796: 
 797:         # -----------------------------
 798:         # 5. FORWARD SWEEP: Distribute power from sources
 799:         # -----------------------------
 800:         # Process in forward topological order (sources first)
 801:         for node in reversed(order):
 802:             node_obj = self.nodes[node]
 803:             node_gen = getattr(node_obj, 'generation', 0) or 0
 804: 
 805:             if node_gen <= 0:
 806:                 continue
 807: 
 808:             # Distribute this node's generation to its children based on their demands
 809:             node_demand = total_demand.get(node, 0)
 810: 
 811:             if node_demand <= 0:
 812:                 continue
 813: 
 814:             # Children that need power
 815:             children = [
 816:                 c for c in self.graph.successors(node)
 817:                 if self.graph[node][c].get("active", True) and total_demand.get(c, 0) > 0
 818:             ]
 819: 
 820:             if not children:
 821:                 continue
 822: 
 823:             for child in children:
 824:                 edge = self.graph[node][child]
 825:                 child_demand = total_demand.get(child, 0)
 826: 
 827:                 # Flow = portion of generation proportional to child's demand
 828:                 flow = (child_demand / node_demand) * node_gen
 829: 
 830:                 edge["flow"] += flow
 831:                 self.graph[node][child]["source_type"] = getattr(node_obj, "source_type", "none")
 832: 
 833:         # -----------------------------
 834:         # 6. Track received power & mark isolated nodes
 835:         # -----------------------------
 836:         energized = set()
 837:         for source in sources:
 838:             energized.update(self.get_downstream_nodes(source))
 839:             energized.add(source)
 840: 
 841:         # Track received power at each node for visualization
 842:         for nid in self.nodes:
 843:             node = self.nodes[nid]
 844:             if nid in energized and not node.failed:
 845:                 node.isolated = False
 846:                 # received_power = total power arriving at this node
 847:                 received = 0.0
 848:                 for pred in self.graph.predecessors(nid):
 849:                     edge = self.graph[pred][nid]
 850:                     if edge.get("active", True):
 851:                         received += edge.get("flow", 0)
 852:                 node.received_power = max(0.0, received)
 853:             else:
 854:                 node.isolated = True
 855:                 node.voltage = 0.0
 856:                 node.received_power = 0.0
 857: 
 858: 
 859: 
 860: 
 861:     def _multi_agent_coordination(self):
 862:         """
 863:         Enhanced multi-agent coordination with bidirectional flow support.
 864:         Nodes with excess offer energy to deficient neighbours with priority routing.
 865:         """
 866:         # First pass: identify surplus and deficit nodes
 867:         surplus_nodes = []
 868:         deficit_nodes = []
 869: 
 870:         for node_id, node in self.nodes.items():
 871:             if node.failed or node.isolated:
 872:                 continue
 873:             if node.excess_energy > 0.1:
 874:                 surplus_nodes.append((node_id, node.excess_energy))
 875:             elif node.deficit > 0.1:
 876:                 deficit_nodes.append((node_id, node.deficit))
 877: 
 878:         # Second pass: match surplus to deficit with path optimization
 879:         for surplus_id, surplus_amount in surplus_nodes:
 880:             if surplus_amount <= 0:
 881:                 continue
 882: 
 883:             surplus_node = self.nodes[surplus_id]
 884: 
 885:             # Find best deficit neighbor using shortest path
 886:             best_match = None
 887:             best_distance = float('inf')
 888: 
 889:             for deficit_id, deficit_amount in deficit_nodes:
 890:                 if deficit_amount <= 0:
 891:                     continue
 892: 
 893:                 try:
 894:                     path = nx.shortest_path(self.graph, surplus_id, deficit_id, weight='resistance')
 895:                     distance = len(path) - 1  # hop count
 896: 
 897:                     if distance < best_distance:
 898:                         best_distance = distance
 899:                         best_match = (deficit_id, deficit_amount)
 900:                 except nx.NetworkXNoPath:
 901:                     continue
 902: 
 903:             if best_match:
 904:                 deficit_id, deficit_amount = best_match
 905:                 deficit_node = self.nodes[deficit_id]
 906: 
 907:                 # Transfer energy with efficiency loss
 908:                 transfer_amount = min(surplus_amount, deficit_amount, 0.2)
 909:                 efficiency = max(0.85, 1.0 - 0.02 * best_distance)  # distance-based efficiency
 910:                 received_amount = transfer_amount * efficiency
 911: 
 912:                 surplus_node.excess_energy -= transfer_amount
 913:                 deficit_node.deficit = max(0.0, deficit_node.deficit - received_amount)
 914:                 deficit_node.generation = min(2.5, deficit_node.generation + received_amount * 0.95)
 915: 
 916:                 # Update flow on the path
 917:                 path = nx.shortest_path(self.graph, surplus_id, deficit_id, weight='resistance')
 918:                 for i in range(len(path) - 1):
 919:                     u, v = path[i], path[i + 1]
 920:                     if self.graph.has_edge(u, v):
 921:                         self.graph[u][v]['flow'] = self.graph[u][v].get('flow', 0) + transfer_amount
 922: 
 923:     def _update_stress(self):
 924:         """Enhanced stress computation with voltage regulation and reactive power awareness."""
 925:         for node in self.nodes.values():
 926:             if node.failed or node.isolated:
 927:                 continue
 928: 
 929:             # Voltage deviation stress (only penalize drops beyond healthy 5% margin)
 930:             v_dev = max(0.0, abs(node.voltage - 1.0) - 0.05) / 0.15
 931: 
 932:             # Frequency deviation stress (allow small 0.2 Hz drift)
 933:             f_dev = max(0.0, abs(node.frequency - 50.0) - 0.2) / 1.3
 934: 
 935:             # Reactive power stress (inferred from voltage-frequency coupling)
 936:             reactive_stress = max(0.0, (v_dev + f_dev) - 0.2) / 0.8
 937: 
 938:             # Load factor stress (high utilization) - only for generators
 939:             # Substations and transformers do not generate, so comparing load/generation is invalid.
 940:             if node.node_type == "generator":
 941:                 load_factor = node.load / max(node.generation + 0.1, 1.0)
 942:                 utilization_stress = max(0.0, load_factor - 0.8) / 0.2
 943:             else:
 944:                 utilization_stress = 0.0  # Houses/Transformers/Poles
 945: 
 946:             # Combine stresses with weights
 947:             node.stress_level = float(min(1.0,
 948:                 0.40 * v_dev +
 949:                 0.30 * f_dev +
 950:                 0.15 * reactive_stress +
 951:                 0.15 * utilization_stress
 952:             ))
 953: 
 954:             # Add voltage regulation logic
 955:             if node.node_type in ("transformer", "substation"):
 956:                 # Transformers can provide voltage support
 957:                 if v_dev > 0.1:
 958:                     # Boost voltage by adjusting tap (simplified)
 959:                     node.voltage = min(1.08, node.voltage + 0.02)
 960:                 elif v_dev < 0.05 and node.voltage > 0.98:
 961:                     # Reduce voltage to save energy
 962:                     node.voltage = max(0.95, node.voltage - 0.01)
 963: 
 964:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 965:     # User Control Interactions
 966:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 967: 
 968:     def add_user_node(self, node_type: str, x: float = 0.0, y: float = 0.0) -> dict:
 969:         """User API to add a node at an explicit CAD coordinate."""
 970:         if len(self.nodes) >= 500:
 971:             raise ValueError("Max nodes (500) reached.")
 972: 
 973:         if node_type == "generator":
 974:             gens = sum(1 for n in self.nodes.values() if n.node_type == "generator")
 975:             if gens >= 20:
 976:                 raise ValueError("Max generators (20) reached.")
 977: 
 978:         prefix = node_type[0].upper()
 979:         existing = [int(nid[1:]) for nid in self.nodes.keys() if nid.startswith(prefix) and nid[len(prefix):].isdigit()]
 980:         next_id = f"{prefix}{max(existing) + 1 if existing else 0}"
 981: 
 982:         node = GridNode(next_id, node_type=node_type, x=x, y=y)
 983:         if node_type == "generator":
 984:             node.generation = random.uniform(5.0, 8.0)
 985:             node.load = 0.1
 986:         elif node_type == "substation":
 987:             node.generation = 0.0
 988:             node.load = random.uniform(1.0, 2.0)
 989:         elif node_type == "transformer":
 990:             node.generation = 0.0
 991:             node.load = random.uniform(0.5, 1.5)
 992:         elif node_type == "solar":
 993:             node.generation = random.uniform(1.0, 3.0)
 994:             node.load = 0.0
 995:             node.role = "generation"
 996:             node.source_type = "solar"
 997:         elif node_type == "wind":
 998:             node.generation = random.uniform(1.5, 4.0)
 999:             node.load = 0.0
1000:             node.role = "generation"
1001:             node.source_type = "wind"
1002:         elif node_type == "battery":
1003:             node.generation = 0.0
1004:             node.load = 0.0
1005:             node.role = "storage"
1006:             node.source_type = "battery"
1007:             node.battery_capacity = random.uniform(2.0, 6.0)
1008:             node.battery_level = 0.9
1009:         elif node_type == "supercap":
1010:             node.generation = 0.0
1011:             node.load = 0.0
1012:             node.role = "support"
1013:             node.supercap_capacity = 2.0
1014:             node.supercap_level = 1.0
1015:         else:
1016:             node.generation = random.uniform(0.0, 0.2)
1017:             node.load = random.uniform(0.2, 0.8)
1018: 
1019:         node._base_generation = node.generation
1020:         node._base_load = node.load
1021: 
1022:         if node.node_type == "house":
1023:             if node._base_generation >= 0.25:
1024:                 node.role = "generation"
1025:             elif node._base_generation >= 0.15:
1026:                 node.role = "storage"
1027:             else:
1028:                 node.role = "load"
1029: 
1030:         self.nodes[next_id] = node
1031:         self.graph.add_node(next_id)
1032:         return {"id": next_id, "node_type": node_type, "x": x, "y": y}
1033: 
1034:     def delete_node(self, node_id: str) -> str:
1035:         """User API to delete a node and all its incident edges."""
1036:         if node_id not in self.nodes:
1037:             raise ValueError(f"Node {node_id} not found.")
1038:         self.graph.remove_node(node_id)
1039:         del self.nodes[node_id]
1040:         return f"Deleted node {node_id}"
1041: 
1042:     def add_user_edge(self, u: str, v: str) -> str:
1043:         """User API to add an edge with realistic physics bounds."""
1044:         if u == v:
1045:             raise ValueError("Cannot connect node to itself.")
1046:         if u not in self.nodes or v not in self.nodes:
1047:             raise ValueError("Node not found.")
1048:         if self.graph.has_edge(u, v):
1049:             raise ValueError("Edge already exists.")
1050: 
1051:         # Defer physics computations (distance and dynamic resistance)
1052:         # and constraint checks directly to the core `_add_edge` builder engine.
1053:         self._add_edge(u, v)
1054:         return f"Connected {u}-{v}"
1055: 
1056:     def cut_user_edge(self, u: str, v: str) -> str:
1057:         """User API to cut a wire entirely."""
1058:         if not self.graph.has_edge(u, v):
1059:             raise ValueError("Edge not found.")
1060: 
1061:         self.graph[u][v]["active"] = False
1062:         msg = f"✂️ Line {u}-{v} was physically cut."
1063:         self.event_log.append(msg)
1064: 
1065:         # Validation metric: Warn on disconnect
1066:         try:
1067:             active_edges = [(nu, nv) for nu, nv, data in self.graph.edges(data=True) if data.get("active", True)]
1068:             test_g = self.graph.edge_subgraph(active_edges)
1069:             if len(test_g.nodes) < len(self.nodes) or not nx.is_connected(test_g):
1070:                 self.event_log.append("⚠️ Grid Collapse Risk: Network partitioning detected!")
1071:         except Exception:
1072:             pass # Failsafe
1073: 
1074:         return msg
1075: 
1076:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
1077:     # Failure Injection & Self-Healing
1078:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
1079: 
1080:     def _balance_transformers(self) -> None:
1081:         """
1082:         Activates normally-open tie-switches to mechanically balance load
1083:         across the distribution layer. Called by SCADA Control Center.
1084:         """
1085:         balanced = 0
1086:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
1087:             nu, nv = self.nodes[u], self.nodes[v]
1088:             if nu.node_type == "switch" or nv.node_type == "switch":
1089:                 if not data.get("active", True) and not nu.failed and not nv.failed:
1090:                     data["active"] = True
1091:                     balanced += 1
1092: 
1093:         if balanced > 0:
1094:             self.event_log.append(f"🔄 Closed {balanced} tie-switches for load balancing.")
1095: 
1096:     def inject_failure(self, node_id: str) -> str:
1097:         if node_id not in self.nodes:
1098:             return f"Unknown node: {node_id}"
1099: 
1100:         self.nodes[node_id].failed = True
1101: 
1102:         # Disable all connected edges (outgoing)
1103:         for neighbor in list(self.graph.neighbors(node_id)):
1104:             if self.graph.has_edge(node_id, neighbor):
1105:                 self.graph[node_id][neighbor]["active"] = False
1106:                 self.graph[node_id][neighbor]["switch_status"] = "fault_locked"
1107:             # Also disable reverse edge if it exists
1108:             if self.graph.has_edge(neighbor, node_id):
1109:                 self.graph[neighbor][node_id]["active"] = False
1110:                 self.graph[neighbor][node_id]["switch_status"] = "fault_locked"
1111: 
1112:         # Mark downstream as isolated
1113:         downstream = self.get_downstream_nodes(node_id)
1114:         for n in downstream:
1115:             self.nodes[n].isolated = True
1116: 
1117:         msg = f"⚠️ Node {node_id} FAILED — segment isolation + FLISR triggered."
1118:         self.event_log.append(msg)
1119:         self.event_log = self.event_log[-20:]  # type: ignore
1120:         return msg
1121: 
1122:     def random_failure(self) -> str:
1123:         """Inject a random failure on a pole node for demo purposes."""
1124:         poles = [nid for nid, n in self.nodes.items() if n.node_type == "pole" and not n.failed]
1125:         if not poles:
1126:             return "No healthy poles available for random failure."
1127:         target = random.choice(poles)
1128:         return self.inject_failure(target)
1129: 
1130:     def _reroute(self, failed_node_id: str) -> str:
1131:         """
1132:         Multi-Path Deterministic FLISR Rerouting via AI Switch Optimization.
1133: 
1134:         Algorithm (3 steps):
1135:           Step 1 — Enumerate ALL candidate paths from each live isolated node to any substation.
1136:                    The search graph only allows closed active cables OR valid open switches.
1137:           Step 2 — Filter paths by: (a) physical validity, (b) capacity, (c) voltage drop.
1138:           Step 3 — Score paths comparing normalized metrics:
1139:                    score = (0.35 * R_norm) + (0.25 * V_norm) + (0.25 * S_norm) - (0.15 * priority_bonus)
1140:                    Minimum score wins.
1141:         """
1142:         # ── Build active sub-graph including open switches but NOT fault-locked ones ────
1143:         search_graph = nx.Graph()
1144:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
1145:             nu, nv = self.nodes[u], self.nodes[v]
1146:             if nu.failed or nv.failed:
1147:                 continue
1148: 
1149:             # Do NOT bypass isolating fault-locked switches
1150:             if data.get("switch_status") == "fault_locked":
1151:                 continue
1152: 
1153:             cap  = data.get("capacity", 1.0)
1154:             flow = abs(data.get("flow", 0.0))
1155:             res  = data.get("resistance", 0.05)
1156: 
1157:             if data.get("active", True):
1158:                 search_graph.add_edge(u, v, capacity=cap, flow=flow, resistance=res, is_switch=False)
1159:             elif data.get("switch_type"):
1160:                 search_graph.add_edge(u, v, capacity=cap, flow=0.0, resistance=res, is_switch=True)
1161: 
1162:         substations = [
1163:             nid for nid, n in self.nodes.items()
1164:             if n.node_type == "substation" and not n.failed and nid in search_graph
1165:         ]
1166:         if not substations:
1167:             return "❌ All substations failed — no rerouting possible."
1168: 
1169:         def capacity_ok(path: list) -> bool:
1170:             for i in range(len(path) - 1):
1171:                 u, v = path[i], path[i + 1]
1172:                 if not search_graph.has_edge(u, v): return False
1173:                 d = search_graph[u][v]
1174:                 if d["flow"] >= 0.9 * d["capacity"]: return False
1175:             return True
1176: 
1177:         def voltage_ok(path: list) -> bool:
1178:             v = self.nodes[path[0]].voltage if path else 1.05
1179:             for i in range(len(path) - 1):
1180:                 u, vn = path[i], path[i + 1]
1181:                 d = search_graph[u][vn]
1182:                 v = v - (d.get("flow", 0.0) * d.get("resistance", 0.05)) / max(v, 0.01)
1183:             return v >= 0.90
1184: 
1185:         def valid_path(path: list) -> bool:
1186:             """Restrict search: ONLY allow un-active traversing if it's explicitly a switch edge."""
1187:             for i in range(len(path) - 1):
1188:                 u, v = path[i], path[i + 1]
1189:                 edge_data = self.graph[u][v]
1190:                 if not edge_data.get("active", True) and not edge_data.get("switch_type"):
1191:                     return False
1192:             return True
1193: 
1194:         def total_resistance(path: list) -> float:
1195:             return sum(search_graph[path[i]][path[i+1]].get("resistance", 0.05) for i in range(len(path)-1))
1196: 
1197:         def switch_count_fn(path: list) -> int:
1198:             return sum(1 for i in range(len(path)-1) if search_graph[path[i]][path[i+1]].get("is_switch", False))
1199: 
1200:         def voltage_drop(path: list) -> float:
1201:             return sum(search_graph[path[i]][path[i+1]].get("resistance", 0.05) * 1.0 for i in range(len(path)-1))
1202: 
1203:         def priority_bonus_fn(path: list) -> float:
1204:             return sum(1.0 / max(1, self.nodes[n].priority) for n in path)
1205: 
1206:         disconnected: list[str] = []
1207:         rerouted_paths: list[list[str]] = []
1208:         switches_flipped_this_cycle = set()
1209: 
1210:         for nid, node in self.nodes.items():
1211:             if nid == failed_node_id or node.failed:
1212:                 continue
1213:             if nid not in search_graph:
1214:                 disconnected.append(nid)
1215:                 continue
1216: 
1217:             # Optimization: only attempt to route nodes that are currently isolated/disconnected
1218:             if not node.isolated and node.voltage > 0.01:
1219:                 # Node seems to have power via existing active graph, skip rerouting
1220:                 continue
1221: 
1222:             all_valid_candidates = []
1223:             for sub in substations:
1224:                 if nid == sub:
1225:                     all_valid_candidates.append([nid])
1226:                     continue
1227:                 try:
1228:                     candidates = list(nx.all_simple_paths(search_graph, nid, sub, cutoff=6))
1229:                 except (nx.NetworkXError, nx.NodeNotFound):
1230:                     continue
1231: 
1232:                 valid = [p for p in candidates if capacity_ok(p) and voltage_ok(p) and valid_path(p)]
1233:                 all_valid_candidates.extend(valid)
1234: 
1235:             if not all_valid_candidates:
1236:                 disconnected.append(nid)
1237:                 continue
1238: 
1239:             # ── Normalised Grid Metrics & Scoring ──
1240:             max_R = max((total_resistance(p) for p in all_valid_candidates), default=0.001) or 0.001
1241:             max_V = max((voltage_drop(p) for p in all_valid_candidates), default=0.001) or 0.001
1242:             max_S = max((switch_count_fn(p) for p in all_valid_candidates), default=1) or 1
1243: 
1244:             best_path = None
1245:             best_score = float("inf")
1246: 
1247:             for p in all_valid_candidates:
1248:                 if len(p) == 1:
1249:                     score = -100.0
1250:                 else:
1251:                     r_norm = total_resistance(p) / max_R
1252:                     v_norm = voltage_drop(p) / max_V
1253:                     s_norm = switch_count_fn(p) / max_S
1254:                     priority_b = priority_bonus_fn(p)
1255: 
1256:                     score = (0.35 * r_norm) + (0.25 * v_norm) + (0.25 * s_norm) - (0.15 * priority_b)
1257: 
1258:                 if score < best_score:
1259:                     best_score = score
1260:                     best_path = p
1261: 
1262:             if best_path and len(best_path) > 1:
1263:                 # Perform the physical auto-switching sequence!
1264:                 switched_any = False
1265:                 for i in range(len(best_path) - 1):
1266:                     u, v = best_path[i], best_path[i + 1]
1267:                     edge = self.graph[u][v]
1268:                     if not edge.get("active", True) and (u, v) not in switches_flipped_this_cycle:
1269:                         edge["active"] = True
1270:                         edge["switch_status"] = "closed"
1271:                         switches_flipped_this_cycle.add((u, v))
1272:                         switches_flipped_this_cycle.add((v, u))
1273:                         switched_any = True
1274:                         self.event_log.append(f"🔄 FLISR AI closed {edge.get('switch_type', 'switch')} {u}─{v} (Priority Score: {best_score:.3f}).")
1275: 
1276:                 if switched_any:
1277:                     rerouted_paths.append(best_path)
1278: 
1279:             # The node is technically connected now
1280:             node.isolated = False
1281: 
1282:         if disconnected:
1283:             for nid in disconnected:
1284:                 self.nodes[nid].isolated = True
1285: 
1286:         self._last_reroute_paths = rerouted_paths[:5]
1287: 
1288:         if not disconnected:
1289:             return f"✅ FLISR AI Optimization Complete: Evaluated via normalized paths bounds."
1290:         return f"⚡ FLISR: {len(disconnected)} node(s) remain isolated."
1291: 
1292:     def get_optimal_path(self, source: str, target: str) -> dict:
1293:         """
1294:         Public API: find the optimal (minimum-loss, capacity-constrained)
1295:         path between any two live nodes using Dijkstra.
1296: 
1297:         Returns path list, total weight, and hop count.
1298:         """
1299:         if source not in self.nodes or target not in self.nodes:
1300:             return {"error": "Node not found", "path": []}
1301: 
1302:         G = nx.Graph()
1303:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
1304:             if not data.get("active", True):
1305:                 continue
1306:             nu, nv = self.nodes[u], self.nodes[v]
1307:             if nu.failed or nv.failed or nu.isolated or nv.isolated:
1308:                 continue
1309:             cap    = data.get("capacity", 1.0)
1310:             flow   = abs(data.get("flow", 0.0))
1311:             load_pct = flow / max(cap, 0.01)
1312:             # Penalise congested lines: weight increases with utilisation
1313:             weight = (1.0 / max(cap, 0.01)) * (1.0 + load_pct)
1314:             G.add_edge(u, v, weight=weight, capacity=cap, load_pct=round(load_pct, 3))
1315: 
1316:         try:
1317:             path = nx.dijkstra_path(G, source, target, weight="weight")
1318:             cost = nx.dijkstra_path_length(G, source, target, weight="weight")
1319:             edges = []
1320:             for i in range(len(path) - 1):
1321:                 e = G[path[i]][path[i+1]]
1322:                 edges.append({
1323:                     "from": path[i], "to": path[i+1],
1324:                     "capacity": e["capacity"], "load_pct": e["load_pct"],
1325:                 })
1326:             return {
1327:                 "path":       path,
1328:                 "hops":       len(path) - 1,
1329:                 "total_cost": round(cost, 4),
1330:                 "edges":      edges,
1331:                 "algorithm":  "Constrained Dijkstra (capacity-weighted)",
1332:             }
1333:         except (nx.NetworkXNoPath, nx.NodeNotFound) as e:
1334:             return {"error": str(e), "path": []}
1335: 
1336:     def restore_node(self, node_id: str) -> str:
1337:         """
1338:         Recover a failed/isolated node AND its downstream nodes.
1339: 
1340:         Switch State Machine:
1341:           fault_locked → closed   (sectionalizer / recloser that isolated the fault)
1342:           fault_locked → open     (tie switch — stays normally-open after repair)
1343:           open / closed → unchanged (switches not involved in this fault stay put)
1344:         """
1345:         if node_id not in self.nodes:
1346:             return f"Unknown node: {node_id}"
1347: 
1348:         self.nodes[node_id].recover()
1349:         self.nodes[node_id].isolated = False
1350: 
1351:         # Restore all downstream nodes (from the failed segment)
1352:         for nid in self.nodes:
1353:             if self.nodes[nid].isolated:
1354:                 self.nodes[nid].isolated = False
1355: 
1356:         # Reactivate ALL switches (boundary will re-close automatically in next step)
1357:         for u, v in self.graph.edges():
1358:             self.graph[u][v]["active"] = True
1359: 
1360:         # Check if grid has any remaining faults
1361:         if not any(n.failed for n in self.nodes.values()):
1362:             # If healthy, proactively reset all protection relays / boundary switches
1363:             self.reset_all_switches()
1364:             msg = f"✅ Node {node_id} restored to service. Grid healthy, protection relays reset."
1365:         else:
1366:             msg = f"🔧 Node {node_id} restored to service. Other active faults remain."
1367: 
1368:         self.event_log.append(msg)
1369:         return msg
1370: 
1371:     def reset_all_switches(self) -> str:
1372:         """
1373:         Reset ALL fault-locked switches to their normal idle state.
1374:         Callable after a multi-node repair scenario.
1375:         """
1376:         count = 0
1377:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
1378:             if data.get("switch_status") == "fault_locked":
1379:                 sw_type = data.get("switch_type")
1380:                 if sw_type == "tie":
1381:                     data["active"]        = False
1382:                     data["switch_status"] = "open"
1383:                 else:
1384:                     data["active"]        = True
1385:                     data["switch_status"] = "closed"
1386:                 count += 1
1387:         self.last_fault_segment = {}
1388:         msg = f"🔧 {count} fault-locked switch(es) reset to normal idle state."
1389:         self.event_log.append(msg)
1390:         return msg
1391:

1396:     def trigger_storm(self):
1397:         """
1398:         Activate a storm event — increases load across all nodes and
1399:         reduces solar/wind generation.
1400:         """
1401:         self.storm_active = True
1402:         for node in self.nodes.values():
1403:             if not node.failed:
1404:                 node.load = min(2.0, node.load * 1.35)
1405:                 node.generation = max(0.05, node.generation * 0.6)
1406:         msg = "🌩️ Storm triggered — demand spike, generation reduced."
1407:         self.event_log.append(msg)
1408:         return msg
1409: 
1410:     def clear_storm(self):
1411:         """Deactivate storm."""
1412:         self.storm_active = False
1413:         msg = "☀️ Storm cleared."
1414:         self.event_log.append(msg)
1415:         return msg

1421:     def increase_generation(self, amount: float = 0.3):
1422:         """Boost generation on solar, wind, and substations."""
1423:         count = 0
1424:         for nid, node in self.nodes.items():
1425:             if node.node_type in ["solar", "wind", "substation"] and not node.failed:
1426:                 node.generation = min(2.5, node.generation + amount)
1427:                 count += 1
1428:         return f"⚡ Generation increased by {amount} MW on {count} generation nodes."
1429: 
1430:     def increase_demand(self, amount: float = 0.2):
1431:         """Simulate demand surge across house, hospital, and industry nodes."""
1432:         count = 0
1433:         for nid, node in self.nodes.items():
1434:             if node.node_type in ["house", "hospital", "industry"] and not node.failed:
1435:                 node.load = min(2.0, node.load + amount)
1436:                 count += 1
1437:         return f"📈 Demand increased by {amount} MW across {count} load nodes."
1438: 
1439:     def heal_all(self):
1440:         """Restore all failed/isolated nodes to healthy state."""
1441:         healed = 0
1442:         for node in self.nodes.values():
1443:             if node.failed or node.isolated:
1444:                 node.failed = False
1445:                 node.isolated = False
1446:                 healed += 1
1447:         return f"🔧 Healed {healed} nodes."
1448: 
1449:     def reset(self):
1450:         """Reset entire grid to initial state."""
1451:         self.graph.clear()
1452:         self.nodes.clear()
1453:         self.timestep = 0
1454:         self.storm_active = False
1455:         self.total_energy_loss = 0.0
1456:         self.event_log = []
1457:         self._build_grid()
1458:         return "🔄 Grid reset to initial state."

1464:     def get_active_paths(self) -> list:
1465:         """
1466:         Get all active edges with flow for continuous path animation.
1467:         Returns simplified edge list with from/to/flow for frontend path building.
1468:         """
1469:         paths = []
1470:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
1471:             if data.get("active", True) and abs(data.get("flow", 0)) > 0.001:
1472:                 paths.append({
1473:                     "from": u,
1474:                     "to": v,
1475:                     "flow": data["flow"],
1476:                     "source_type": self.nodes[u].source_type if u in self.nodes else "none",
1477:                     "active": data.get("active", True)
1478:                 })
1479:         return paths
1480: 
1481:     def get_state(self) -> dict:
1482:         """
1483:         Return a full serialisable snapshot of the grid for the frontend.
1484:         Includes last_fault_segment for the UI overlay rendering.
1485:         """
1486:         edges = []
1487:         for u, v, data in self.graph.edges(data=True):
1488:             edges.append({
1489:                 "source":        u,
1490:                 "target":        v,
1491:                 "capacity":      data.get("capacity", 1.0),
1492:                 "flow":          data.get("flow", 0.0),
1493:                 "source_type":   data.get("source_type", None),
1494:                 "active":        data.get("active", True),
1495:                 "is_tie_switch": data.get("is_tie_switch", False),
1496:                 "has_switch":    data.get("has_switch", False),
1497:                 "switch_type":   data.get("switch_type", None),
1498:                 "switch_status": data.get("switch_status",
1499:                                           "closed" if data.get("active", True) else "open"),
1500:                 "resistance":    data.get("resistance", 0.0),
1501:             })
1502: 
1503:         # System-level aggregates
1504:         active_nodes  = [n for n in self.nodes.values() if not n.failed and not n.isolated]
1505:         total_gen     = sum(n.generation for n in active_nodes)
1506:         total_load    = sum(n.load for n in active_nodes)
1507:         avg_voltage   = sum(n.voltage  for n in active_nodes) / max(len(active_nodes), 1)
1508:         avg_freq      = sum(n.frequency for n in active_nodes) / max(len(active_nodes), 1)
1509:         health_score  = max(0.0, 1.0 - sum(n.stress_level for n in self.nodes.values()) / len(self.nodes))
1510: 
1511:         # Count failed vs isolated (not both)
1512:         failed_count = sum(1 for n in self.nodes.values() if n.failed)
1513:         isolated_count = sum(1 for n in self.nodes.values() if n.isolated and not n.failed)
1514: 
1515:         # Edge-based flow for animation (already edge-level, not route-based)
1516:         active_paths = self.get_active_paths()
1517: 
1518:         return {
1519:             "timestep":           self.timestep,
1520:             "storm_active":       self.storm_active,
1521:             "nodes":              {nid: n.to_dict() for nid, n in self.nodes.items()},
1522:             "edges":              edges,
1523:             "active_paths":       active_paths,  # Edge-based flow for continuous particle animation
1524:             "last_fault_segment": self.last_fault_segment,   # UI overlay data
1525:             "system": {
1526:                 "total_generation": round(float(total_gen),   4),   # type: ignore
1527:                 "total_load":       round(float(total_load),  4),   # type: ignore
1528:                 "balance":          round(float(total_gen - total_load), 4),  # type: ignore
1529:                 "avg_voltage":      round(float(avg_voltage), 4),   # type: ignore
1530:                 "avg_frequency":    round(float(avg_freq),    4),   # type: ignore
1531:                 "health_score":     round(float(health_score),4),   # type: ignore
1532:                 "total_energy_loss":round(float(self.total_energy_loss), 4),  # type: ignore
1533:                 "failed_count":     failed_count,
1534:                 "isolated_count":   isolated_count,
1535:             },
1536:             "recent_events": self.event_log[-5:],  # type: ignore
1537:         }
1538: 
1539:     def get_lstm_input(self, node_id: str) -> list:
1540:         """Return the last 10 timesteps of [load, generation, weather] for LSTM."""
1541:         node = self.nodes.get(node_id)
1542:         if not node:
1543:             return [[0.5, 0.5, 0.0]] * 10
1544:         result = []
1545:         for l, g in zip(node.load_history, node.gen_history):
1546:             result.append([l, g, node.weather])
1547:         return result
1548: 
1549:     def get_rl_state(self) -> list:
1550:         """
1551:         Flatten core primary nodes (G0-G2, S0-S5) into a fixed vector for the DQN agent,
1552:         plus global context features for better situational awareness.
1553:         This completely decouples the AI dimension scale from the dynamic house graph!
1554:         Format per node: [voltage, frequency, load, generation, stress]
1555:         Globals: [total_load, total_generation, balance, avg_voltage, avg_freq, failed_count, isolated_count]
1556:         """
1557:         state_vec = []
1558:         target_nodes = ["G0", "G1", "G2", "S0", "S1", "S2", "S3", "S4", "S5"]
1559:         for nid in target_nodes:
1560:             if nid in self.nodes:
1561:                 n = self.nodes[nid]
1562:                 state_vec.extend([
1563:                     n.voltage,
1564:                     n.frequency / 50.0,   # normalise around 1.0
1565:                     n.load,
1566:                     n.generation,
1567:                     n.stress_level,
1568:                 ])
1569:             else:
1570:                 state_vec.extend([0.0] * 5)
1571: 
1572:         # Global features
1573:         active_nodes = [n for n in self.nodes.values() if not n.failed and not n.isolated]
1574:         total_gen = sum(n.generation for n in active_nodes)
1575:         total_load = sum(n.load for n in active_nodes)
1576:         balance = total_gen - total_load
1577:         avg_voltage = sum(n.voltage for n in active_nodes) / max(len(active_nodes), 1)
1578:         avg_freq = sum(n.frequency for n in active_nodes) / max(len(active_nodes), 1)
1579:         failed_count = sum(1 for n in self.nodes.values() if n.failed)
1580:         isolated_count = sum(1 for n in self.nodes.values() if n.isolated)
1581: 
1582:         state_vec.extend([
1583:             total_load,
1584:             total_gen,
1585:             balance,
1586:             avg_voltage,
1587:             avg_freq / 50.0,
1588:             failed_count,
1589:             isolated_count
1590:         ])
1591: 
1592:         return state_vec
1593: 
1594:     def predictive_islanding(self, failed_nodes: list) -> dict:
1595:         """
1596:         Advanced resilience: Form microgrids around generators with sufficient local generation.
1597:         Returns island configuration for major outage scenarios.
1598:         """
1599:         # Find healthy generators
1600:         healthy_generators = [
1601:             nid for nid, node in self.nodes.items()
1602:             if node.node_type == "generator" and not node.failed
1603:         ]
1604: 
1605:         islands = []
1606: 
1607:         for gen_id in healthy_generators:
1608:             # Find all nodes that can be powered by this generator
1609:             reachable = set()
1610:             queue = deque([gen_id])
1611:             visited = set([gen_id])
1612: 
1613:             while queue:
1614:                 current = queue.popleft()
1615:                 for neighbor in self.graph.successors(current):
1616:                     if neighbor not in visited:
1617:                         edge_data = self.graph[current][neighbor]
1618:                         if edge_data.get("active", True):
1619:                             neighbor_node = self.nodes[neighbor]
1620:                             if not neighbor_node.failed and neighbor not in failed_nodes:
1621:                                 visited.add(neighbor)
1622:                                 queue.append(neighbor)
1623: 
1624: 
1625: 
1626:             # Calculate island capacity
1627:             island_nodes = [nid for nid in visited if nid != gen_id]
1628:             total_load = sum(self.nodes[nid].load for nid in island_nodes)
1629:             total_gen = self.nodes[gen_id].generation + sum(
1630:                 self.nodes[nid].generation for nid in island_nodes
1631:             )
1632: 
1633:             # Check if island is viable (generation >= 80% of load)
1634:             if total_gen >= 0.8 * total_load and len(island_nodes) > 0:
1635:                 islands.append({
1636:                     "generator": gen_id,
1637:                     "nodes": island_nodes,
1638:                     "total_load": round(total_load, 2),
1639:                     "total_generation": round(total_gen, 2),
1640:                     "balance_ratio": round(total_gen / max(total_load, 0.1), 2),
1641:                     "size": len(island_nodes)
1642:                 })
1643: 
1644:         return {
1645:             "islands": islands,
1646:             "total_islands": len(islands),
1647:             "coverage": sum(len(i["nodes"]) for i in islands),
1648:             "recommendation": "Form islands" if islands else "Total blackout - no viable islands"
1649:         }
1650: 
1651:     def suggest_tie_lines(self) -> list:
1652:         """
1653:         AI Suggestion Engine (Graph Theory).
1654:         Detects structural vulnerabilities (articulation points) and proposes new minimal-length ties.
1655: 
1656:         IMPROVED: Uses articulation points for LOCAL vulnerability detection (exact single points of failure)
1657:         and suggests connections to nearest alternate feeders for redundancy.
1658:         """
1659:         import networkx as nx
1660:         import random
1661:         suggestions = []
1662:         try:
1663:             # Active core topology (exclude disconnected graphs and minor branches for macro analysis)
1664:             core_nodes = [n for n, node in self.nodes.items() if not node.failed and node.node_type not in ["house", "service"]]
1665:             sub_g = self.graph.subgraph(core_nodes)
1666: 
1667:             # Find generators and their feeder assignments for identifying alternate sources
1668:             generators = [n for n, node in self.nodes.items() if node.node_type == "generator" and not node.failed]
1669: 
1670:             # Exact single points of failure according to graph connectivity
1671:             weak_nodes = list(nx.articulation_points(sub_g))
1672: 
1673:             sampled_weak = random.sample(weak_nodes, min(4, len(weak_nodes)))
1674: 
1675:             for ap in sampled_weak:
1676:                 node_ap = self.nodes[ap]
1677:                 candidates = []
1678: 
1679:                 # Find which feeder this articulation point currently belongs to
1680:                 ap_feeder = None
1681:                 for gen in generators:
1682:                     if nx.has_path(sub_g, ap, gen):
1683:                         ap_feeder = gen
1684:                         break
1685: 
1686:                 for n, node in self.nodes.items():
1687:                     if n == ap or node.node_type in ["house", "service"] or node.failed:
1688:                         continue
1689:                     if not self.graph.has_edge(ap, n):
1690:                         # Ensure we recommend connecting to a DIFFERENT feeder or far branch
1691:                         dist = ((node_ap.x - node.x)**2 + (node_ap.y - node.y)**2)**0.5
1692:                         if dist > 50: # Arbitrary minimum distance so it's not the same pole group
1693:                             # Check if this candidate connects to a DIFFERENT generator (alternate feeder)
1694:                             alt_feeder = False
1695:                             for gen in generators:
1696:                                 if gen != ap_feeder and nx.has_path(sub_g, n, gen):
1697:                                     alt_feeder = True
1698:                                     break
1699: 
1700:                             # Bonus score for alternate feeders
1701:                             score = dist - (100 if alt_feeder else 0)
1702:                             candidates.append((n, score, dist, alt_feeder))
1703: 
1704:                 if candidates:
1705:                     # Sort by score (lower is better) - prioritizes alternate feeders then proximity
1706:                     candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[1])
1707:                     best = candidates[0]
1708:                     target, _, distance, is_alt = best
1709: 
1710:                     reason = f"Articulation point '{ap}' is a single point of failure. "
1711:                     if is_alt:
1712:                         reason += f"Connect to {target} on alternate feeder for true redundancy."
1713:                     else:
1714:                         reason += f"Connect to {target} ({distance:.0f}m) to reduce isolation risk."
1715: 
1716:                     suggestions.append({
1717:                         "source": ap,
1718:                         "target": target,
1719:                         "distance_m": round(distance, 1),
1720:                         "is_alternate_feeder": is_alt,
1721:                         "reason": reason
1722:                     })
1723:         except Exception as e:
1724:             pass
1725:         return suggestions[:4]
1726: 
1727:     def suggest_best_parent(self, x: float, y: float) -> dict:
1728:         """Recommend the optimal grid connection point for a new load."""
1729:         candidates = []
1730:         for n, node in self.nodes.items():
1731:             if node.node_type in ["transformer", "substation", "service", "switch"]:
1732:                 dist = ((node.x - x)**2 + (node.y - y)**2)**0.5
1733:                 if dist < 500:
1734:                     score = dist + (node.load * 150) # Penalize heavily loaded parents
1735:                     candidates.append((n, score, dist))
1736: 
1737:         if candidates:
1738:             candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[1])
1739:             best = candidates[0]
1740:             return {
1741:                 "parent": best[0],
1742:                 "distance": round(best[2], 1),
1743:                 "reason": "Optimal balance of proximity and available capacity."
1744:             }
1745:         return {}

FILE: backend\simulation\grid.py_append.py

   1: # NOTE: This file is an append-patch for grid.py methods.
   2: # Imports below resolve IDE static-analysis warnings.
   3: import random
   4: from simulation.node import GridNode  # type: ignore
   5: 
   6:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   7:     # User / UI Dynamic Grid Creation
   8:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
   9: 
  10: def add_user_node(self, node_type: str, x: float, y: float) -> dict:
  11:         """Adds a new node from the frontend Add Node mode."""
  12: 
  13:         # Determine prefix and simple ID scheme
  14:         prefix_map = {
  15:             "generator": "G",
  16:             "step_up": "SU",
  17:             "substation": "S",
  18:             "transformer": "T",
  19:             "service": "P",  # Using P for Pole/Service
  20:             "house": "H"
  21:         }
  22:         prefix = prefix_map.get(node_type, "U")
  23: 
  24:         # generate unique ID
  25:         import uuid
  26:         nid = f"{prefix}_{str(uuid.uuid4())[:4]}"
  27: 
  28:         node = GridNode(nid, node_type=node_type, x=x, y=y)
  29: 
  30:         # Base parameters
  31:         if node_type == "generator":
  32:             node.generation = random.uniform(5.0, 8.0)
  33:             node.load = 0.1
  34:         elif node_type == "house":
  35:             node.generation = random.uniform(0.1, 0.4)
  36:             node.load = random.uniform(0.2, 0.8)
  37:         else:
  38:             node.generation = 0.0
  39:             node.load = 0.1
  40: 
  41:         node._base_generation = node.generation
  42:         node._base_load = node.load
  43: 
  44:         self.nodes[nid] = node
  45:         self.graph.add_node(nid)
  46: 
  47:         return node.to_dict()
  48: 
  49: def add_user_edge(self, u: str, v: str) -> str:
  50:         """Adds a new edge natively enforcing realistic logic constraint."""
  51:         if u not in self.nodes or v not in self.nodes:
  52:             raise ValueError(f"Both nodes {u} and {v} must exist.")
  53: 
  54:         # Call the internal _add_edge which has the constraints logic + distance computation
  55:         self._add_edge(u, v)
  56:         return f"Connected {u} to {v}"
  57: 
  58: def cut_user_edge(self, u: str, v: str) -> str:
  59:         if self.graph.has_edge(u, v):
  60:             self.graph.remove_edge(u, v)
  61:             return f"Removed link between {u} and {v}"
  62:         raise ValueError(f"No edge exists between {u} and {v}")

FILE: backend\simulation\node.py
