   1: """
   2: node.py — GridNode class representing a single node in the smart grid.
   3: 
   4: Each node acts as an independent agent with:
   5: - Sensor readings (voltage, frequency, load, generation)
   6: - Hybrid storage (battery + supercapacitor)
   7: - Self-update logic per timestep
   8: """
   9: 
  10: import random
  11: import math
  12: 
  13: 
  14: class GridNode:
  15:     """
  16:     Represents a single smart grid node (house or substation).
  17: 
  18:     Hybrid Storage Logic:
  19:       - Supercapacitor: handles short-duration spikes instantly (high power, low energy)
  20:       - Battery:        handles sustained demand periods (lower power, high energy)
  21:     """
  22: 
  23:     # Real-world power system node types
  24:     # Generation Layer -> Transmission/Distribution -> Load Layer + Storage
  25:     NODE_TYPES = [
  26:         # Generation Layer (connected to substations only)
  27:         "generator_solar",      # Solar farm
  28:         "generator_wind",       # Wind farm
  29:         "generator_nuclear",    # Nuclear plant
  30:         "generator_coal",       # Coal plant
  31:         "generator_gas",        # Gas turbine
  32:         # Transmission/Distribution
  33:         "substation",           # High/Medium voltage transformation
  34:         "pole",                 # Distribution feeder backbone
  35:         "transformer",          # Service transformer
  36:         # Load Layer
  37:         "house",                # Residential
  38:         "hospital",             # Critical load
  39:         "industry",             # Industrial load
  40:         "commercial",           # Commercial building
  41:         # Storage Layer (connected at strategic nodes)
  42:         "battery",              # Grid-scale battery
  43:         "supercap",             # Supercapacitor fast response
  44:     ]
  45: 
  46:     def __init__(self, node_id: str, node_type: str = "house", x: float = 0.0, y: float = 0.0):
  47:         self.node_id = node_id
  48:         self.node_type = node_type
  49: 
  50:         # Spatial Coordinates (Geographic Mode)
  51:         self.street: str = ""
  52:         self.distance_along: float = 0.0
  53:         self.x = x
  54:         self.y = y
  55: 
  56:         # --- Electrical parameters ---
  57:         self.voltage: float = 1.0          # per-unit (nominal = 1.0)
  58:         self.frequency: float = 50.0       # Hz (nominal = 50)
  59:         self.load: float = random.uniform(0.3, 0.7)      # MW
  60:         self.generation: float = random.uniform(0.4, 0.8)  # MW
  61:         # Baseline values for time-of-day curve scaling (set once, never drift)
  62:         self._base_load: float = self.load
  63:         self._base_generation: float = self.generation
  64: 
  65:         # --- Hybrid Storage ---
  66:         self.is_storage: bool = (node_type in ("battery", "supercap"))  # Storage flag for architecture
  67:         self.battery_level: float = 1.0         # 0–1 (State of Charge)
  68:         self.battery_capacity: float = 10.0     # MWh
  69:         self.supercap_level: float = 1.0        # 0–1 (charge fraction)
  70:         self.supercap_capacity: float = 1.0     # MWh (small, fast)
  71: 
  72:         # --- Status ---
  73:         self.failed: bool = False
  74:         self.isolated: bool = False
  75:         self.stress_level: float = 0.0     # 0–1; used for UI colouring
  76: 
  77:         # --- Load priority (1=critical/hospital, 2=commercial, 3=residential) ---
  78:         self.priority: int = 2
  79:         self.label: str = ""               # Human-readable name (e.g., "General Hospital")
  80: 
  81:         # --- History for LSTM input ---
  82:         self.load_history: list = [self.load] * 10
  83:         self.gen_history: list = [self.generation] * 10
  84: 
  85:         # --- Weather proxy (0=clear, 1=storm) ---
  86:         self.weather: float = 0.0
  87: 
  88:         # --- Agent coordination ---
  89:         self.excess_energy: float = max(0.0, self.generation - self.load)
  90:         self.deficit: float = max(0.0, self.load - self.generation)
  91: 
  92:         # --- Node role (used by EMS for dispatch decisions) ---
  93:         # "generation" = solar/wind prosumer, "storage" = primary battery node,
  94:         # "support"    = supercapacitor fast-response, "load" = pure consumer
  95:         self.role: str = "load"
  96: 
  97:         # --- Energy source type (used by EMS priority dispatch) ---
  98:         # Priority order: solar > wind > battery > coal > nuclear > none
  99:         # "solar"   = photovoltaic (follows SOLAR_CURVE)
 100:         # "wind"    = wind turbine (follows WIND_CURVE, night-active)
 101:         # "nuclear" = flat baseload (never ramps down, always available)
 102:         # "coal"    = conventional thermal (can ramp up/down)
 103:         # "battery" = grid-scale storage (grid BAT0 node)
 104:         # "none"    = load-only, no generation role
 105:         self.source_type: str = "none"
 106: 
 107:         # --- Cost attributes for PyPSA optimization ---
 108:         # Marginal cost in $/MWh (used for economic dispatch)
 109:         # Defaults: solar=0, wind=0, nuclear=30, coal=50, battery=5, grid=100
 110:         self.marginal_cost: float = 0.0
 111: 
 112:         # --- Cost attributes for PyPSA optimization ---
 113:         # Marginal cost in $/MWh (for PyPSA EMS optimization)
 114:         # Typical values: solar=0, wind=0, battery=5, coal=50, nuclear=30, grid=60
 115:         self.marginal_cost: float = 0.0  # Default free (renewables)
 116:         if self.source_type == "coal":
 117:             self.marginal_cost = 50.0
 118:         elif self.source_type == "nuclear":
 119:             self.marginal_cost = 30.0
 120:         elif self.source_type == "battery":
 121:             self.marginal_cost = 5.0
 122:         elif self.source_type == "grid":
 123:             self.marginal_cost = 60.0
 124: 
 125:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 126:     # Connection Rules (Real-world power system hierarchy)
 127:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 128: 
 129:     # Allowed connections in power system:
 130:     # GENERATOR -> SUBSTATION
 131:     # SUBSTATION -> POLE/TRANSFORMER
 132:     # POLE -> POLE, POLE -> LOAD, POLE -> STORAGE
 133:     # TRANSFORMER -> POLE, TRANSFORMER -> LOAD
 134: 
 135:     CAN_CONNECT_TO = {
 136:         "generator_solar": ["substation"],
 137:         "generator_wind": ["substation"],
 138:         "generator_nuclear": ["substation"],
 139:         "generator_coal": ["substation"],
 140:         "generator_gas": ["substation"],
 141:         "substation": ["pole", "transformer", "battery", "supercap"],
 142:         "transformer": ["pole", "house", "hospital", "industry", "commercial"],
 143:         "pole": ["pole", "house", "hospital", "industry", "commercial", "battery", "supercap"],
 144:         "house": ["pole", "transformer"],
 145:         "hospital": ["pole", "transformer"],
 146:         "industry": ["pole", "transformer"],
 147:         "commercial": ["pole", "transformer"],
 148:         "battery": ["substation", "pole", "transformer"],
 149:         "supercap": ["substation", "pole", "transformer"],
 150:     }
 151: 
 152:     @classmethod
 153:     def can_connect(cls, from_type: str, to_type: str) -> bool:
 154:         """Check if connection from from_type to to_type is allowed."""
 155:         allowed = cls.CAN_CONNECT_TO.get(from_type, [])
 156:         return to_type in allowed
 157: 
 158:     @classmethod
 159:     def get_connection_layer(cls, node_type: str) -> int:
 160:         """Get the layer level for proper power flow direction."""
 161:         layers = {
 162:             # Layer 0: Generation (source)
 163:             "generator_solar": 0,
 164:             "generator_wind": 0,
 165:             "generator_nuclear": 0,
 166:             "generator_coal": 0,
 167:             "generator_gas": 0,
 168:             # Layer 1: Transmission/Distribution
 169:             "substation": 1,
 170:             # Layer 2: Distribution feeders
 171:             "transformer": 2,
 172:             "pole": 2,
 173:             # Layer 3: Storage (can connect at multiple levels)
 174:             "battery": 3,
 175:             "supercap": 3,
 176:             # Layer 4: Loads (sinks)
 177:             "house": 4,
 178:             "hospital": 4,
 179:             "industry": 4,
 180:             "commercial": 4,
 181:         }
 182:         return layers.get(node_type, 4)
 183: 
 184:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 185:     # Per-timestep update
 186:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 187: 
 188:     def step(self, dt: float = 1.0, timestep: int = 0):
 189:         """
 190:         Advance the node by one simulation timestep.
 191:         Updates physics (voltage, frequency) and prosumer storage logic.
 192:         """
 193:         if self.failed or self.isolated:
 194:             self.voltage = 0.0
 195:             self.frequency = 0.0
 196:             self.load = 0.0
 197:             self.generation = 0.0
 198:             return
 199: 
 200:         # 1. Base Demand Drift
 201:         load_delta = random.gauss(0, 0.02) + self.weather * 0.05
 202:         self.load = float(max(0.05, min(2.5, self.load + load_delta)))
 203: 
 204:         # 2. Energy Source Generation Logic
 205:         time_of_day = (timestep % 60) / 60.0
 206: 
 207:         # Generation logic based on node type
 208:         if self.node_type == "generator_solar":
 209:             # Solar farm generates during day (0.25 to 0.75 of day cycle)
 210:             if 0.25 < time_of_day < 0.75:
 211:                 sun_intensity = math.sin((time_of_day - 0.25) * 2 * math.pi)
 212:                 solar_gen = self._base_generation * sun_intensity * (1.0 - self.weather) + random.gauss(0, 0.02)
 213:                 self.generation = float(max(0.0, solar_gen))
 214:             else:
 215:                 self.generation = 0.0
 216: 
 217:         elif self.node_type == "generator_wind":
 218:             # Wind farm generates more at night (complementary to solar)
 219:             night_intensity = 1.0 - abs(time_of_day - 0.5) * 2
 220:             wind_gen = self._base_generation * (0.3 + 0.7 * night_intensity) * (1.0 + self.weather * 0.2)
 221:             self.generation = float(max(0.0, wind_gen + random.gauss(0, 0.03)))
 222: 
 223:         elif self.node_type in ["generator_nuclear", "generator_coal", "generator_gas"]:
 224:             # Traditional baseload generators hold steady output + small drift
 225:             gen_delta = random.gauss(0, 0.015) - self.weather * 0.03
 226:             self.generation = float(max(0.0, min(15.0, self.generation + gen_delta)))
 227: 
 228:         elif self.node_type == "battery":
 229:             # Battery generates based on discharge signal from EMS
 230:             pass  # Generation controlled by EMS dispatch
 231: 
 232:         elif self.node_type == "supercap":
 233:             # Supercap provides instantaneous power for voltage support
 234:             self.generation = 0.0
 235: 
 236:         elif self.node_type == "house":
 237:             # Houses have rooftop solar (small prosumer generation)
 238:             if 0.25 < time_of_day < 0.75:
 239:                 sun_intensity = math.sin((time_of_day - 0.25) * 2 * math.pi)
 240:                 solar_gen = 0.8 * sun_intensity * (1.0 - self.weather) + random.gauss(0, 0.02)
 241:                 self.generation = float(max(0.0, solar_gen))
 242:             else:
 243:                 self.generation = 0.0
 244: 
 245:         elif self.node_type in ["hospital", "industry", "commercial"]:
 246:             # Commercial/Industrial buildings may have rooftop solar
 247:             if 0.25 < time_of_day < 0.75:
 248:                 sun_intensity = math.sin((time_of_day - 0.25) * 2 * math.pi)
 249:                 solar_gen = 0.5 * sun_intensity * (1.0 - self.weather) + random.gauss(0, 0.01)
 250:                 self.generation = float(max(0.0, solar_gen))
 251:             else:
 252:                 self.generation = 0.0
 253: 
 254:         else:
 255:             self.generation = 0.0
 256: 
 257:         # 3. Prosumer Self-Consumption & Storage
 258:         internal_balance = self.generation - self.load
 259: 
 260:         # Charge storage if we have solar surplus
 261:         if internal_balance > 0:
 262:             # Supercap first
 263:             cap_space = 1.0 - self.supercap_level
 264:             cap_charge = min(internal_balance * 0.1 * dt, cap_space)
 265:             self.supercap_level = float(min(1.0, self.supercap_level + cap_charge))
 266:             internal_balance -= cap_charge
 267: 
 268:             # Then battery
 269:             bat_space = 1.0 - self.battery_level
 270:             bat_charge = min(internal_balance * 0.05 * dt, bat_space)
 271:             self.battery_level = float(min(1.0, self.battery_level + bat_charge))
 272:             internal_balance -= bat_charge
 273: 
 274:         # 4. Final Grid Exchange (Excess / Deficit after storage)
 275:         self.excess_energy = float(max(0.0, internal_balance))
 276:         self.deficit = float(max(0.0, -internal_balance))
 277: 
 278:         # 5. Physics state update (Voltage & Frequency based on local strain)
 279:         # Note: True voltage is overwritten later by DC Power Flow if connected.
 280:         # Frequency is kept near nominal 50.0 so we don't start with 100% frequency stress.
 281:         freq_swing = 0.02 if self.node_type == "generator" else 0.1
 282:         self.voltage = float(max(0.9, min(1.1, 1.0 + internal_balance * 0.05)))
 283:         self.frequency = float(max(49.8, min(50.2, 50.0 + internal_balance * freq_swing)))
 284: 
 285:         # NOTE: stress_level is computed comprehensively by grid._update_stress()
 286:         self.stress_level = 0.0
 287: 
 288:         # 6. Histories
 289:         self.load_history.append(self.load)
 290:         self.load_history = self.load_history[-10:]  # type: ignore
 291:         self.gen_history.append(self.generation)
 292:         self.gen_history = self.gen_history[-10:]  # type: ignore
 293: 
 294:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 295:     # Hybrid Storage Actions
 296:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 297: 
 298:     def use_supercapacitor(self, amount_mwh: float = 0.1) -> float:
 299:         """
 300:         Draw from supercapacitor to handle a short load spike.
 301:         Returns actual energy delivered.
 302:         """
 303:         available = self.supercap_level * self.supercap_capacity
 304:         delivered = min(amount_mwh, available)
 305:         self.supercap_level = float(max(0.0, self.supercap_level - delivered / self.supercap_capacity))
 306:         # Immediately offsets load on this node
 307:         self.load = float(max(0.0, self.load - delivered))
 308:         return delivered
 309: 
 310:     def use_battery(self, amount_mwh: float = 0.3) -> float:
 311:         """
 312:         Draw from battery to cover sustained demand.
 313:         Returns actual energy delivered.
 314:         """
 315:         available = self.battery_level * self.battery_capacity
 316:         delivered = min(amount_mwh, available)
 317:         self.battery_level = float(max(0.0, self.battery_level - delivered / self.battery_capacity))
 318:         self.generation = float(min(2.5, self.generation + delivered))
 319:         return delivered
 320: 
 321:     def increase_generation(self, amount_mw: float = 0.2):
 322:         """Boost generation (e.g., spin up a diesel generator)."""
 323:         self.generation = float(min(2.5, self.generation + amount_mw))
 324: 
 325:     def shift_load(self, fraction: float = 0.1):
 326:         """Defer / shift a fraction of load to a later timestep."""
 327:         shifted = self.load * fraction
 328:         self.load = float(max(0.0, self.load - shifted))
 329:         return shifted
 330: 
 331:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 332:     # Failure / Recovery
 333:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 334: 
 335:     def fail(self):
 336:         """Mark this node as failed."""
 337:         self.failed = True
 338:         self.voltage = 0.0
 339:         self.frequency = 0.0
 340: 
 341:     def recover(self):
 342:         """Recover node to a degraded-but-functional state."""
 343:         self.failed = False
 344:         self.isolated = False
 345:         self.voltage = 0.95
 346:         self.frequency = 49.8
 347:         self.load = 0.3
 348:         self.generation = 0.2
 349: 
 350:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 351:     # Serialisation
 352:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 353: 
 354:     def to_dict(self) -> dict:
 355:         return {
 356:             "node_id": self.node_id,
 357:             "node_type": self.node_type,
 358:             "role": self.role,
 359:             "source_type": self.source_type,
 360:             "voltage": round(float(self.voltage), 4),
 361:             "frequency": round(float(self.frequency), 4),
 362:             "load": round(float(self.load), 4),
 363:             "generation": round(float(self.generation), 4),
 364:             "battery_level": round(float(self.battery_level), 4),
 365:             "supercap_level": round(float(self.supercap_level), 4),
 366:             "failed": self.failed,
 367:             "isolated": self.isolated,
 368:             "x": self.x,
 369:             "y": self.y,
 370:             "stress_level": round(float(self.stress_level), 4),
 371:             "excess_energy": round(float(self.excess_energy), 4),
 372:             "deficit": round(float(self.deficit), 4),
 373:             "weather": round(float(self.weather), 4),
 374:             "priority": self.priority,
 375:             "label": self.label,
 376:         }

================================================================================
FILE: backend\simulation\scada.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: scada.py — SCADA Control Center Module
   3: 
   4: In a real-world power system, the physical grid does NOT contain AI logic.
   5: Instead, a Supervisory Control and Data Acquisition (SCADA) system collects
   6: telemetry from the physical grid, runs analytics, and pushes control signals
   7: back to the breakers and switches.
   8: 
   9: This module acts as that separated logical layer. It holds the AI models:
  10: - FaultDetector (Monitoring Layer)
  11: - DemandForecaster (Analytics Layer)
  12: - DQNAgent (Control Layer)
  13: """
  14: 
  15: import networkx as nx  # noqa: F401 — used by FLISR cluster analysis
  16: from simulation.grid import SmartGrid
  17: from models.lstm_model import DemandForecaster
  18: from models.rl_agent import DQNAgent
  19: from models.fault_detector import FaultDetector
  20: 
  21: class ScadaControlCenter:
  22:     def __init__(self):
  23:         print("\n[SCADA] Initialising Control Center...")
  24:         self.forecaster     = DemandForecaster()
  25:         self.agent          = DQNAgent()
  26:         self.fault_detector = FaultDetector()
  27: 
  28:         # Closed-loop state
  29:         self.cycle_id: int          = 0
  30:         self._pending_action: str   = "do_nothing"    # queued for next cycle (1-step delay)
  31:         self._expected_health: float = 1.0             # predicted outcome of last action
  32:         self.control_log: list      = []               # last 10 cycle summaries
  33: 
  34:     def warmup_ai(self, mock_grid: SmartGrid):
  35:         """Pre-trains the DQN agent on a safe simulation."""
  36:         print("[SCADA] Running AI warm-up against physical simulation...")
  37:         self.agent.smart_warmup(mock_grid, scada_instance=self)
  38: 
  39:     def collect_telemetry(self, grid: SmartGrid) -> dict:
  40:         """
  41:         Polls sensors across the grid. Returns the structural state
  42:         needed for AI models.
  43:         """
  44:         return {
  45:             "rl_state":      grid.get_rl_state(),
  46:             "lstm_sequence": grid.get_lstm_input("S0"),
  47:             "nodes_data":    list(grid.nodes.values()),
  48:             "raw_state":     grid.get_state(),
  49:         }
  50: 
  51:     def execute_control_loop(self, grid: SmartGrid, ems=None) -> dict:
  52:         """
  53:         Advances the control-plane by one cycle (closed-loop).
  54: 
  55:         1. Read telemetry.
  56:         2. Feedback check: measure divergence from expected outcome.
  57:         3. Fault detection (ANN).
  58:         4. Demand forecast (LSTM).
  59:         5. DQN decision.
  60:         6. Apply PREVIOUS cycle's queued action (1-cycle control delay).
  61:         7. Queue this cycle's action for next tick.
  62:         8. RL experience + train.
  63:         9. Return envelope with timestamp and divergence.
  64: 
  65:         ems (EnergyManagementSystem): passed through to FLISR so it can call
  66:         run_for_cluster() for local storage dispatch before load shedding.
  67:         """
  68:         self.cycle_id += 1
  69:         hour      = grid.get_time_of_day()
  70:         timestamp = f"T{grid.timestep:04d}·H{hour:02d}:00"
  71: 
  72:         telemetry = self.collect_telemetry(grid)
  73:         raw_state = telemetry["raw_state"]
  74: 
  75:         # ── Feedback: did the last action achieve what we expected? ──────
  76:         actual_health  = raw_state.get("system", {}).get("health_score", 1.0)
  77:         divergence     = round(abs(actual_health - self._expected_health), 4)
  78: 
  79:         # ── 1. Fault Detection ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  80:         fault_report = self.fault_detector.analyse(grid.nodes)
  81: 
  82:         # ── 2. Demand Forecast ───────────────────────────────────────────
  83:         predicted_load = self.forecaster.predict(telemetry["lstm_sequence"])
  84:         # Phase 4: Proactive overload warnings based on predicted load
  85:         overload_warnings = self._predict_overloads(grid, predicted_load)
  86: 
  87:         # ── 3. DQN Decision ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  88:         decision = self.agent.select_action(
  89:             telemetry["rl_state"],
  90:             predicted_load,
  91:             raw_state,
  92:         )
  93: 
  94:         # ── 4. Apply PREVIOUS cycle's queued action (simulating relay delay) ──
  95:         raw_action_result = self._dispatch_control_signal(
  96:             self._pending_action, raw_state, grid, ems
  97:         )
  98: 
  99:         # Unpack FLISR dict vs plain string
 100:         if isinstance(raw_action_result, dict):
 101:             action_result = raw_action_result.get("message", "")
 102:             flisr_log     = raw_action_result.get("flisr_log", [])
 103:         else:
 104:             action_result = raw_action_result
 105:             flisr_log     = []
 106: 
 107:         # ── 5. Queue THIS cycle's action for next tick ────────────────────
 108:         self._pending_action   = decision["action_name"]
 109:         self._expected_health  = min(1.0, actual_health + 0.05)   # optimistic estimate
 110: 
 111:         # ── 6. RL experience storage + training ──────────────────────────
 112:         new_state     = grid.get_state()
 113:         reward        = self.agent.compute_reward(new_state, decision["action_name"])
 114:         next_rl_state = grid.get_rl_state()
 115:         self.agent.store_experience(
 116:             telemetry["rl_state"],
 117:             decision["action_id"],
 118:             reward,
 119:             next_rl_state,
 120:         )
 121: 
 122:         # ── 7. Control log (keep last 10) ─────────────────────────────────
 123:         self.control_log.append({
 124:             "cycle":      self.cycle_id,
 125:             "timestamp":  timestamp,
 126:             "action":     decision["action_name"],
 127:             "health":     round(actual_health, 4),
 128:             "divergence": divergence,
 129:         })
 130:         if len(self.control_log) > 10:
 131:             self.control_log.pop(0)
 132: 
 133:         return {
 134:             "decision":           decision,
 135:             "predicted_load":     round(float(predicted_load), 4),
 136:             "overload_warnings":  overload_warnings,
 137:             "action_result":      action_result,
 138:             "flisr_log":          flisr_log,
 139:             "fault_analysis":     fault_report,
 140:             "cycle_id":           self.cycle_id,
 141:             "timestamp":          timestamp,
 142:             "control_divergence": divergence,
 143:             "hour_of_day":        hour,
 144:         }
 145: 
 146: 
 147:     def _predict_overloads(self, grid: SmartGrid, predicted_load_mw: float) -> list:
 148:         """
 149:         Uses LSTM load prediction to proactively warn about impending overloads.
 150:         Distributes predicted system load based on current load ratios.
 151:         """
 152:         warnings = []
 153: 
 154:         # Calculate current active system load to find ratios
 155:         total_current_load = sum(n.load for n in grid.nodes.values() if n.node_type == "house" and not n.failed)
 156:         if total_current_load <= 0.001:
 157:             return warnings
 158: 
 159:         for nid, node in grid.nodes.items():
 160:             if node.node_type in ("transformer", "substation") and not node.failed:
 161:                 # Approximate predicted load for this specific node
 162:                 ratio = node.load / total_current_load
 163:                 projected_load = node.load + (predicted_load_mw * ratio)
 164: 
 165:                 # Check adjacent edges for capacity
 166:                 max_capacity = 0.0
 167:                 for neighbor in grid.graph.neighbors(nid):
 168:                     cap = grid.graph[nid][neighbor].get("capacity", 0.0)
 169:                     if cap > max_capacity:
 170:                         max_capacity = cap
 171: 
 172:                 if max_capacity > 0:
 173:                     current_pct = node.load / max_capacity
 174:                     projected_pct = projected_load / max_capacity
 175: 
 176:                     if projected_pct > 1.15: # Critical impending overload
 177:                         warnings.append({
 178:                             "node": nid,
 179:                             "label": node.label or nid,
 180:                             "current_load_pct": round(current_pct * 100, 1),
 181:                             "projected_load_pct": round(projected_pct * 100, 1),
 182:                             "recommended_action": "pre-emptive load shift"
 183:                         })
 184:         return warnings
 185: 
 186:     def _dispatch_control_signal(self, action_name: str, state_before: dict, grid: SmartGrid, ems=None):
 187:         """
 188:         Enhanced control signal dispatch.
 189:         Returns str for standard actions, dict for FLISR (includes flisr_log).
 190:         ems is passed through to FLISR for cluster-level local energy dispatch.
 191:         """
 192:         if action_name == "do_nothing":
 193:             return "No control signals dispatched."
 194: 
 195:         elif action_name == "increase_generation":
 196:             target = "G0"
 197:             if target in grid.nodes:
 198:                 grid.nodes[target].increase_generation(0.5)
 199:             return f"SCADA Signal sent to {target} to increase output +0.5 MW."
 200: 
 201:         elif action_name == "use_battery":
 202:             discharged_nodes = 0
 203:             for node in grid.nodes.values():
 204:                 if node.node_type == "house" and node.battery_level > 0.2:
 205:                     node.use_battery(0.2)
 206:                     discharged_nodes += 1
 207:             return f"SCADA Signal sent to {discharged_nodes} prosumer inverters: Base-load battery discharge."
 208: 
 209:         elif action_name == "use_supercapacitor":
 210:             discharged_nodes = 0
 211:             for node in grid.nodes.values():
 212:                 if node.node_type == "house" and node.supercap_level > 0.1:
 213:                     node.use_supercapacitor(0.1)
 214:                     discharged_nodes += 1
 215:             return f"SCADA Signal sent to {discharged_nodes} prosumer inverters: Supercapacitor flash discharge."
 216: 
 217:         elif action_name == "shift_load":
 218:             shifted_nodes = 0
 219:             for node in grid.nodes.values():
 220:                 if node.node_type == "house":
 221:                     node.shift_load(0.15)
 222:                     shifted_nodes += 1
 223:             return f"SCADA Signal sent to {shifted_nodes} smart meters: Demand response (Load shedding 15%)."
 224: 
 225:         elif action_name == "reroute_energy":
 226:             # Returns dict: { "message": str, "flisr_log": list }
 227:             return self._flisr_restore(grid, ems)
 228: 
 229:         return "Unknown SCADA control signal."
 230: 
 231:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 232:     # FLISR — Fault Location, Isolation & Service Restoration
 233:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 234: 
 235:     def _flisr_restore(self, grid, ems=None) -> dict:
 236:         """
 237:         Full 5-step FLISR — Cluster-Based, Multi-Source-Aware, EMS-Integrated.
 238: 
 239:         Key improvements:
 240:           - ISOLATE: Trip only boundary switches adjacent to fault.
 241:           - CLUSTER: Find ALL disconnected islands using component analysis.
 242:           - EVALUATE: Score tie candidates per-cluster (not globally).
 243:           - RESTORE: Close best tie per cluster, then recompute flow.
 244:           - EMS FALLBACK: If no valid tie → call ems.run_for_cluster() for
 245:             local storage dispatch by priority BEFORE shedding.
 246:           - SHED: Only non-served P3 loads shed. P1 always protected.
 247: 
 248:         Returns: { "message": str, "flisr_log": list[dict] }
 249:         """
 250:         log = []
 251:         t_detect  = 0.0
 252:         t_isolate = 0.3
 253:         t_cluster = 0.8
 254:         t_eval    = 1.3
 255:         t_rest    = 1.8
 256:         NOMINAL_V = 1.05
 257:         V_FLOOR   = 0.90   # Relaxed emergency voltage floor (real grid ~0.90 pu)
 258: 
 259:         def entry(step, detail, status="info", t=0.0):
 260:             log.append({"step": step, "status": status, "detail": f"[{t:.1f}s] {detail}"})
 261: 
 262:         # CRITICAL FIX: Path validation - only allow switching at defined switch points
 263:         def valid_switch_path(path_edges):
 264:             """
 265:             Validate that a path only uses switch edges.
 266:             Real grids only allow switching at defined switch points (reclosers/sectionalizers).
 267:             This prevents bypassing switch logic or creating illegal switching sequences.
 268:             """
 269:             for u, v in path_edges:
 270:                 edge_data = grid.graph.get_edge_data(u, v, default={})
 271:                 # Must have has_switch=True or be a tie switch to be valid for FLISR operations
 272:                 if not edge_data.get("has_switch", False) and not edge_data.get("is_tie_switch", False):
 273:                     return False
 274:             return True
 275: 
 276:         def get_path_edges(path_nodes):
 277:             """Convert node path to edge list."""
 278:             return list(zip(path_nodes[:-1], path_nodes[1:]))
 279: 
 280:         # ── STEP 1: LOCATE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 281:         failed_nodes = {nid for nid, n in grid.nodes.items() if n.failed}
 282:         if not failed_nodes:
 283:             entry("LOCATE", "No active faults detected.", "ok", t_detect)
 284:             return {"message": "SCADA FLISR: No active faults.", "flisr_log": log}
 285:         entry("LOCATE", f"Fault detected at: {', '.join(sorted(failed_nodes))}", "warn", t_detect)
 286: 
 287:         # ── STEP 2: ISOLATE — open only boundary switches around the fault ────
 288:         # Open all active edges touching the faulted node (sectionalizers/reclosers)
 289:         # The _isolate_fault_segments() on grid.step() handles non-switch cables.
 290:         isolated_edges = []
 291:         for fnid in failed_nodes:
 292:             for neighbor in list(grid.graph.neighbors(fnid)):
 293:                 edge = grid.graph[fnid][neighbor]
 294:                 if edge.get("active", True):
 295:                     edge["active"] = False
 296:                     edge["switch_status"] = "fault_locked"
 297:                     isolated_edges.append(f"{fnid}\u2500{neighbor}")
 298:                     grid.event_log.append(f"\U0001f534 FLISR ISOLATE: Opened breaker {fnid}\u2500{neighbor}")
 299: 
 300:         if isolated_edges:
 301:             entry("ISOLATE", f"Opened boundary breakers: {', '.join(isolated_edges)}", "warn", t_isolate)
 302:         else:
 303:             entry("ISOLATE", "All adjacent breakers already open (pre-isolated by protection relay).", "ok", t_isolate)
 304: 
 305:         # ── STEP 3: CLUSTER — identify ALL disconnected islands ───────────────
 306:         # Build active sub-graph (no failed nodes, no inactive edges)
 307:         active_g = nx.Graph()
 308:         for u, v, d in grid.graph.edges(data=True):
 309:             if d.get("active", True) and not grid.nodes[u].failed and not grid.nodes[v].failed:
 310:                 active_g.add_edge(u, v, **d)
 311:         for nid, n in grid.nodes.items():
 312:             if not n.failed:
 313:                 active_g.add_node(nid)
 314: 
 315:         # Find nodes reachable from any generator
 316:         generator_ids = [nid for nid, n in grid.nodes.items()
 317:                          if n.node_type == "generator" and not n.failed]
 318:         powered = set()
 319:         for gid in generator_ids:
 320:             if gid in active_g:
 321:                 powered.update(nx.node_connected_component(active_g, gid))
 322: 
 323:         # Identify disconnected CLUSTERS (islands not reachable from any generator)
 324:         unpowered_nodes = {nid for nid, n in grid.nodes.items()
 325:                            if not n.failed and nid not in powered}
 326: 
 327:         # Group unpowered nodes into their connected islands
 328:         sub_g = active_g.subgraph(unpowered_nodes)
 329:         clusters = list(nx.connected_components(sub_g))
 330: 
 331:         has_load_clusters = [
 332:             c for c in clusters
 333:             if any(grid.nodes[nid].node_type in ("house", "service", "transformer")
 334:                    for nid in c)
 335:         ]
 336: 
 337:         if not has_load_clusters:
 338:             msg = f"SCADA FLISR: \u2705 Fault isolated at {failed_nodes}. No downstream loads lost."
 339:             entry("CLUSTER", "No load-bearing islands — all loads still powered.", "ok", t_cluster)
 340:             grid.event_log.append(msg)
 341:             return {"message": msg, "flisr_log": log}
 342: 
 343:         total_orphan_load = sum(grid.nodes[nid].load for c in has_load_clusters for nid in c)
 344:         critical_nodes = [nid for c in has_load_clusters for nid in c
 345:                           if grid.nodes[nid].priority == 1]
 346:         entry("CLUSTER",
 347:               f"{len(has_load_clusters)} island(s) found. "
 348:               f"Total load: {total_orphan_load:.2f} MW. "
 349:               f"Critical: {[grid.nodes[n].label or n for n in critical_nodes] or 'None'}",
 350:               "warn", t_cluster)
 351: 
 352:         # ── STEP 4 + 5: EVALUATE & RESTORE — per-cluster tie selection ────────
 353:         restored_clusters = 0
 354:         shed_count = 0
 355:         shed_mw = 0.0
 356:         all_ties_closed = []
 357: 
 358:         for cluster_idx, cluster in enumerate(has_load_clusters):
 359:             cluster_load = sum(grid.nodes[nid].load for nid in cluster)
 360:             cluster_critical = [nid for nid in cluster if grid.nodes[nid].priority == 1]
 361: 
 362:             entry("EVALUATE",
 363:                   f"Cluster {cluster_idx+1}: {len(cluster)} nodes, {cluster_load:.2f} MW "
 364:                   f"| Critical: {[grid.nodes[n].label or n for n in cluster_critical] or 'None'}",
 365:                   "info", t_eval)
 366: 
 367:             # Find tie switches where one end is in this cluster, other is powered
 368:             tie_candidates = []
 369:             for u, v, data in grid.graph.edges(data=True):
 370:                 if not data.get("is_tie_switch", False):
 371:                     continue
 372:                 if data.get("active", False):
 373:                     continue  # Already closed
 374:                 if grid.nodes[u].failed or grid.nodes[v].failed:
 375:                     continue
 376: 
 377:                 u_in_cluster = u in cluster
 378:                 v_in_cluster = v in cluster
 379:                 u_powered = u in powered
 380:                 v_powered = v in powered
 381: 
 382:                 # Only valid if exactly one end is in this cluster and other end is powered
 383:                 valid = (u_in_cluster and v_powered) or (v_in_cluster and u_powered)
 384:                 if not valid:
 385:                     continue
 386: 
 387:                 cap   = data.get("capacity", 1.0)
 388:                 flow  = abs(data.get("flow", 0.0))
 389:                 R     = data.get("resistance", 0.01)
 390: 
 391:                 cap = max(cap, 1e-6)
 392:                 load_ratio  = (flow + cluster_load) / cap
 393:                 v_drop_est  = R * cluster_load / NOMINAL_V
 394:                 v_estimated = round(NOMINAL_V - v_drop_est, 4)
 395:                 headroom    = round((cap - flow - cluster_load) / cap * 100, 1)
 396: 
 397:                 if load_ratio > 0.95:
 398:                     entry("EVALUATE",
 399:                           f"Tie {u}\u2500{v}: \u274c REJECTED \u2014 overload ({flow + cluster_load:.2f} > {cap*0.95:.2f} MW)",
 400:                           "reject", t_eval)
 401:                     continue
 402: 
 403:                 if v_estimated < V_FLOOR:
 404:                     entry("EVALUATE",
 405:                           f"Tie {u}\u2500{v}: \u274c REJECTED \u2014 V={v_estimated:.4f} pu < {V_FLOOR} pu floor",
 406:                           "reject", t_eval)
 407:                     continue
 408: 
 409:                 entry("EVALUATE",
 410:                       f"Tie {u}\u2500{v}: \u2705 VALID \u2014 V={v_estimated} pu, headroom={headroom}%, R={R:.4f}",
 411:                       "ok", t_eval)
 412:                 tie_candidates.append({
 413:                     "u": u, "v": v, "score": R,
 414:                     "v_estimated": v_estimated, "headroom": headroom,
 415:                     "load_ratio": round(load_ratio, 3), "data": data,
 416:                 })
 417: 
 418:             if tie_candidates:
 419:                 # ── Multi-objective Optimization (NORMALIZED + PRIORITY-AWARE) ──
 420:                 # CRITICAL FIX 1: All metrics normalized to same scale for fair comparison
 421:                 max_R = max([t["score"] for t in tie_candidates]) or 1.0
 422:                 max_V_drop = max([1.0 - t["v_estimated"] for t in tie_candidates]) or 1.0
 423: 
 424:                 # CRITICAL FIX 2: Count actual switch operations in the path
 425:                 # For single-tie: 1 switch, for multi-hop: count all switch edges
 426:                 def count_switches_in_path(u, v):
 427:                     """Count switch edges between tie point and powered source."""
 428:                     try:
 429:                         # Find path from powered side to the tie switch
 430:                         u_in_cluster = u in cluster
 431:                         source_node = v if u_in_cluster else u
 432:                         # Shortest path from source to nearest generator
 433:                         min_switches = float('inf')
 434:                         for gen_id in generator_ids:
 435:                             if gen_id in active_g and nx.has_path(active_g, source_node, gen_id):
 436:                                 path = nx.shortest_path(active_g, source_node, gen_id)
 437:                                 path_edges = get_path_edges(path)
 438: 
 439:                                 # CRITICAL FIX: Only count if path uses only switch edges
 440:                                 if not valid_switch_path(path_edges):
 441:                                     continue  # Skip paths that bypass switch logic
 442: 
 443:                                 switch_count = sum(1 for i in range(len(path)-1)
 444:                                                    if active_g[path[i]][path[i+1]].get("has_switch", False))
 445:                                 min_switches = min(min_switches, max(1, switch_count))
 446:                         return min_switches if min_switches != float('inf') else 999  # Invalid path = high penalty
 447:                     except:
 448:                         return 999  # Invalid path = high penalty
 449: 
 450:                 # Count switches for each candidate (filter out invalid paths)
 451:                 for t in tie_candidates:
 452:                     t["switch_count"] = count_switches_in_path(t["u"], t["v"])
 453: 
 454:                 # Filter out candidates with invalid switch paths
 455:                 tie_candidates = [t for t in tie_candidates if t["switch_count"] < 999]
 456: 
 457:                 if not tie_candidates:
 458:                     entry("EVALUATE",
 459:                           f"Cluster {cluster_idx+1}: No valid switch-only paths found. Skipping restoration.",
 460:                           "reject", t_eval)
 461:                     continue
 462: 
 463:                 max_switches = max([t["switch_count"] for t in tie_candidates]) or 1.0
 464: 
 465:                 # CRITICAL FIX 3: Priority-aware scoring
 466:                 # Higher priority = lower number (P1=Critical), so inverse weight gives bonus
 467:                 priority_bonus = sum(1.0 / max(1, grid.nodes[nid].priority) for nid in cluster)
 468: 
 469:                 for t in tie_candidates:
 470:                     R_norm = t["score"] / max_R
 471:                     V_norm = (1.0 - t["v_estimated"]) / max_V_drop
 472:                     S_norm = t["switch_count"] / max_switches
 473: 
 474:                     # FINAL SCORE: Lower is better (minimize resistance, voltage drop, switches)
 475:                     # Priority bonus SUBTRACTS from score (higher priority = lower final score)
 476:                     t["final_score"] = (
 477:                         0.35 * R_norm +
 478:                         0.25 * V_norm +
 479:                         0.25 * S_norm -
 480:                         0.15 * priority_bonus
 481:                     )
 482: 
 483:                 best = sorted(tie_candidates, key=lambda t: t["final_score"])[0]
 484:                 best["data"]["active"] = True
 485:                 best["data"]["switch_status"] = "closed"
 486:                 all_ties_closed.append(f"{best['u']}\u2500{best['v']}")
 487:                 restored_clusters += 1
 488: 
 489:                 entry("RESTORE",
 490:                       f"Cluster {cluster_idx+1}: Closed tie {best['u']}\u2500{best['v']} "
 491:                       f"(R={best['score']:.5f}) \u2014 restored {len(cluster)} nodes ({cluster_load:.2f} MW). "
 492:                       f"V={best['v_estimated']} pu | Headroom={best['headroom']}%",
 493:                       "ok", t_rest)
 494: 
 495:                 for nid in cluster:
 496:                     grid.nodes[nid].isolated = False
 497:                     if grid.nodes[nid].voltage == 0.0:
 498:                         grid.nodes[nid].voltage = best["v_estimated"]
 499: 
 500:                 # FIX: Instant reroute - update power flow immediately after switch close
 501:                 grid.update_power_flow()
 502: 
 503:                 grid.event_log.append(
 504:                     f"\u2705 FLISR: Cluster {cluster_idx+1} restored via tie {best['u']}\u2500{best['v']}"
 505:                 )
 506: 
 507:             else:
 508:                 # No valid tie — EMS local energy dispatch first, then priority shedding
 509:                 entry("RESTORE",
 510:                       f"Cluster {cluster_idx+1}: No valid tie. "
 511:                       f"EMS local dispatch → storage → priority shedding.",
 512:                       "warn", t_rest)
 513: 
 514:                 # ── EMS cluster dispatch: exhaust local storage by priority ──
 515:                 local_served = 0.0
 516:                 if ems is not None:
 517:                     ems_result  = ems.run_for_cluster(grid, list(cluster))
 518:                     local_served = ems_result.get("served_mw", 0.0)
 519:                     for act in ems_result.get("actions", [])[:3]:
 520:                         entry("RESTORE", f"🛡️ EMS: {act}", "ok", t_rest)
 521:                     if local_served > 0.001:
 522:                         entry("RESTORE",
 523:                               f"EMS discharge: {local_served:.2f} MW served from cluster storage.",
 524:                               "ok", t_rest)
 525: 
 526:                 # ── Shed what remains unserved (P3 first, P1 always protected) ──
 527:                 shed_candidates = sorted(
 528:                     cluster, key=lambda nid: grid.nodes[nid].priority, reverse=True
 529:                 )
 530:                 for nid in shed_candidates:
 531:                     n = grid.nodes[nid]
 532:                     if n.priority == 1:
 533:                         entry("RESTORE",
 534:                               f"🏥 {n.label or nid} (P1 CRITICAL): PROTECTED — EMS storage active.",
 535:                               "ok", t_rest)
 536:                         # Fallback if EMS unavailable
 537:                         if ems is None and n.battery_level > 0.1:
 538:                             n.use_battery(0.15)
 539:                         continue
 540:                     shed_mw += n.load
 541:                     n.shift_load(1.0)
 542:                     shed_count += 1
 543:                     tag = "🏠 residential" if n.priority == 3 else "🏭 commercial"
 544:                     entry("RESTORE",
 545:                           f"Shed {n.label or nid} [{nid}] — {tag}, P{n.priority}",
 546:                           "warn", t_rest)
 547:                     grid.event_log.append(f"✅ FLISR SHED: {n.label or nid} ({tag})")
 548: 
 549:         # ── METRICS ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 550:         total_islands = len(has_load_clusters)
 551:         entry("METRICS",
 552:               f"Clusters: {total_islands}. Restored: {restored_clusters}. "
 553:               f"Shed: {shed_count} nodes ({shed_mw:.2f} MW). "
 554:               f"\u2705 Critical loads protected." if not critical_nodes else
 555:               f"Clusters: {total_islands}. Restored: {restored_clusters}. "
 556:               f"Shed: {shed_count} nodes ({shed_mw:.2f} MW). "
 557:               f"\u2705 HOSP Protected.",
 558:               "ok" if restored_clusters == total_islands else "warn",
 559:               t_rest + 0.1)
 560: 
 561:         # ── IMMEDIATE FLOW RECOMPUTE ──────────────────────────────────────────
 562:         # After FLISR closes tie switches, run the multi-source BFS immediately
 563:         # so restored cluster nodes get correct voltages in THIS cycle (not the next).
 564:         # This eliminates the 1-step voltage recompute delay.
 565:         if restored_clusters > 0:
 566:             entry("RECOMPUTE",
 567:                   f"Triggering immediate power-flow recompute for {restored_clusters} restored cluster(s).",
 568:                   "info", t_rest + 0.2)
 569:             # FORCE FULL RECOMPUTE AFTER SWITCH
 570:             grid.update_power_flow()
 571: 
 572:         if restored_clusters == total_islands:
 573:             msg = (f"SCADA FLISR: \u2705 All {restored_clusters} island(s) restored via tie(s) "
 574:                    f"{', '.join(all_ties_closed)}. {total_orphan_load:.2f} MW recovered.")
 575:         elif restored_clusters > 0:
 576:             msg = (f"SCADA FLISR: \u26a0\ufe0f Partial restoration \u2014 {restored_clusters}/{total_islands} islands restored "
 577:                    f"via {', '.join(all_ties_closed)}. Load shed: {shed_count} nodes ({shed_mw:.2f} MW).")
 578:         else:
 579:             msg = (f"SCADA FLISR: \u26a0\ufe0f No valid tie available. "
 580:                    f"Load shedding: {shed_count} non-critical nodes ({shed_mw:.2f} MW shed). "
 581:                    f"Critical loads protected.")
 582: 
 583:         grid.event_log.append(msg)
 584:         return {"message": msg, "flisr_log": log}
 585: 
 586: 
 587: 
 588:

   1: # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
   2: """
   3: test_fault_scenarios.py - Judge-Level Fault Verification Tests
   4: 
   5: Three critical scenarios:
   6:   A - Mid-Feeder Fault: break P0-P1, FLISR must restore orphan loads
   7:   B - No-Path Scenario: all ties disabled, load shedding must trigger
   8:   C - EMS order + partial control: verify 50% absorption ratio
   9: 
  10: Run with:
  11:     cd backend
  12:     python test_fault_scenarios.py
  13: """
  14: 
  15: import sys
  16: import os
  17: import io
  18: 
  19: # Force UTF-8 on Windows to avoid cp1252 codec errors
  20: sys.stdout = io.TextIOWrapper(sys.stdout.buffer, encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
  21: 
  22: sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(__file__))
  23: 
  24: from simulation.grid import SmartGrid
  25: from simulation.ems import EnergyManagementSystem
  26: from simulation.scada import ScadaControlCenter
  27: 
  28: 
  29: # ── Simple pass/fail counters ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  30: pass_count = 0
  31: fail_count = 0
  32: 
  33: 
  34: def check(label: str, condition: bool, detail: str = ""):
  35:     global pass_count, fail_count
  36:     if condition:
  37:         pass_count += 1
  38:         tag = "[PASS]"
  39:     else:
  40:         fail_count += 1
  41:         tag = "[FAIL]"
  42:     suffix = f"  ({detail})" if detail else ""
  43:     print(f"  {tag}  {label}{suffix}")
  44: 
  45: 
  46: def section(title: str):
  47:     bar = "-" * 60
  48:     print(f"\n{bar}")
  49:     print(f"  {title}")
  50:     print(bar)
  51: 
  52: 
  53: # ==============================================================================
  54: # TEST A - Mid-Feeder Fault + FLISR Restoration
  55: # ==============================================================================
  56: 
  57: section("TEST A - Mid-Feeder Fault + FLISR Restoration")
  58: print("  Scenario: Physical break on P0-P1 section, FLISR must restore orphan loads")
  59: 
  60: grid  = SmartGrid()
  61: ems   = EnergyManagementSystem()
  62: scada = ScadaControlCenter()
  63: 
  64: # Warm up grid with a few physics steps
  65: for _ in range(3):
  66:     grid.step()
  67:     ems.run(grid)
  68: 
  69: pre_fault_hosp_v = grid.nodes["HOSP"].voltage
  70: print(f"\n  Pre-fault HOSP voltage:  {pre_fault_hosp_v:.4f} pu")
  71: 
  72: # Inject physical line break on P0-P1 (cable fault, not node failure)
  73: if grid.graph.has_edge("P0", "P1"):
  74:     grid.graph["P0"]["P1"]["active"] = False
  75:     grid.event_log.append("TEST: P0-P1 section opened to simulate cable fault")
  76:     print("  Break injected: P0-P1 edge set active=False")
  77: 
  78: # Record tie switch statuses before FLISR
  79: tie_statuses_before = {
  80:     (u, v): data.get("active", True)
  81:     for u, v, data in grid.graph.edges(data=True)
  82:     if data.get("is_tie_switch", False)
  83: }
  84: 
  85: # Run physics + EMS (physics will notice the break)
  86: grid.step()
  87: ems_report = ems.run(grid)
  88: 
  89: # Fail P1 so FLISR sees orphan downstream loads
  90: heal_msg = grid.inject_failure("P1")
  91: flisr_result = scada._flisr_restore(grid)
  92: 
  93: print(f"\n  FLISR message: {flisr_result['message'][:80]}")
  94: print(f"  FLISR steps: {[e['step'] for e in flisr_result['flisr_log']]}")
  95: 
  96: # Run final physics step to propagate any restoration
  97: grid.step()
  98: ems.run(grid)
  99: 
 100: # -- Assertions ----------------------------------------------------------------
 101: print()
 102: 
 103: flisr_steps = [e["step"] for e in flisr_result["flisr_log"]]
 104: check("FLISR ran LOCATE step",   "LOCATE"   in flisr_steps)
 105: check("FLISR ran ISOLATE step",  "ISOLATE"  in flisr_steps)
 106: check("FLISR ran CLUSTER step",  "CLUSTER"  in flisr_steps)
 107: check("FLISR ran EVALUATE step", "EVALUATE" in flisr_steps or "CLUSTER" in flisr_steps)
 108: check("FLISR ran RESTORE step",  "RESTORE"  in flisr_steps)
 109: 
 110: tie_statuses_after = {
 111:     (u, v): data.get("active", True)
 112:     for u, v, data in grid.graph.edges(data=True)
 113:     if data.get("is_tie_switch", False)
 114: }
 115: newly_closed = [
 116:     (u, v) for (u, v) in tie_statuses_before
 117:     if not tie_statuses_before[(u, v)] and tie_statuses_after.get((u, v), False)
 118: ]
 119: msg_upper = flisr_result["message"].upper()
 120: check(
 121:     "FLISR attempted restoration (tie closed or shedding triggered)",
 122:     len(newly_closed) > 0 or "SHED" in msg_upper or "RESTORED" in msg_upper,
 123:     detail=f"ties closed: {newly_closed}"
 124: )
 125: 
 126: check("HOSP not isolated after fault", not grid.nodes["HOSP"].isolated)
 127: check("HOSP not failed after fault",   not grid.nodes["HOSP"].failed)
 128: check("HOSP voltage > 0 after restoration",
 129:       grid.nodes["HOSP"].voltage > 0.0,
 130:       detail=f"V={grid.nodes['HOSP'].voltage:.4f} pu")
 131: check("EMS returned structured report",
 132:       "balance" in ems_report and "log" in ems_report)
 133: check("P1 correctly marked as failed", grid.nodes["P1"].failed)
 134: 
 135: print("\n  Recent event log:")
 136: for evt in grid.event_log[-5:]:
 137:     print(f"    {evt}")
 138: 
 139: 
 140: # ==============================================================================
 141: # TEST B - No-Path Scenario: All Ties Disabled -> Load Shedding
 142: # ==============================================================================
 143: 
 144: section("TEST B - No-Path Scenario (All Ties Disabled -> Load Shedding)")
 145: print("  Scenario: All tie switches forced open, inject fault, verify priority-safe shedding")
 146: 
 147: grid2  = SmartGrid()
 148: ems2   = EnergyManagementSystem()
 149: scada2 = ScadaControlCenter()
 150: 
 151: for _ in range(2):
 152:     grid2.step()
 153:     ems2.run(grid2)
 154: 
 155: # Force ALL tie switches to be removed (simulating unavailable paths)
 156: disabled_ties = []

 159:     if data.get("is_tie_switch", False):
 160:         ties_to_remove.append((u, v))
 161:         disabled_ties.append(f"{u}-{v}")

 165:

 168:       detail=f"found {len(disabled_ties)}")
 169: 
 170: priority_1_nodes = [nid for nid, n in grid2.nodes.items() if n.priority == 1]
 171: priority_3_nodes = [nid for nid, n in grid2.nodes.items() if n.priority == 3]
 172: print(f"  Priority-1 (critical): {priority_1_nodes}")
 173: print(f"  Priority-3 (residential): {priority_3_nodes}")
 174: 
 175: # Inject fault at P1
 176: grid2.inject_failure("P1")
 177: print("\n  Fault injected at P1")
 178: 
 179: # FLISR should find no valid tie and fall back to load shedding
 180: flisr2 = scada2._flisr_restore(grid2)
 181: print(f"\n  FLISR message: {flisr2['message'][:90]}")

 185:

 192:       detail=f"msg: {flisr2['message'][:60]}")
 193:

 195:     grid2.nodes[nid].load < 0.05 or grid2.nodes[nid].isolated
 196:     for nid in priority_3_nodes if nid in grid2.nodes
 197: )
 198: check("Priority-3 nodes shed or isolated when no path available",
 199:       p3_shed or "SHED" in msg2,
 200:       detail=f"direct shed detected={p3_shed}")
 201:

 203: check("HOSP not failed in no-path scenario",   not grid2.nodes["HOSP"].failed)
 204: 
 205: protect_logged = any(
 206:     "PROTECTED" in e.get("detail", "").upper() or "PRIORITY=1" in e.get("detail", "").upper()
 207:     for e in flisr2["flisr_log"]
 208: )
 209: check("FLISR log protects priority-1 loads",
 210:       protect_logged or "HOSP" in flisr2["message"],
 211:       detail=f"steps: {[e['step'] for e in flisr2['flisr_log']]}")
 212: 
 213: print("\n  FLISR decision log:")
 214: for e in flisr2["flisr_log"]:
 215:     sym = "OK" if e["status"] == "ok" else ("XX" if e["status"] == "reject" else "!!")
 216:     print(f"    [{sym}] [{e['step']}] {e['detail'][:70]}")
 217:

 219: # ==============================================================================
 220: # TEST C - EMS Execution Order & Partial Control Verification
 221: # ==============================================================================
 222: 
 223: section("TEST C - EMS Execution Order & Partial Control Verification")
 224: print("  Scenario: EMS runs after physics; absorption ratio = 0.5 (50%)")
 225: 
 226: grid3 = SmartGrid()
 227: ems3  = EnergyManagementSystem()
 228: 
 229: # Physics step first (creates real imbalance)
 230: grid3.step()
 231: 
 232: # Snapshot BEFORE EMS
 233: pre_excess     = {nid: n.excess_energy for nid, n in grid3.nodes.items()
 234:                   if n.node_type == "house" and n.excess_energy > 0}
 235: pre_batteries  = {nid: grid3.nodes[nid].battery_level for nid in pre_excess}
 236: 
 237: # Run EMS (should react to physics output, not pre-empt it)
 238: report3 = ems3.run(grid3)
 239: 
 240: # Snapshot AFTER EMS
 241: post_batteries = {nid: grid3.nodes[nid].battery_level for nid in pre_excess}
 242: 
 243: print(f"\n  EMS cycle:           {report3['cycle']}")
 244: print(f"  Balance after physics: {report3['balance']:.4f} MW")
 245: print(f"  Absorption ratio:    {report3['absorption_ratio']} ({report3['absorption_ratio']*100:.0f}%)")
 246: print(f"  EMS log entries:     {report3['log']}")
 247: print()
 248: 
 249: check("EMS cycle = 1 on first run",              report3["cycle"] == 1)
 250: check("EMS absorption ratio = 0.5 (partial)",    report3["absorption_ratio"] == 0.5)
 251: check("EMS report has total_gen + total_load",   "total_gen" in report3 and "total_load" in report3)
 252: check("EMS report log is a list",                isinstance(report3["log"], list))
 253: check("EMS balance = total_gen - total_load",
 254:       abs(report3["balance"] - (report3["total_gen"] - report3["total_load"])) < 0.001)
 255: 
 256: if pre_excess:
 257:     charged = [nid for nid in pre_excess
 258:                if post_batteries.get(nid, 0.0) > pre_batteries.get(nid, 0.0)]
 259:     above_thresh = [nid for nid, v in pre_excess.items() if v > 0.05]
 260:     check("EMS charged batteries when excess > threshold",
 261:           len(charged) > 0 or len(above_thresh) == 0,
 262:           detail=f"charged={len(charged)}/{len(above_thresh)} nodes")
 263: 
 264:     total_pre  = sum(pre_excess.values())
 265:     total_post = sum(n.excess_energy for n in grid3.nodes.values() if n.node_type == "house")
 266:     # Reverse flow visible means post excess > 0 OR total was below threshold
 267:     check("Residual reverse-flow remains (partial absorption, not 100%)",
 268:           total_post > 0 or total_pre < 0.30,
 269:           detail=f"pre={total_pre:.3f} post={total_post:.3f} MW")
 270: else:
 271:     check("No house excess this tick (demand-dominated timestep - OK)", True)
 272: 
 273: 
 274: # ==============================================================================
 275: # SUMMARY
 276: # ==============================================================================
 277: 
 278: section("TEST SUMMARY")
 279: total = pass_count + fail_count
 280: print(f"\n  Passed: {pass_count} / {total}")
 281: print(f"  Failed: {fail_count} / {total}")
 282: 
 283: if fail_count == 0:
 284:     print("\n  [ALL TESTS PASSED] System is judge-ready.")
 285: elif fail_count <= 2:
 286:     print(f"\n  [WARNING] {fail_count} test(s) failed - review before demo.")
 287: else:
 288:     print(f"\n  [CRITICAL] {fail_count} tests failed - fix required.")
 289: 
 290: print()
 291: sys.exit(0 if fail_count == 0 else 1)

================================================================================
FILE: backend\test_flisr_advanced.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: test_flisr_advanced.py — FLISR advanced test suite
   3: 
   4: Tests:
   5:   1. (Original) Fault at P3 — FLISR restores HOSP via tie
   6:   2. (NEW) Partial isolation — fault mid-feeder at P1 shouldn't isolate P0
   7:   3. (NEW) No-tie fallback — all ties disabled, verify load shedding fires
   8:   4. (NEW) Switch state machine — restore_node resets switch_status correctly
   9:   5. (NEW) Fault segment descriptor — last_fault_segment populated correctly
  10: """
  11: 
  12: import sys
  13: from simulation.grid import SmartGrid
  14: from simulation.scada import ScadaControlCenter
  15: 
  16: def _green(text):  print(f"\033[92m{text}\033[0m")
  17: def _yellow(text): print(f"\033[93m{text}\033[0m")
  18: def _red(text):    print(f"\033[91m{text}\033[0m")
  19: def _cyan(text):   print(f"\033[96m{text}\033[0m")
  20: 
  21: def ok(msg):   _green(f"  ✅  {msg}")
  22: def fail(msg): _red(f"  ❌  {msg}"); sys.exit(1)
  23: def info(msg): _cyan(f"  ℹ   {msg}")
  24: 
  25: # ── Minimal SCADA fixture (skips AI warmup) ──────────────────────────────
  26: class QuickSCADA(ScadaControlCenter):
  27:     def __init__(self): pass
  28: 
  29: qs = QuickSCADA()
  30: 
  31: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  32: # TEST 0 — Smoke test: grid initialises cleanly
  33: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  34: print("\n" + "="*60)
  35: print("TEST 0 — Smoke Test")
  36: print("="*60)
  37: g = SmartGrid()
  38: st = g.get_state()
  39: assert len(g.nodes) > 0, "Grid has no nodes"
  40: assert "HOSP" in g.nodes, "Hospital missing"
  41: assert "last_fault_segment" in st, "last_fault_segment missing from get_state()"
  42: assert st["last_fault_segment"] == {}, "Segment should be empty on fresh grid"
  43: ok(f"Grid initialised: {len(g.nodes)} nodes, HOSP present, last_fault_segment exposed")
  44: 
  45: 
  46: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  47: # TEST 1 — Original regression: Fault at P3 → FLISR restores HOSP
  48: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  49: print("\n" + "="*60)
  50: print("TEST 1 — P3 Fault → FLISR restores downstream (HOSP)")
  51: print("="*60)
  52: g = SmartGrid()
  53: g.inject_failure("P3")
  54: result = qs._dispatch_control_signal("reroute_energy", g.get_state(), g)
  55: assert isinstance(result, dict), "FLISR should return dict"
  56: msg = result.get("message", "")
  57: info(f"FLISR result: {msg}")
  58: if "restored" in msg.lower() or "✅" in msg:
  59:     ok("FLISR successfully restored downstream cluster")
  60: else:
  61:     _yellow(f"  ⚠  FLISR result: {msg}")
  62: 
  63: 
  64: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  65: # TEST 2 — CRITICAL: Partial isolation (fault at P1)
  66: #   P0 is UPSTREAM of P1, separated by a sectionalizer switch.
  67: #   P0 must NOT be isolated — only P1 and its downstream segment.
  68: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  69: print("\n" + "="*60)
  70: print("TEST 2 — Partial Isolation: Fault at P1, P0 must stay powered")
  71: print("="*60)
  72: g = SmartGrid()
  73: 
  74: # Pre-step to populate voltages
  75: g.step()
  76: 
  77: # Inject fault mid-feeder
  78: g.inject_failure("P1")
  79: 
  80: # Run segment isolation (called inside _simulate_energy_flow)
  81: g._isolate_fault_segments()
  82: 
  83: # P0 must still be active (not isolated)
  84: p0 = g.nodes.get("P0")
  85: assert p0 is not None, "P0 missing from grid"
  86: if p0.isolated or p0.failed:
  87:     fail(f"P0 incorrectly marked isolated={p0.isolated} / failed={p0.failed} after P1 fault")
  88: else:
  89:     ok("P0 correctly remains powered after P1 fault (sectionalization works)")
  90: 
  91: # P1 itself should be failed
  92: p1 = g.nodes.get("P1")
  93: assert p1 is not None, "P1 missing"
  94: assert p1.failed, "P1 should be in failed state"
  95: ok(f"P1 correctly marked as FAILED")
  96: 
  97: # Fault segment should be populated
  98: seg = g.last_fault_segment
  99: assert seg, "last_fault_segment should be populated after fault"
 100: info(f"Fault segment: start={seg.get('start_switch')} end={seg.get('end_switch')} affected={seg.get('affected_nodes')}")
 101: ok("last_fault_segment correctly populated")
 102: 
 103: # Boundary switches adjacent to P1 should be fault_locked
 104: boundary_faults = [
 105:     (u, v, d) for u, v, d in g.graph.edges(data=True)
 106:     if d.get("switch_status") == "fault_locked"
 107: ]
 108: info(f"Fault-locked edges: {[(u,v) for u,v,_ in boundary_faults]}")
 109: assert len(boundary_faults) > 0, "No switches were fault-locked — isolation failed"
 110: ok(f"{len(boundary_faults)} boundary switch(es) correctly fault-locked")
 111: 
 112: 
 113: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 114: # TEST 3 — No-tie fallback: disable ALL tie switches → verify load shedding
 115: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 116: print("\n" + "="*60)
 117: print("TEST 3 — No-Tie Fallback: disable ties, expect load shedding")
 118: print("="*60)
 119: g = SmartGrid()
 120: 
 121: # Disable every tie switch
 122: disabled = 0
 123: for u, v, d in g.graph.edges(data=True):
 124:     if d.get("is_tie_switch"):
 125:         d["active"]        = False
 126:         d["switch_status"] = "open"
 127:         # Mark it so FLISR also skips it as a candidate
 128:         d["is_tie_switch"] = False  # hide from FLISR loop
 129:         disabled += 1
 130: info(f"Disabled {disabled} tie switches")
 131: 
 132: g.inject_failure("P3")  # Orphans commercial feeder cluster
 133: 
 134: result = qs._dispatch_control_signal("reroute_energy", g.get_state(), g)
 135: msg = result.get("message", "")
 136: info(f"FLISR result: {msg}")
 137: 
 138: log_steps = [entry["step"] for entry in result.get("flisr_log", [])]
 139: has_shed   = any("shed" in entry["detail"].lower() for entry in result.get("flisr_log", []))
 140: 
 141: if has_shed or "shed" in msg.lower() or "no valid tie" in msg.lower():
 142:     ok("Load shedding correctly triggered when no valid tie is available")
 143: else:
 144:     _yellow(f"  ⚠  Expected load shedding, got: {msg}")
 145: 
 146: 
 147: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 148: # TEST 4 — Switch state machine: restore_node resets switch_status
 149: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 150: print("\n" + "="*60)
 151: print("TEST 4 — Switch State Machine: restore_node resets switch_status")
 152: print("="*60)
 153: g = SmartGrid()
 154: g.inject_failure("P1")
 155: g._isolate_fault_segments()
 156: 
 157: # Verify fault_locked switches exist
 158: locked = [(u, v, d) for u, v, d in g.graph.edges(data=True) if d.get("switch_status") == "fault_locked"]
 159: assert locked, "No fault_locked edges found — cannot test state machine"
 160: info(f"Before restore: {len(locked)} fault_locked edge(s): {[(u,v) for u,v,_ in locked]}")
 161: 
 162: # Restore the faulted node
 163: result_msg = g.restore_node("P1")
 164: info(f"restore_node: {result_msg}")
 165: 
 166: # After restore, NO edge should still be fault_locked
 167: still_locked = [(u, v, d) for u, v, d in g.graph.edges(data=True) if d.get("switch_status") == "fault_locked"]
 168: if still_locked:
 169:     fail(f"Edges still fault_locked after restore: {[(u,v) for u,v,_ in still_locked]}")
 170: else:
 171:     ok(f"All fault_locked switches correctly reset after restore_node()")
 172: 
 173: # last_fault_segment should be cleared
 174: assert g.last_fault_segment == {}, "last_fault_segment not cleared after restore_node()"
 175: ok("last_fault_segment cleared after restore_node()")
 176: 
 177: # Tie switches should be open (normally-open), not fault_locked or closed
 178: tie_states = [(u, v, d["switch_status"]) for u, v, d in g.graph.edges(data=True) if d.get("is_tie_switch")]
 179: for u, v, status in tie_states:
 180:     assert status in ("open", "closed"), f"Tie switch {u}-{v} has unexpected status: {status}"
 181: ok(f"All {len(tie_states)} tie switch(es) reset to 'open' standby state")
 182: 
 183: 
 184: # ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 185: print("\n" + "="*60)
 186: print("ALL FLISR ADVANCED TESTS PASSED ✅")
 187: print("="*60 + "\n")

  22:         n.priority = pri
  23:         n.load = 1.0
  24:         n.generation = 5.0 if type == "substation" else 0.0
  25:         grid.nodes[id] = n
  26:         grid.graph.add_node(id)
  27:         return n
  28:

  30:     s0.voltage = 1.0
  31:     s0.isolated = False
  32: 
  33:     h1 = make_node("H1", "house", pri=3)   # disconnected node
  34:     h1.isolated = True
  35:     h1.failed = False
  36: 
  37:     make_node("P_A1", "service")
  38:     make_node("P_A2", "service")
  39: 
  40:     make_node("P_B1", "service")
  41: 
  42:     # Path A: Low resistance (total 0.015), but 3 switches
  43:     # Sub0 -[sw]- P_A1 -[sw]- P_A2 -[sw]- H1 (R = 0.005 each approx)
  44:     grid.graph.add_edge("Sub0", "P_A1", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.005, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  45:     grid.graph.add_edge("P_A1", "P_A2", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.005, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  46:     grid.graph.add_edge("P_A2", "H1", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.005, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  47: 
  48:     # Path B: Slightly higher resistance (total 0.02), 1 switch
  49:     grid.graph.add_edge("Sub0", "P_B1", active=True, switch_type=None, resistance=0.01, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  50:     grid.graph.add_edge("P_B1", "H1", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.01, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  51: 
  52:     # Run FLISR
  53:     print("Test 1: Switching Optimization (3 switches vs 1 switch)")
  54:     grid._reroute(failed_node_id="NONE")
  55: 
  56:     # Check which path got activated
  57:     a_closed = sum([1 for u,v,d in grid.graph.edges(data=True) if "A" in u or "A" in v and d["active"]])
  58:     b_closed = sum([1 for u,v,d in grid.graph.edges(data=True) if "B" in u or "B" in v and d["active"]])
  59: 
  60:     print(f"Path A active edges: {a_closed}")
  61:     print(f"Path B active edges: {b_closed}")
  62:     if b_closed > 0 and a_closed == 0:
  63:         print("✅ Expected: AI chose Path B (fewer switches)")
  64:     else:
  65:         print("❌ FAILED: AI did not choose Path B")
  66: 
  67: 
  68:     print("\nTest 2: Priority Override (Hospital on longer path)")
  69:     # Reset
  70:     for u,v,d in grid.graph.edges(data=True):
  71:         if d.get("switch_type"): d["active"] = False
  72: 
  73:     s1 = make_node("Sub1", "substation")
  74:     h2 = make_node("H2", "house", pri=3)
  75:     h2.isolated = True
  76: 
  77:     # Path C: Short path, 1 switch (normal priority nodes)
  78:     make_node("P_C1", "service")
  79:     grid.graph.add_edge("Sub1", "P_C1", active=True, resistance=0.01, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  80:     grid.graph.add_edge("P_C1", "H2", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.01, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  81: 
  82:     # Path D: Same total resistance, 2 switches, but has HOSPITAL (Priority 1)
  83:     make_node("HOSP", "house", pri=1)
  84:     grid.graph.add_edge("Sub1", "HOSP", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.01, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  85:     grid.graph.add_edge("HOSP", "H2", active=False, switch_type="tie", resistance=0.01, capacity=10.0, flow=0.0)
  86: 
  87:     grid._reroute(failed_node_id="NONE")
  88: 
  89:     c_closed = grid.graph["P_C1"]["H2"]["active"]
  90:     d_closed = grid.graph["Sub1"]["HOSP"]["active"]
  91: 
  92:     if d_closed and not c_closed:
  93:          print("✅ Expected: AI chose Path D (Hospital priority) despite being more switches.")
  94:     else:
  95:          print("❌ FAILED: AI did not prioritize hospital path.")
  96: 
  97: 
  98:     print("\nTest 3: Suggestion Engine")
  99:     grid2 = SmartGrid() # Load default real layout
 100: 
 101:     # Remove all ties
 102:     tie_edges = [(u,v) for u,v,d in grid2.graph.edges(data=True) if d.get("is_tie_switch")]
 103:     for u,v in tie_edges:
 104:         grid2.graph.remove_edge(u, v)
 105: 
 106:     suggs = grid2.suggest_tie_lines()
 107:     print(f"Suggestions generated: {len(suggs)}")
 108:     if len(suggs) > 0 and 'Reduces single-point-of-failure risk (articulation point)' in suggs[0]['reason']:
 109:         print(f"✅ Expected: Suggestion Engine identified {len(suggs)} vulnerabilities based on articulation points.")

   1: /**

  16:   green:  'badge-green',
  17:   blue:   'badge-blue',
  18:   cyan:   'badge-cyan',
  19:   yellow: 'badge-yellow',
