  24: function SystemMetricsCard({ gridState, faultAnalysis }) {
  25:   if (!gridState) return null
  26:   const nodes = Object.values(gridState.nodes || {}).filter(n => !n.is_scada)
  27: 
  28:   const houseNodes = nodes.filter(n => n.node_type === 'house' && n.priority === 3)
  29:   const activeHouses = houseNodes.filter(n => (n.voltage || 0) > 0.1).length
  30: 
  31:   const hospNode = nodes.find(n => n.priority === 1)
  32:   const hospActive = hospNode && (hospNode.voltage || 0) > 0.1
  33: 
  34:   const vsi = faultAnalysis?.system_health ? (faultAnalysis.system_health * 100).toFixed(1) : 100.0
  35: 
  36:   return (
  37:     <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '16px', marginBottom: '16px', border: '1px solid var(--border)' }}>
  38:       <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: 0.5, color: '#f8fafc', marginBottom: 12 }}>
  39:         ⚡ GRID HEALTH: {vsi}%
  40:       </div>
  41:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>
  42:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', padding: '6px 10px', background: hospActive ? 'rgba(34,197,94,0.1)' : 'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)', borderRadius: 4, border: `1px solid ${hospActive ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-red)'}` }}>
  43:           <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600 }}>🏥 Hospital</span>
  44:           <b style={{ fontSize: 13, color: hospActive ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-red)' }}>
  45:             {hospActive ? 'ACTIVE' : 'OFFLINE'}
  46:           </b>
  47:         </div>
  48:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', padding: '6px 10px', background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)', borderRadius: 4 }}>
  49:           <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-secondary)' }}>🏠 Houses Served</span>
  50:           <b style={{ fontSize: 13, color: activeHouses === houseNodes.length ? 'var(--accent-cyan)' : 'var(--accent-yellow)' }}>
  51:             {activeHouses} / {houseNodes.length}
  52:           </b>
  53:         </div>
  54:       </div>
  55:     </div>
  56:   )
  57: }
  58: 
  59: function DemandGauge({ predicted, current }) {
  60:   const pct = Math.min(100, Math.round((predicted / 2.0) * 100))
  61:   const cPct = Math.min(100, Math.round((current / 2.0) * 100))
  62:   const color =
  63:     pct > 75 ? 'var(--accent-red)' :
  64:     pct > 50 ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'var(--accent-green)'
  65: 
  66:   return (
  67:     <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '16px' }}>
  68:       <div className="panel-title">🧠 LSTM Demand Forecast</div>
  69: 
  70:       {/* Circular gauge (SVG) */}
  71:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', margin: '4px 0 12px' }}>
  72:         <svg width="120" height="80" viewBox="0 0 120 80">
  73:           {/* Background arc */}
  74:           <path
  75:             d="M 10,70 A 50,50 0 0,1 110,70"
  76:             fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.06)" strokeWidth="10" strokeLinecap="round"
  77:           />
  78:           {/* Value arc */}
  79:           {pct > 0 && (
  80:             <path
  81:               d="M 10,70 A 50,50 0 0,1 110,70"
  82:               fill="none" stroke={color} strokeWidth="10" strokeLinecap="round"
  83:               strokeDasharray="157"
  84:               strokeDashoffset={157 - (pct / 100) * 157}
  85:               style={{ transition: 'stroke-dashoffset 0.8s ease, stroke 0.5s' }}
  86:             />
  87:           )}
  88:           {/* Label */}
  89:           <text x="60" y="65" textAnchor="middle" fill={color}
  90:             fontSize="18" fontFamily="JetBrains Mono" fontWeight="600">
  91:             {predicted.toFixed(2)}
  92:           </text>
  93:           <text x="60" y="78" textAnchor="middle" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.35)"
  94:             fontSize="9" fontFamily="Inter">
  95:             MW
  96:           </text>
  97:         </svg>
  98:       </div>
  99: 
 100:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
 101:         <span className="metric-label">Current Avg Load</span>
 102:         <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--text-secondary)' }}>
 103:           {current.toFixed(2)} MW
 104:         </span>
 105:       </div>
 106: 
 107:       <div style={{ marginTop: 8 }}>
 108:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 4 }}>
 109:           <span className="metric-label">Predicted Load</span>
 110:           <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color }}>
 111:             {pct > 70 ? '🔴 HIGH' : pct > 40 ? '🟡 MODERATE' : '🟢 LOW'}
 112:           </span>
 113:         </div>
 114:         <div className="progress-bar">
 115:           <div className="progress-fill"
 116:             style={{ width: `${pct}%`, background: color }} />
 117:         </div>
 118:       </div>
 119:     </div>
 120:   )
 121: }
 122: 
 123: function FLISRDecisionLog({ flisrLog }) {
 124:   if (!flisrLog || flisrLog.length === 0) return null
 125: 
 126:   const statusStyle = {
 127:     ok:     { border: 'var(--accent-green)',  bg: 'rgba(34,197,94,0.07)',   icon: '✅' },
 128:     warn:   { border: 'var(--accent-yellow)', bg: 'rgba(234,179,8,0.07)',   icon: '⚠️' },
 129:     reject: { border: 'var(--accent-red)',    bg: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.07)',   icon: '❌' },
 130:     info:   { border: 'var(--accent-cyan)',   bg: 'rgba(0,212,255,0.05)',   icon: '🔹' },
 131:   }
 132: 
 133:   const stepColors = {
 134:     LOCATE:   '#f59e0b',
 135:     ISOLATE:  '#ef4444',
 136:     CLUSTER:  '#8b5cf6',
 137:     EVALUATE: '#3b82f6',
 138:     RESTORE:  '#22c55e',
 139:     METRICS:  '#ec4899',
 140:   }
 141: 
 142:   return (
 143:     <div style={{ padding: '14px', borderRadius: 10, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)', border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.08)' }}>
 144:       <div style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '0.5px', color: 'var(--text-muted)', marginBottom: 10 }}>
 145:         ⚡ FLISR DECISION LOG — THOUGHT PROCESS
 146:       </div>
 147:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 5 }}>
 148:         {flisrLog.map((entry, i) => {
 149:           const s = statusStyle[entry.status] || statusStyle.info
 150:           const stepColor = stepColors[entry.step] || 'var(--accent-cyan)'
 151:           return (
 152:             <div key={i} style={{
 153:               display: 'flex', gap: 8, alignItems: 'flex-start',
 154:               padding: '7px 10px', borderRadius: 7,
 155:               background: s.bg, borderLeft: `2px solid ${s.border}`,
 156:             }}>
 157:               <div style={{ flexShrink: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: 2 }}>
 158:                 <span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 800, color: stepColor,
 159:                                background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 3, padding: '1px 4px',
 160:                                letterSpacing: '0.3px', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono' }}>
 161:                   {entry.step}
 162:                 </span>
 163:               </div>
 164:               <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
 165:                 {entry.detail}
 166:               </span>
 167:             </div>
 168:           )
 169:         })}
 170:       </div>
 171:     </div>
 172:   )

 175: function FaultAnalysisCard({ faultAnalysis }) {
 176: 
 177:   if (!faultAnalysis) return null
 178: 
 179:   const { alerts = [], system_health = 1.0, fault_count = 0 } = faultAnalysis
 180: 
 181:   const healthPct = Math.round(system_health * 100)
 182:   const healthColor = healthPct > 85 ? 'var(--accent-green)' : healthPct > 60 ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'var(--accent-red)'
 183: 
 184:   return (
 185:     <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '16px' }}>
 186:       <div className="panel-title" style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
 187:         <span>🔍 AI Fault Detection</span>
 188:         <span style={{ color: healthColor, fontSize: 13 }}>
 189:           Health: {healthPct}%
 190:         </span>
 191:       </div>
 192: 
 193:       {alerts.length === 0 ? (
 194:         <div style={{ padding: '12px', background: 'rgba(0,255,136,0.05)', borderRadius: 8, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
 195:           <span style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>✅</span>
 196:           <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--accent-green)' }}>Grid Operating Normally. No anomalies detected.</span>
 197:         </div>
 198:       ) : (
 199:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>
 200:           {alerts.map((alert, idx) => (
 201:             <div key={idx} style={{
 202:               padding: '10px 12px',
 203:               background: alert.severity === 'CRITICAL' ? 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.1)' :
 204:                           alert.severity === 'HIGH' ? 'rgba(234, 179, 8, 0.1)' : 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1)',
 205:               borderRadius: 8,
 206:               borderLeft: `2px solid ${alert.severity === 'CRITICAL' ? 'var(--accent-red)' :
 207:                                       alert.severity === 'HIGH' ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'var(--accent-blue)'}`
 208:             }}>
 209:               <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 4 }}>
 210:                 <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--text-primary)' }}>
 211:                   {alert.node_id} - {alert.fault_type.replace('_', ' ').toUpperCase()}
 212:                 </span>
 213:                 <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-muted)' }}>Score: {alert.score.toFixed(2)}</span>
 214:               </div>
 215:               <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-secondary)' }}>{alert.message}</div>
 216:             </div>
 217:           ))}
 218:         </div>
 219:       )}
 220:     </div>
 221:   )
 222: }

 224: function DecisionCard({ decision }) {
 225:   if (!decision) return null
 226:   const badgeClass = ACTION_COLORS[decision.color] || 'badge-cyan'
 227: 
 228:   return (
 229:     <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '16px' }}>
 230:       <div className="panel-title">🤖 DQN Decision</div>
 231: 
 232:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'flex-start', gap: 10 }}>
 233:         <span className={`badge ${badgeClass}`} style={{ marginTop: 2, flexShrink: 0 }}>
 234:           ACT-{decision.action_id}
 235:         </span>
 236:         <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 500, color: 'var(--text-primary)', lineHeight: 1.4 }}>
 237:           {decision.label}
 238:         </span>
 239:       </div>
 240: 
 241:       <div style={{
 242:         marginTop: 12, padding: '10px 12px',
 243:         background: 'rgba(0,212,255,0.05)',
 244:         borderRadius: 8, borderLeft: '2px solid var(--accent-cyan)'
 245:       }}>
 246:         <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-muted)', marginBottom: 4 }}>Reasoning</div>
 247:         <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', lineHeight: 1.6 }}>
 248:           {decision.reasoning}
 249:         </div>
 250:       </div>
 251: 
 252:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 16, marginTop: 12 }}>
 253:         <div>
 254:           <div className="metric-label">Exploration ε</div>
 255:           <div className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-purple)', fontSize: 12 }}>
 256:             {(decision.epsilon || 0).toFixed(3)}
 257:           </div>
 258:         </div>
 259:         <div>
 260:           <div className="metric-label">Action</div>
 261:           <div className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-cyan)', fontSize: 12 }}>
 262:             {decision.action_name}
 263:           </div>
 264:         </div>
 265:         {decision.confidence !== undefined && (
 266:           <div>
 267:             <div className="metric-label">Confidence</div>
 268:             <div className="metric-value" style={{ color: decision.confidence > 0.8 ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-yellow)', fontSize: 12 }}>
 269:               {Math.round(decision.confidence * 100)}%
 270:             </div>
 271:           </div>
 272:         )}
 273:       </div>
 274:     </div>
 275:   )
 276: }

 278: function AIArchitectCard({ timestep }) {
 279:   const [suggestions, setSuggestions] = useState([])
 280:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
 281: 
 282:   const fetchSuggestions = async () => {
 283:     setLoading(true)
 284:     try {
 285:       const res = await getAISuggestions()
 286:       setSuggestions(res.suggestions || [])
 287:     } catch {
 288:     } finally {
 289:       setLoading(false)
 290:     }
 291:   }
 292: 
 293:   // Poll exactly every 50 timesteps to avoid spanning backend excessively, or on component mount
 294:   useEffect(() => {
 295:     if (!timestep || timestep % 50 === 0) fetchSuggestions()
 296:   }, [timestep])
 297: 
 298:   return (
 299:     <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '16px', marginBottom: '16px', border: '1px solid var(--border)' }}>
 300:       <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 12 }}>
 301:         <span className="panel-title" style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: 13 }}>💡 AI Architect</span>
 302:         <button className="btn btn-cyan" onClick={fetchSuggestions} disabled={loading} style={{ padding: '2px 6px', fontSize: 10 }}>Scan</button>
 303:       </div>
 304: 
 305:       {suggestions.length === 0 ? (
 306:         <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-muted)' }}>Grid topology is structurally stable. No critical single-points of failure detected.</div>
 307:       ) : (
 308:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>
 309:           {suggestions.map((s, i) => (
 310:             <div key={i} style={{ padding: '8px 10px', background: 'rgba(234,179,8,0.1)', borderRadius: 6, borderLeft: '2px solid var(--accent-yellow)' }}>
 311:               <div style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--accent-yellow)', marginBottom: 4 }}>SUGGEST TIE LINE</div>
 312:               <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-primary)', marginBottom: 2, fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono' }}>{s.source} ↔ {s.target}</div>
 313:               <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', lineHeight: 1.4 }}>{s.reason}</div>
 314:             </div>
 315:           ))}
 316:         </div>
 317:       )}
 318:     </div>
 319:   )
 320: }

 322: export default function AIDecisionPanel({ aiState, gridState }) {
 323:   const logRef = useRef(null)
 324: 
 325:   const system = gridState?.system || {}
 326:   const currentLoad = (system.total_load || 0) / Math.max(
 327:     Object.keys(gridState?.nodes || {}).length, 1
 328:   )
 329: 
 330:   // Auto-scroll log
 331:   useEffect(() => {
 332:     if (logRef.current) {
 333:       logRef.current.scrollTop = 0
 334:     }
 335:   }, [aiState?.log?.length])
 336: 
 337:   return (
 338:     <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 14, height: '100%', overflowY: 'auto', paddingRight: 4 }}>
 339: 
 340:       {/* System Pulse Metrics Array */}
 341:       <SystemMetricsCard gridState={gridState} faultAnalysis={aiState?.latest?.fault_analysis} />
 342: 
 343:       {/* AI Topological Suggestions */}
 344:       <AIArchitectCard timestep={gridState?.timestep} />
 345: 
 346:       {/* Header */}
 347:       <div>
 348:         <div className="panel-title">🔵 AI Decision Engine</div>
 349: 
 350:         {/* Status pill */}
 351:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, marginBottom: 14 }}>
 352:           <div className={`pulse`} style={{
 353:             width: 8, height: 8, borderRadius: '50%',
 354:             background: 'var(--accent-green)',
 355:           }} />
 356:           <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-secondary)' }}>
 357:             LSTM + DQN Active — Step {gridState?.timestep || 0}
 358:           </span>
 359:         </div>
 360:       </div>
 361: 
 362:       {/* Demand Gauge */}
 363:       <DemandGauge
 364:         predicted={aiState?.latest?.predicted_load || 0.5}
 365:         current={currentLoad}
 366:       />
 367: 
 368:       {/* AI Fault Detection Card */}
 369:       {aiState?.latest?.fault_analysis && (
 370:         <FaultAnalysisCard faultAnalysis={aiState.latest.fault_analysis} />
 371:       )}
 372: 
 373:       {/* Decision Card */}
 374:       <DecisionCard decision={aiState?.latest?.decision} />
 375: 
 376:       {/* FLISR / Action Result — Prominent Reasoning Card */}
 377:       {aiState?.latest?.action_result && (() => {
 378:         const result = aiState.latest.action_result
 379:         const isFlisr   = result.includes('FLISR')
 380:         const isSuccess = result.includes('✅')
 381:         const isWarning = result.includes('⚠️')
 382: 
 383:         // Parse tie info from FLISR result string
 384:         const tieMatch  = result.match(/via tie (\S+)/)
 385:         const vMatch    = result.match(/V≈([\d.]+)/)
 386:         const hmMatch   = result.match(/Headroom (\d+)%/)
 387:         const mwMatch   = result.match(/([\d.]+) MW/)
 388: 
 389:         const borderColor = isSuccess ? 'var(--accent-green)' : isWarning ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'
 390:         const bgColor     = isSuccess ? 'rgba(34,197,94,0.07)' : isWarning ? 'rgba(234,179,8,0.07)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)'
 391: 
 392:         return (
 393:           <div style={{
 394:             padding: '14px', borderRadius: 10,
 395:             background: bgColor,
 396:             border: `1px solid ${borderColor}`,
 397:           }}>
 398:             <div style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '0.5px', color: 'var(--text-muted)', marginBottom: 8 }}>
 399:               {isFlisr ? '⚡ SCADA FLISR DECISION' : '🤖 CONTROL ACTION'}
 400:             </div>
 401: 
 402:             {/* Main result text */}
 403:             <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: isSuccess ? 'var(--accent-green)' : isWarning ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'var(--text-secondary)', lineHeight: 1.6, marginBottom: isFlisr ? 10 : 0 }}>
 404:               {result}
 405:             </div>
 406: 
 407:             {/* FLISR metrics grid */}
 408:             {isFlisr && (tieMatch || vMatch || hmMatch) && (
 409:               <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr 1fr', gap: 8, marginTop: 8, paddingTop: 8, borderTop: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)' }}>
 410:                 {tieMatch && (
 411:                   <div>
 412:                     <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-muted)' }}>Tie Closed</div>
 413:                     <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--accent-cyan)', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono' }}>{tieMatch[1]}</div>
 414:                   </div>
 415:                 )}
 416:                 {vMatch && (
 417:                   <div>
 418:                     <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-muted)' }}>Voltage</div>
 419:                     <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: parseFloat(vMatch[1]) >= 0.95 ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-yellow)', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono' }}>
 420:                       {vMatch[1]} pu
 421:                     </div>
 422:                   </div>
 423:                 )}
 424:                 {hmMatch && (
 425:                   <div>
 426:                     <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-muted)' }}>Headroom</div>
 427:                     <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: parseInt(hmMatch[1]) > 30 ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-yellow)', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono' }}>
 428:                       {hmMatch[1]}%
 429:                     </div>
 430:                   </div>
 431:                 )}
 432:               </div>
 433:             )}
 434:           </div>
 435:         )
 436:       })()}
 437: 
 438: 
 439:       {/* FLISR Decision Log — step-by-step AI reasoning */}
 440:       {aiState?.latest?.flisr_log?.length > 0 && (
 441:         <FLISRDecisionLog flisrLog={aiState.latest.flisr_log} />
 442:       )}
 443: 
 444:       {/* Reward */}
 445:       {aiState?.latest?.reward !== undefined && (
 446:         <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '12px 16px' }}>
 447:           <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
 448:             <div>
 449:               <div className="metric-label">Last Reward</div>
 450:               <div className="metric-value" style={{
 451:                 color: aiState.latest.reward >= 0 ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-red)',
 452:                 fontSize: 16, marginTop: 4,
 453:               }}>
 454:                 {aiState.latest.reward >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{aiState.latest.reward.toFixed(2)}
 455:               </div>
 456:             </div>
 457:             <div style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>
 458:               <div className="metric-label">Energy Loss</div>
 459:               <div className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-yellow)', fontSize: 16, marginTop: 4 }}>
 460:                 {(system.total_energy_loss || 0).toFixed(2)} MWh
 461:               </div>
 462:             </div>
 463:           </div>
 464:         </div>
 465:       )}
 466: 
 467:       {/* Event Log — merged AI log + grid physical events */}
 468:       <div>
 469:         <div className="section-title">📋 Event Log</div>
 470:         {/* Grid physical events (FLISR breaker ops, relay trips) */}
 471:         {(gridState?.recent_events || []).length > 0 && (
 472:           <div style={{ marginBottom: 8 }}>
 473:             {(gridState.recent_events).map((evt, i) => {
 474:               const isIsolate = evt.includes('ISOLATE') || evt.includes('trip')
 475:               const isRestore = evt.includes('✅') || evt.includes('Restored')
 476:               const color = isIsolate ? 'var(--accent-red)' : isRestore ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-yellow)'
 477:               return (
 478:                 <div key={i} style={{
 479:                   padding: '6px 10px', marginBottom: 4,
 480:                   background: isIsolate ? 'rgba(239,68,68,0.06)' : isRestore ? 'rgba(34,197,94,0.06)' : 'rgba(234,179,8,0.06)',
 481:                   borderRadius: 6, borderLeft: `2px solid ${color}`,
 482:                   fontSize: 11, color,
 483:                 }}>
 484:                   {evt}
 485:                 </div>
 486:               )
 487:             })}
 488:           </div>
 489:         )}
 490:         <div className="log-scroll" ref={logRef}>
 491:           {(aiState?.log || []).slice().reverse().map((entry, i) => (
 492:             <div
 493:               key={i}
 494:               className="slide-in"
 495:               style={{
 496:                 padding: '8px 12px',
 497:                 background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)',
 498:                 borderRadius: 8,
 499:                 borderLeft: `2px solid ${entry.color || 'var(--accent-cyan)'}`,
 500:                 fontSize: 11,
 501:                 color: 'var(--text-secondary)',
 502:                 lineHeight: 1.5,
 503:               }}
 504:             >
 505:               <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 2 }}>
 506:                 <span className={`badge ${ACTION_COLORS[entry.color] || 'badge-cyan'}`} style={{ fontSize: 9 }}>
 507:                   T{entry.timestep}
 508:                 </span>
 509:                 <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-muted)', fontSize: 10 }}>{entry.time}</span>
 510:               </div>
 511:               <div>{entry.text}</div>
 512:             </div>
 513:           ))}
 514:           {(!aiState?.log || aiState.log.length === 0) && (
 515:             <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-muted)', fontSize: 12, textAlign: 'center', padding: 20 }}>
 516:               Awaiting simulation data...
 517:             </div>
 518:           )}
 519:         </div>
 520:       </div>
 521:     </div>
 522:   )
 523: }

FILE: frontend\src\components\ControlPanel.jsx
================================================================================
   1: /**
   2:  * ControlPanel.jsx — Left panel with simulation control buttons.
   3:  *
   4:  * Buttons:
   5:  *  - Increase Demand      → triggerEvent('demand')
   6:  *  - Trigger Storm        → triggerEvent('storm')
   7:  *  - Simulate Node Failure → triggerEvent('failure', selectedNode)
   8:  *  - Adjust Generation    → triggerEvent('generation')
   9:  *  - Reset Grid           → resetGrid()
  10:  *
  11:  * Also shows: selected node picker, live system stats, and storage levels.
  12:  */
  13: 
  14: import React, { useState } from 'react'
  15: import { triggerEvent, resetGrid, randomFaultAPI } from '../services/api'
  16: 
  17: export default function ControlPanel({ gridState, onUpdate, onMessage, selectedNode, setSelectedNode }) {
  18:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  19: 
  20:   const nodes = gridState?.nodes || {}
  21:   const system = gridState?.system || {}
  22: 
  23:   const call = async (fn, label) => {
  24:     if (loading) return
  25:     setLoading(true)
  26:     try {
  27:       const result = await fn()
  28:       onUpdate(result.grid || result)
  29:       if (result.message) onMessage(result.message)
  30:     } catch (e) {
  31:       onMessage('❌ Error: ' + (e?.response?.data?.detail || e.message))
  32:     } finally {
  33:       setLoading(false)
  34:     }
  35:   }
  36: 
  37:   // Bar helper
  38:   const Bar = ({ value, color }) => (
  39:     <div className="progress-bar" style={{ marginTop: 4 }}>
  40:       <div
  41:         className="progress-fill"
  42:         style={{ width: `${Math.round(value * 100)}%`, background: color }}
  43:       />
  44:     </div>
  45:   )
  46: 
  47:   const healthPct = Math.round((system.health_score || 0) * 100)
  48:   const healthColor =
  49:     healthPct > 70 ? 'var(--accent-green)' :
  50:     healthPct > 40 ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'var(--accent-red)'
  51: 
  52:   // Get selected node state for contextual actions
  53:   const selectedNodeData = nodes[selectedNode]
  54:   const isNodeFailed = selectedNodeData?.failed
  55:   const isNodeIsolated = selectedNodeData?.isolated
  56: 
  57:   return (
  58:     <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 16, height: '100%', overflowY: 'auto', paddingRight: 4 }}>
  59: 
  60:       {/* Header */}
  61:       <div>
  62:         <div className="panel-title">🎮 Simulation Controls</div>
  63: 
  64:         {/* Action Buttons */}
  65:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>
  66:           <button
  67:             className="btn btn-yellow"
  68:             disabled={loading}
  69:             onClick={() => call(() => randomFaultAPI(), 'Random Fault')}
  70:           >
  71:             ⚠️ Random Fault
  72:           </button>
  73: 
  74:           <button
  75:             className="btn btn-yellow"
  76:             disabled={loading}
  77:             onClick={() => call(() => triggerEvent('demand', null, 0.3), 'Demand')}
  78:           >
  79:             📈 Increase Demand
  80:           </button>
  81: 
  82:           <button
  83:             className="btn btn-red"
  84:             disabled={loading || gridState?.storm_active}
  85:             onClick={() => call(() => triggerEvent('storm'), 'Storm')}
  86:           >
  87:             🌩️ Trigger Storm
  88:           </button>
  89: 
  90:           {gridState?.storm_active && (
  91:             <button
  92:               className="btn btn-cyan"
  93:               disabled={loading}
  94:               onClick={() => call(() => triggerEvent('clear_storm'), 'Clear Storm')}
  95:             >
  96:               ☀️ Clear Storm
  97:             </button>
  98:           )}
  99: 
 100:           <button
 101:             className="btn btn-green"
 102:             disabled={loading}
 103:             onClick={() => call(() => triggerEvent('generation', null, 0.4), 'Generation')}
 104:           >
 105:             ⚡ Boost Generation
 106:           </button>
 107: 
 108:           <button
 109:             className="btn btn-purple"
 110:             disabled={loading}
 111:             onClick={() => call(() => resetGrid(), 'Reset')}
 112:           >
 113:             🔄 Reset Grid
 114:           </button>
 115:         </div>
 116:       </div>
 117: 
 118:       {/* Node Selector */}
 119:       <div>
 120:         <div className="section-title">Target Node</div>
 121:         <div className="node-selector">
 122:           {Object.keys(nodes)
 123:             .filter(n => n.startsWith('G') || n.startsWith('S'))
 124:             .sort()
 125:             .map(nid => {
 126:             const n = nodes[nid]
 127:             const isFailed = n?.failed || n?.isolated
 128:             return (
 129:               <button
 130:                 key={nid}
 131:                 className={`node-btn ${selectedNode === nid ? 'active' : ''} ${isFailed ? 'failed' : ''}`}
 132:                 onClick={() => setSelectedNode(nid)}
 133:               >
 134:                 {nid}
 135:               </button>
 136:             )
 137:           })}
 138:         </div>
 139:       </div>
 140: 
 141:       {/* Contextual Node Actions - Show only relevant inverse actions */}
 142:       {selectedNodeData && (
 143:         <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '12px 16px', background: 'rgba(100,180,255,0.08)', border: '1px solid rgba(100,180,255,0.2)' }}>
 144:           <div className="section-title">⚙️ Node Actions</div>
 145:           <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 6 }}>
 146:             {(() => {
 147:               function getNodeActionLabel(node) {
 148:                 return node.failed ? "Restore Node" : "Fail Node";
 149:               }
 150: 
 151:               function handleNodeAction(node) {
 152:                 if (node.failed) {
 153:                   fetch("http://localhost:8000/restore_node", {
 154:                     method: "POST",
 155:                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 156:                     body: JSON.stringify({ node_id: node.id }),
 157:                   });
 158:                 } else {
 159:                   fetch("http://localhost:8000/fail_node", {
 160:                     method: "POST",
 161:                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 162:                     body: JSON.stringify({ node_id: node.id }),
 163:                   });
 164:                 }
 165:               }
 166: 
 167:               return (
 168:                  <button
 169:                    className={`btn ${selectedNodeData.failed ? 'btn-cyan' : 'btn-red'}`}
 170:                    disabled={loading}
 171:                    onClick={() => handleNodeAction(selectedNodeData)}
 172:                  >
 173:                    {selectedNodeData.failed ? '🔧 ' : '⚠️ '}
 174:                    {getNodeActionLabel(selectedNodeData)}
 175:                  </button>
 176:               );
 177:             })()}
 178:           </div>
 179:         </div>
 180:       )}
 181: 
 182:       {/* System Stats */}
 183:       <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
 184:         <div className="panel-title">📊 System Stats</div>
 185: 
 186:         <div className="metric-row">
 187:           <span className="metric-label">Total Generation</span>
 188:           <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-green)' }}>
 189:             {(system.total_generation || 0).toFixed(2)} MW
 190:           </span>
 191:         </div>
 192:         <div className="metric-row">
 193:           <span className="metric-label">Total Load</span>
 194:           <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-yellow)' }}>
 195:             {(system.total_load || 0).toFixed(2)} MW
 196:           </span>
 197:         </div>
 198:         <div className="metric-row">
 199:           <span className="metric-label">Balance</span>
 200:           <span
 201:             className="metric-value"
 202:             style={{ color: (system.balance || 0) >= 0 ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'var(--accent-red)' }}
 203:           >
 204:             {(system.balance || 0) >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{(system.balance || 0).toFixed(2)} MW
 205:           </span>
 206:         </div>
 207:         <div className="metric-row">
 208:           <span className="metric-label">Avg Voltage</span>
 209:           <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-cyan)' }}>
 210:             {(system.avg_voltage || 0).toFixed(3)} p.u.
 211:           </span>
 212:         </div>
 213:         <div className="metric-row">
 214:           <span className="metric-label">Avg Frequency</span>
 215:           <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-cyan)' }}>
 216:             {(system.avg_frequency || 0).toFixed(2)} Hz
 217:           </span>
 218:         </div>
 219:         {/* ✅ FIX: separate failed poles vs no-power houses */}
 220:         {(() => {
 221:           const nodesArr = Object.entries(nodes)
 222:           const failedPoles = nodesArr.filter(([, n]) => (n.node_type === 'pole') && n.failed).length
 223:           const noPowerHouses = nodesArr.filter(([, n]) => (n.node_type === 'house') && n.isolated).length
 224:           return (
 225:             <>
 226:               <div className="metric-row">
 227:                 <span className="metric-label">🚨 Failed Poles</span>
 228:                 <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: failedPoles > 0 ? 'var(--accent-red)' : 'var(--accent-green)' }}>
 229:                   {failedPoles}
 230:                 </span>
 231:               </div>
 232:               <div className="metric-row">
 233:                 <span className="metric-label">🏠 No-Power Houses</span>
 234:                 <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: noPowerHouses > 0 ? 'var(--accent-yellow)' : 'var(--accent-green)' }}>
 235:                   {noPowerHouses}
 236:                 </span>
 237:               </div>
 238:             </>
 239:           )
 240:         })()}
 241: 
 242:         <div style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
 243:           <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 4 }}>
 244:             <span className="metric-label">Grid Health</span>
 245:             <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: healthColor }}>{healthPct}%</span>
 246:           </div>
 247:           <Bar value={system.health_score || 0} color={healthColor} />
 248:         </div>
 249:       </div>
 250: 
 251:       {/* Selected Node Detail */}
 252:       {nodes[selectedNode] && (
 253:         <div className="glass-card" style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
 254:           <div className="panel-title">🔍 Node: {selectedNode}</div>
 255:           {(() => {
 256:             const n = nodes[selectedNode]
 257:             return (
 258:               <>
 259:                 <div className="metric-row">
 260:                   <span className="metric-label">Status</span>
 261:                   <span className={`badge badge-${n.failed ? 'red' : n.isolated ? 'yellow' : 'green'}`}>
 262:                     {n.failed ? 'FAILED' : n.isolated ? 'ISOLATED' : 'ONLINE'}
 263:                   </span>
 264:                 </div>
 265:                 <div className="metric-row">
 266:                   <span className="metric-label">Voltage</span>
 267:                   <span className="metric-value">{n.voltage.toFixed(3)} p.u.</span>
 268:                 </div>
 269:                 <div className="metric-row">
 270:                   <span className="metric-label">Load / Gen</span>
 271:                   <span className="metric-value">{n.load.toFixed(2)} / {n.generation.toFixed(2)} MW</span>
 272:                 </div>
 273:                 <div style={{ marginTop: 10 }}>
 274:                   <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 4 }}>
 275:                     <span className="metric-label">🔋 Battery</span>
 276:                     <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-blue)' }}>
 277:                       {Math.round(n.battery_level * 100)}%
 278:                     </span>
 279:                   </div>
 280:                   <Bar value={n.battery_level} color="var(--accent-blue)" />
 281:                 </div>
 282:                 <div style={{ marginTop: 8 }}>
 283:                   <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 4 }}>
 284:                     <span className="metric-label">⚡ Supercap</span>
 285:                     <span className="metric-value" style={{ color: 'var(--accent-cyan)' }}>
 286:                       {Math.round(n.supercap_level * 100)}%
 287:                     </span>
 288:                   </div>
 289:                   <Bar value={n.supercap_level} color="var(--accent-cyan)" />
 290:                 </div>
 291:               </>
 292:             )
 293:           })()}
 294:         </div>
 295:       )}
 296:     </div>
 297:   )
 298: }

   6: const getShape = (type) => {
   7:   // Generation Layer
   8:   if (type === 'generator')               return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolTriangle).size(800)()
   9:   if (type === 'generator_solar')         return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolStar).size(1000)()
  10:   if (type === 'generator_wind')           return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolTriangle).size(900)()
  11:   if (type === 'generator_nuclear')        return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolWye).size(1000)()
  12:   if (type === 'generator_coal')           return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolTriangle).size(800)()
  13:   if (type === 'generator_gas')            return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolTriangle).size(800)()
  14:   // Legacy types
  15:   if (type === 'solar')                    return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolStar).size(800)()
  16:   if (type === 'wind')                     return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolTriangle).size(600)()
  17:   // Storage

  19:   if (type === 'supercap')                return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolDiamond).size(700)()

  29:   if (type === 'commercial')              return d3.symbol().type(d3.symbolCircle).size(400)()

  67: function getNodeColor(node) {
  68:   // ── Physics-first coloring: state > voltage > type ──────────────────
  69:   // 🔴 Hard fault — root-cause node that failed
  70:   if (node.failed) return '#ff3333'
  71:   // 🟠 Isolated — downstream of fault, awaiting FLISR restoration
  72:   if (node.isolated) return '#ff6600'
  73:   // SCADA node is purely decorative
  74:   if (node.is_scada) return 'none'
  75:   // 🟡 Under-voltage warning (< 0.95 pu) — physics-driven stress indicator
  76:   const v = node.voltage ?? 1.0
  77:   if (v > 0 && v < 0.90) return '#ff4444'   // critical low voltage
  78:   if (v > 0 && v < 0.95) return '#ffcc00'   // under-voltage warning
  79:   // 🟢 Energized — type-based color (hierarchy)
  80:   switch (node.node_type) {
  81:     case 'generator':         return '#ffb84d'
  82:     case 'generator_solar':   return '#ffee00'
  83:     case 'generator_wind':    return '#87ceeb'
  84:     case 'generator_nuclear': return '#3b82f6'
  85:     case 'generator_coal':    return '#888888'
  86:     case 'generator_gas':     return '#ff6633'
  87:     case 'solar':             return '#ffee00'
  88:     case 'wind':              return '#87ceeb'
  89:     case 'battery':           return '#dd55ff'
  90:     case 'supercap':          return '#ff3399'
  91:     case 'step_up':           return '#ff6633'
  92:     case 'substation':        return '#7777ff'
  93:     case 'transformer':       return '#3399ff'
  94:     case 'pole':              return '#00dddd'
  95:     case 'switch':            return '#cc77ff'
  96:     case 'service':           return '#00dddd'
  97:     case 'house':             return '#33ff33'
  98:     case 'hospital':          return '#ff4488'
  99:     case 'industry':          return '#bb44ff'
 100:     case 'commercial':        return '#00ccff'
 101:     default:                  return '#cccccc'
 102:   }
 103: }
 104: 
 105: 
 106: // ── Physics-driven edge color ───────────────────────────────────────
 107: // Derived ONLY from grid state — NOT from RL action names or AI colors.
 108: function getEdgeColor(edge) {
 109:   // 🔴 Fault-locked breaker (protection relay tripped)
 110:   if (edge.switch_status === 'fault_locked') return '#ff3333'
 111:   // 🔴 Broken cable
 112:   if (edge.status === 'broken') return '#ff5555'
 113:   // 🟡 FLISR rerouted (new active path after tie-switch closed)
 114:   if (edge.status === 'rerouted') return '#ffaa00'
 115:   // ⚫ Inactive (open switch / disabled)
 116:   if (!edge.active) return 'rgba(180,180,180,0.25)'
 117:   // ─── Active edge: color by ENERGY SOURCE TYPE (set by physics engine) ───
 118:   const flow = Math.abs(edge.flow || 0)
 119:   if (flow > 0.01) {
 120:     const src = edge.source_type || edge.source?.source_type || 'grid'
 121:     if (src === 'solar')                    return '#FFD700'  // Yellow  — solar
 122:     if (src === 'wind')                     return '#00BFFF'  // Cyan    — wind
 123:     if (src === 'battery' || src === 'supercap') return '#cc44ff'  // Purple  — storage
 124:     if (src === 'nuclear')                  return '#3b82f6'  // Blue    — nuclear
 125:     if (src === 'coal')                     return '#888888'  // Gray    — coal
 126:     if (src === 'gas')                      return '#ff6633'  // Orange  — gas
 127:     return '#00FFCC'   // Teal — generic grid power
 128:   }
 129:   // Tie switch type colouring when closed (FLISR activated)
 130:   if (edge.is_tie_switch && edge.active) return '#00FFCC'
 131:   return 'rgba(180,180,180,0.3)'  // Idle / no flow
 132: }

 134: // Must match backend grid.py canvas dimensions
 135: const MODEL_W = 1500
 136: const MODEL_H = 920

 138: export default function GridGraph({
 139:   gridState,
 140:   aiState,
 141:   width = 1100, height = 700,
 142:   selectedNode, onSelectNode,
 143:   selectedEdge, onSelectEdge,
 144:   onCutEdge,
 145:   onFailNode,
 146:   onAddHouse,
 147:   currentMode,
 148:   addNodeType,
 149:   interactionState,
 150:   setInteractionState,
 151:   showFlow,
 152:   aiAssistMode,
 153:   onMessage,
 154:   onUpdate,
 155: }) {
 156:   const svgRef  = useRef(null)
 157:   const dataRef = useRef({ nodes: [], links: [] })
 158:   const zoomRef = useRef(null)
 159:   const [suggestions, setSuggestions] = useState([])
 160:   const [flowStatus, setFlowStatus] = useState('flowing') // flowing, stopped, rerouting, no-flow
 161:   const canvasRef = useRef(null)
 162: 
 163:   // ── Canvas Animation Loop for flow ───────────────────────────────────
 164:   useEffect(() => {
 165:     const canvas = canvasRef.current
 166:     if (!canvas) return
 167:     const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d')
 168:     let animationFrameId
 169:     let time = 0
 170: 
 171:     const resize = () => {
 172:       canvas.width = canvas.parentElement.clientWidth * window.devicePixelRatio
 173:       canvas.height = canvas.parentElement.clientHeight * window.devicePixelRatio
 174:       ctx.scale(window.devicePixelRatio, window.devicePixelRatio)
 175:     }
 176:     resize()
 177:     window.addEventListener('resize', resize)
 178: 
 179:     const drawEnergyFlow = (ctx, edge, time, transform) => {
 180:       const flowVal = Math.abs(edge.flow || 0)
 181:       if (flowVal <= 0.001 || !edge.active) return
 182: 
 183:       const speed = 0.002 * flowVal
 184:       const progress = (time * speed) % 1
 185: 
 186:       // Determine flow direction
 187:       let fromNode = edge.source
 188:       let toNode = edge.target
 189: 
 190:       // If flow < 0, flow is flowing from target to source
 191:       if (edge.flow < 0) {
 192:           fromNode = edge.target
 193:           toNode = edge.source
 194:       }
 195: 
 196:       const x1 = transform.applyX(fromNode.x)
 197:       const y1 = transform.applyY(fromNode.y)
 198:       const x2 = transform.applyX(toNode.x)
 199:       const y2 = transform.applyY(toNode.y)
 200: 
 201:       const dx = x2 - x1
 202:       const dy = y2 - y1
 203: 
 204:       const px = x1 + dx * progress
 205:       const py = y1 + dy * progress
 206: 
 207:       ctx.beginPath()
 208:       ctx.moveTo(x1, y1)
 209:       ctx.lineTo(px, py)
 210: 
 211:       const sourceType = edge.source_type || fromNode.node_type || "grid"
 212:       ctx.strokeStyle =
 213:         sourceType.includes("solar") ? "#FFD700" :
 214:         sourceType.includes("wind") ? "#00BFFF" :
 215:         sourceType.includes("battery") || sourceType.includes("supercap") ? "#FF00FF" :
 216:         "#00FFCC"
 217: 
 218:       ctx.lineWidth = 3
 219:       ctx.globalAlpha = 0.8
 220:       ctx.stroke()
 221:     }
 222: 
 223:     const animate = () => {
 224:       time += 16
 225:       const { width, height } = canvas
 226:       ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height)
 227: 
 228:       const links = dataRef.current.links || []
 229:       const svgNode = svgRef.current
 230:       if (!svgNode) {
 231:           animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate)
 232:           return
 233:       }
 234:       const transform = d3.zoomTransform(svgNode)
 235: 
 236:       links.forEach(edge => {
 237:         if (Math.abs(edge.flow || 0) > 0.001) {
 238:           drawEnergyFlow(ctx, edge, time, transform)
 239:         }
 240:       })
 241: 
 242:       animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate)
 243:     }
 244:     animate()
 245: 
 246:     return () => {
 247:       window.removeEventListener('resize', resize)
 248:       cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameId)
 249:     }
 250:   }, [])
 251: 
 252:   // ── Keyboard: Delete / Backspace removes selected edge ──────────
 253:   useEffect(() => {
 254:     const onKey = (e) => {
 255:       if ((e.key === 'Delete' || e.key === 'Backspace') && selectedEdge && onCutEdge)
 256:         onCutEdge(selectedEdge.u, selectedEdge.v)
 257:     }
 258:     window.addEventListener('keydown', onKey)
 259:     return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', onKey)
 260:   }, [selectedEdge, onCutEdge])
 261: 
 262:   // ── AI Assist Mode Fetch ──────────────────────────────────────────
 263:   useEffect(() => {
 264:     if (!aiAssistMode) {
 265:       setSuggestions([])
 266:       return
 267:     }
 268:     const fetchSugg = async () => {
 269:       try {
 270:         const res = await getAISuggestions()
 271:         setSuggestions(res.suggestions || [])
 272:       } catch (e) {}
 273:     }
 274:     fetchSugg()
 275:     const int = setInterval(fetchSugg, 10000)
 276:     return () => clearInterval(int)
 277:   }, [aiAssistMode])
 278: 
 279:   // ── Flow Status Detection ───────────────────────────────────────────
 280:   useEffect(() => {
 281:     if (!gridState) return
 282:     const nodes = Object.values(gridState.nodes || {})
 283:     const failedNodes = nodes.filter(n => n.failed || n.isolated)
 284:     const activePaths = gridState.active_paths || []
 285:     const hasFault = failedNodes.length > 0 || gridState.storm_active
 286:     const hasActiveFlow = activePaths.length > 0
 287: 
 288:     if (hasFault) {
 289:       setFlowStatus(hasActiveFlow ? 'rerouting' : 'stopped')
 290:     } else {
 291:       setFlowStatus(hasActiveFlow ? 'flowing' : 'no-flow')
 292:     }
 293:   }, [gridState])
 294: 
 295:   // ── Convert backend state → d3 data arrays ───────────────────────
 296:   const buildData = useCallback((state) => {
 297:     if (!state) return
 298:     const nodeMap = state.nodes || {}
 299:     const edgeArr = state.edges || []
 300:     dataRef.current.nodes = Object.keys(nodeMap).map(id => ({ id, ...nodeMap[id] }))
 301: 
 302:     // Inject fixed SCADA Control Layer Node
 303:     dataRef.current.nodes.push({
 304:       id: 'SCADA', node_type: 'scada',
 305:       x: MODEL_W / 2, y: -40,
 306:       generation: 0, load: 0,
 307:       is_scada: true
 308:     })
 309: 
 310:     const nMap = Object.fromEntries(dataRef.current.nodes.map(n => [n.id, n]))
 311:     dataRef.current.links = edgeArr
 312:       .map(e => ({ ...e, source: nMap[e.source], target: nMap[e.target] }))
 313:       .filter(e => e.source && e.target)
 314: 
 315:     // — Store fault segment for overlay rendering
 316:     dataRef.current.faultSegment = state.last_fault_segment || {}
 317:   }, [])
 318: 
 319:   // ── One-time SVG init: zoom, markers, grid lines ──────────────────
 320:   useEffect(() => {
 321:     const svg = d3.select(svgRef.current)
 322:     svg.selectAll('*').remove()
 323: 
 324:     // D3 zoom
 325:     const zoom = d3.zoom()
 326:       .scaleExtent([0.15, 5])
 327:       .on('zoom', (event) => svg.select('g.zoom-root').attr('transform', event.transform))
 328:     zoomRef.current = zoom
 329:     svg.call(zoom)
 330: 
 331:     // Fit model into visible viewport on first load
 332:     const s  = Math.min(width / MODEL_W, height / MODEL_H) * 0.90
 333:     const tx = (width  - MODEL_W * s) / 2
 334:     const ty = (height - MODEL_H * s) / 2
 335:     svg.call(zoom.transform, d3.zoomIdentity.translate(tx, ty).scale(s))
 336: 
 337:     // Root zoom group — everything inside scales together
 338:     const root = svg.append('g').attr('class', 'zoom-root')
 339: 
 340:     // Arrow markers (declared outside root, but reference by ID)
 341:     const defs = svg.append('defs')
 342:     defs.append('marker').attr('id', 'arrow-blue')
 343:       .attr('viewBox', '0 -4 10 8').attr('refX', 18).attr('refY', 0)
 344:       .attr('markerWidth', 5).attr('markerHeight', 5).attr('orient', 'auto')
 345:       .append('path').attr('d', 'M0,-4L10,0L0,4').attr('fill', '#3b82f6')
 346:     defs.append('marker').attr('id', 'arrow-purple')
 347:       .attr('viewBox', '0 -4 10 8').attr('refX', 18).attr('refY', 0)
 348:       .attr('markerWidth', 5).attr('markerHeight', 5).attr('orient', 'auto-start-reverse')
 349:       .append('path').attr('d', 'M0,-4L10,0L0,4').attr('fill', '#8b5cf6')
 350: 
 351:     // Engineering faint grid (in model space)
 352:     const grid = root.append('g').style('pointer-events', 'none')
 353:     for (let x = 0; x <= MODEL_W; x += 50)
 354:       grid.append('line').attr('x1', x).attr('y1', 0).attr('x2', x).attr('y2', MODEL_H)
 355:         .attr('stroke', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)')
 356:     for (let y = 0; y <= MODEL_H; y += 50)
 357:       grid.append('line').attr('x1', 0).attr('y1', y).attr('x2', MODEL_W).attr('y2', y)
 358:         .attr('stroke', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)')
 359: 
 360:     // Zoom hint
 361:     root.append('text')
 362:       .attr('x', MODEL_W - 10).attr('y', MODEL_H - 8)
 363:       .attr('text-anchor', 'end')
 364:       .style('font-size', '9px').style('fill', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)')
 365:       .style('font-family', 'JetBrains Mono').style('pointer-events', 'none')
 366:       .text('Scroll to zoom  •  Drag to pan')
 367: 
 368:     // Preview wire (CONNECT mode)
 369:     root.append('line').attr('class', 'preview-link')
 370:       .attr('stroke', '#eab308').attr('stroke-width', 2)
 371:       .attr('stroke-dasharray', '5 5')
 372:       .style('opacity', 0).style('pointer-events', 'none')
 373: 
 374:     root.append('g').attr('class', 'links')
 375:     root.append('g').attr('class', 'scada-layer')  // Above links, below nodes
 376:     root.append('g').attr('class', 'nodes')
 377: 
 378:     // Background click → ADD_NODE (coords inverted through zoom transform)
 379:     svg.on('click.canvas', async (event) => {
 380:       if (currentMode !== MODES.ADD_NODE) return
 381:       const t = d3.zoomTransform(svgRef.current)
 382:       const [mx, my] = d3.pointer(event)
 383:       const [x, y]   = t.invert([mx, my])
 384:       try {
 385:         const res = await addNode(addNodeType, [x, y])
 386:         onUpdate?.(res.grid)
 387:         onMessage?.(res.message)
 388:       } catch (e) {
 389:         onMessage?.('Failed to add node: ' + e.message)
 390:       }
 391:     })
 392: 
 393:     // Mousemove preview wire
 394:     svg.on('mousemove.preview', (event) => {
 395:       if (currentMode === MODES.CONNECT && interactionState.activeSrcNode) {
 396:         const t = d3.zoomTransform(svgRef.current)
 397:         const [mx, my] = d3.pointer(event)
 398:         const [wx, wy] = t.invert([mx, my])
 399:         const src = interactionState.activeSrcNode
 400:         root.select('.preview-link')
 401:           .attr('x1', src.x).attr('y1', src.y)
 402:           .attr('x2', wx).attr('y2', wy)
 403:           .style('opacity', 1)
 404:       } else {
 405:         root.select('.preview-link').style('opacity', 0)
 406:       }
 407:     })
 408: 
 409:     // Tooltip element
 410:     const tip = d3.select('body').append('div')
 411:       .attr('id', 'grid-tooltip')
 412:       .style('position', 'fixed').style('background', 'rgba(15,23,42,0.95)')
 413:       .style('border', '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)').style('border-radius', '6px')
 414:       .style('padding', '8px 12px').style('font-size', '11px').style('color', '#e8f4ff')
 415:       .style('pointer-events', 'none').style('opacity', 0).style('z-index', 9999)
 416: 
 417:     return () => {
 418:       tip.remove()
 419:       svg.on('mousemove.preview', null)
 420:       svg.on('click.canvas', null)
 421:     }
 422:   }, [width, height, currentMode, interactionState, addNodeType])  // eslint-disable-line
 423: 
 424:   // ── Render on every grid state / mode change ──────────────────
 425:   useEffect(() => {
 426:     if (!gridState) return
 427:     buildData(gridState)
 428:     const { nodes, links, faultSegment } = dataRef.current
 429:     if (!nodes.length) return
 430: 
 431:     const svg  = d3.select(svgRef.current)
 432:     const root = svg.select('g.zoom-root')
 433:     const tip  = d3.select('#grid-tooltip')
 434: 
 435:     // Focus+Context: which nodes are connected to selected?
 436:     const connected = new Set()
 437:     if (selectedNode) {
 438:       connected.add(selectedNode)
 439:       links.forEach(l => {
 440:         if (l.source.id === selectedNode) connected.add(l.target.id)
 441:         if (l.target.id === selectedNode) connected.add(l.source.id)
 442:       })
 443:     }
 444: 
 445:     // ── LINKS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 446:     const edgeKey = d => `${d.source.id}|${d.target.id}`
 447: 
 448:     // ── Power Flow paths (⚡ blue, continuous line) ────────────────
 449:     const linkSel = root.select('.links')
 450:       .selectAll('path.wire')
 451:       .data(links, edgeKey)
 452: 
 453:     const linkEnter = linkSel.enter().append('path')
 454:       .attr('class', 'wire')
 455:       .attr('fill', 'none')
 456:       .attr('stroke-linecap', 'round')
 457:       .style('cursor', 'pointer')
 458:       .on('click', (event, d) => {
 459:         event.stopPropagation()
 460:         if (currentMode === MODES.CUT_EDGE)  onCutEdge?.(d.source.id, d.target.id)
 461:         if (currentMode === MODES.SELECT)    onSelectEdge?.({ u: d.source.id, v: d.target.id })
 462:       })
 463: 
 464:     const pathD = d => `M${d.source.x},${d.source.y} L${d.target.x},${d.target.y}`
 465: 
 466:     linkEnter.merge(linkSel)
 467:       .attr('d', pathD)
 468:       .style('opacity', d => {
 469:         if (!selectedNode) return d.active ? 1 : 0.25
 470:         const conn = d.source.id === selectedNode || d.target.id === selectedNode
 471:         return conn ? (d.active ? 1 : 0.4) : 0.12
 472:       })
 473:       .attr('stroke', d => {
 474:         // Cut edge mode — highlight red to confirm action
 475:         if (currentMode === MODES.CUT_EDGE) return '#ff3333'
 476:         // All other coloring is physics-driven via getEdgeColor()
 477:         return getEdgeColor(d)
 478:       })
 479:       .attr('stroke-width', d => {
 480:         if (!d.active) return 1
 481:         // Base width by hierarchy level
 482:         let baseWidth = 1.5
 483:         if (d.source.node_type === 'generator' || d.source.node_type === 'substation' || d.target.node_type === 'substation') baseWidth = 5.0
 484:         else if (d.source.node_type === 'transformer' || d.target.node_type === 'transformer') baseWidth = 4.0
 485:         else if (d.source.node_type === 'pole' && d.target.node_type === 'pole') baseWidth = 3.0
 486:         else if (d.source.node_type === 'house' || d.target.node_type === 'house') baseWidth = 1.2
 487:         else baseWidth = 2.5
 488:         // █ Physics: thicker = more MW flowing through this cable
 489:         const flowBoost = Math.abs(d.flow || 0) * 1.5
 490:         return Math.min(Math.max(baseWidth, 1.5 + flowBoost), 10)
 491:       })
 492:       .style('stroke-dasharray', d => {
 493:         if (d.status === 'broken') return '10 5'
 494:         if (d.is_tie_switch) return '6 4'
 495:         return 'none'
 496:       })
 497:       .style('filter', d => {
 498:         if (d.status === 'rerouted') return 'drop-shadow(0 0 6px #f59e0b)'
 499:         if (d.status === 'broken') return 'drop-shadow(0 0 3px #7f1d1d)'
 500:         return 'none'
 501:       })
 502:       .attr('class', d => {
 503:         if (d.switch_status === 'fault_locked') return 'wire fault-segment'
 504:         if (d.status === 'rerouted')            return 'wire reroute-active'
 505:         if (d.status === 'broken')              return 'wire reroute-broken'
 506:         if (d.is_tie_switch && d.active)        return 'wire tie-switch-closed'
 507:         if (d.is_tie_switch && !d.active)       return 'wire tie-switch-open'
 508:         if (!d.active && (d.source.failed || d.target.failed)) return 'wire fault-segment'
 509:         return 'wire'
 510:       })
 511:       .attr('marker-end', null)
 512: 
 513:     linkSel.exit().remove()
 514: 
 515:     // ── Fault Segment Overlay (amber bounding box) ─────────────────────
 516:     // Drawn when last_fault_segment is populated (after isolation, before repair)
 517:     const overlayGroup = root.select('.links')  // insert below nodes
 518:     overlayGroup.selectAll('rect.fault-segment-overlay').remove()
 519:     if (faultSegment && faultSegment.affected_nodes && faultSegment.affected_nodes.length > 0) {
 520:       const affectedNodes = faultSegment.affected_nodes
 521:         .map(nid => nodes.find(n => n.id === nid))
 522:         .filter(Boolean)
 523:       if (affectedNodes.length > 0) {
 524:         const pad = 18
 525:         const xs  = affectedNodes.map(n => n.x)
 526:         const ys  = affectedNodes.map(n => n.y)
 527:         const x1  = Math.min(...xs) - pad
 528:         const y1  = Math.min(...ys) - pad
 529:         const x2  = Math.max(...xs) + pad
 530:         const y2  = Math.max(...ys) + pad
 531:         overlayGroup.insert('rect', ':first-child')
 532:           .attr('class', 'fault-segment-overlay')
 533:           .attr('x', x1).attr('y', y1)
 534:           .attr('width',  x2 - x1)
 535:           .attr('height', y2 - y1)
 536:           .attr('rx', 6).attr('ry', 6)
 537:           .attr('fill',   'rgba(255,51,51,0.12)')
 538:           .attr('stroke', '#ff3333')
 539:           .attr('stroke-width', 1.5)
 540:           .attr('stroke-dasharray', '6 3')
 541:           .style('pointer-events', 'none')
 542:       }
 543:     }
 544: 
 545:     // ── SCADA / AI Suggestion overlays REMOVED ────────────────────────
 546:     // These were driven by RL action colors (not physics) and misled viewers.
 547:     // All visual state now comes exclusively from the grid physics engine:
 548:     //   node color  → node.failed / node.isolated / node.voltage
 549:     //   edge color  → edge.active / edge.flow / edge.source_type
 550:     //   edge width  → abs(edge.flow)
 551:     // Clear the scada-layer so stale overlays from previous renders vanish.
 552:     root.select('.scada-layer').selectAll('*').remove()
 553: 
 554:     const nodeSel = root.select('.nodes')
 555:       .selectAll('g.node')
 556:       .data(nodes, d => d.id)
 557: 
 558:     let dragStart = [0, 0];
 559:     const dragHandler = d3.drag()
 560:       .on('start', (event, d) => {
 561:         dragStart = [event.x, event.y];
 562:         if (currentMode !== MODES.SELECT) return
 563:         event.sourceEvent.stopPropagation()
 564:       })
 565:       .on('drag', function(event, d) {
 566:         if (currentMode !== MODES.SELECT) return
 567:         d.x = event.x
 568:         d.y = event.y
 569:         d3.select(this).attr('transform', `translate(${d.x},${d.y})`)
 570:         root.selectAll('path.wire').filter(l => l.source.id === d.id || l.target.id === d.id)
 571:           .attr('d', l => `M${l.source.x},${l.source.y} L${l.target.x},${l.target.y}`)
 572:       })
 573:       .on('end', async (event, d) => {
 574:         const dx = Math.abs(event.x - dragStart[0]);
 575:         const dy = Math.abs(event.y - dragStart[1]);
 576: 
 577:         if (dx < 5 && dy < 5) {
 578:           handleNodeClick(event, d);
 579:           return;
 580:         }
 581: 
 582:         if (currentMode !== MODES.SELECT) return
 583:         try {
 584:           const res = await moveNodeAPI(d.id, d.x, d.y)
 585:           onUpdate?.(res.grid)
 586:         } catch (e) {
 587:           onMessage?.('Failed to move: ' + e.message)
 588:         }
 589:       })
 590: 
 591:     const handleNodeClick = async (event, d) => {
 592:       event.stopPropagation?.();
 593:       if (currentMode === MODES.SELECT) {
 594:         onSelectNode?.(d.id)
 595:       } else if (currentMode === MODES.FAIL_NODE) {
 596:         try {
 597:           const res = await failNodeAPI(d.id)
 598:           onUpdate?.(res.grid)
 599:           onMessage?.(res.message)
 600:         } catch (e) {}
 601:       } else if (currentMode === MODES.DELETE_NODE) {
 602:         try {
 603:           const res = await deleteNodeAPI(d.id)
 604:           onUpdate?.(res.grid)
 605:           onMessage?.(res.message)
 606:         } catch (e) {
 607:           onMessage?.('Delete failed: ' + e.message)
 608:         }
 609:       } else if (currentMode === MODES.ADD_HOUSE) {
 610:         onAddHouse?.(d.id)
 611:       } else if (currentMode === MODES.CONNECT) {
 612:         if (!interactionState.activeSrcNode) {
 613:           setInteractionState({ activeSrcNode: d })
 614:         } else {
 615:           try {
 616:             const res = await addEdge(interactionState.activeSrcNode.id, d.id)
 617:             onUpdate?.(res.grid)
 618:             onMessage?.(res.message)
 619:           } catch (e) {
 620:             onMessage?.('Connection failed: ' + e.message)
 621:           } finally {
 622:             setInteractionState({})
 623:             root.select('.preview-link').style('opacity', 0)
 624:           }
 625:         }
 626:       }
 627:     }
 628: 
 629:     const nodeEnter = nodeSel.enter().append('g')
 630:       .attr('class', 'node')
 631:       .style('cursor', 'pointer')
 632:       .call(dragHandler)
 633:       .on('mouseover', (event, d) => {
 634:         if (currentMode === MODES.CUT_EDGE) return
 635:         const n = gridState.nodes[d.id] || d
 636: 
 637:         let faultOverlay = ''
 638:         if (n.failed && aiState?.fault_analysis) {
 639:           // Backend returns 'node_scores' (not 'anomaly_scores')
 640:           const score    = aiState.fault_analysis.node_scores?.[d.id] ?? 1.0
 641:           const alertObj = aiState.fault_analysis.alerts?.find(a => a.node_id === d.id)
 642:           const faultType = alertObj?.fault_type?.replace('_', ' ').toUpperCase() ?? 'HARD FAILURE'
 643:           const severity  = alertObj?.severity ?? 'CRITICAL'
 644:           const sevColor  = severity === 'CRITICAL' ? '#ef4444' : '#eab308'
 645:           faultOverlay = `
 646:             <div style="margin:8px 0;padding:8px;background:rgba(239,68,68,0.12);border:1px solid #ef4444;border-radius:6px;">
 647:               <div style="color:#ef4444;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:6px;letter-spacing:0.5px;">🚨 AI FAULT DIAGNOSIS</div>
 648:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:3px;"><span>Fault Type:</span><b style="color:${sevColor}">${faultType}</b></div>
 649:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:3px;"><span>ANN Confidence:</span><b style="color:#ef4444">${(score * 100).toFixed(1)}%</b></div>
 650:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;"><span>V-State:</span><b>${n.voltage ? n.voltage.toFixed(3) : '0.000'} pu</b></div>
 651:             </div>
 652:           `
 653:         }
 654: 
 655:         if (d.is_scada) {
 656:             tip.style('opacity', 1).html(`
 657:               <div style="font-weight:600;color:#22c55e;font-size:14px;text-align:center;">🧠 SCADA Control Center</div>
 658:               <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:10px;text-align:center;">AI-Driven Autonomous Agent Stack</div>
 659:             `)
 660:         } else {
 661:             const switchInfo = n.switch_type
 662:               ? `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-top:4px;"><span>Switch:</span><b style="color:${
 663:                   n.switch_status === 'fault_locked' ? '#ef4444' :
 664:                   n.switch_status === 'open'         ? '#94a3b8' : '#22c55e'}">${
 665:                   n.switch_type?.toUpperCase()} — ${n.switch_status?.replace('_',' ').toUpperCase()}</b></div>`
 666:               : ''
 667:             tip.style('opacity', 1).html(`
 668:               <div style="font-weight:600;margin-bottom:6px;color:#3b82f6">${d.id} — ${d.node_type}</div>
 669:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span>Volt:</span><b>${n.voltage?.toFixed(3)} V</b></div>
 670:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span>Freq:</span><b>${n.frequency?.toFixed(2)} Hz</b></div>
 671:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span>Load:</span><b>${n.load?.toFixed(2)} MW</b></div>
 672:               <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><span>Gen:</span><b>${n.generation?.toFixed(2)} MW</b></div>
 673:               ${switchInfo}
 674:               <div style="margin-top:6px;font-weight:600;color:${n.failed?'#ef4444':n.isolated?'#eab308':'#22c55e'}">${n.failed?'FAILED':n.isolated?'ISOLATED':'ONLINE'}</div>
 675:               ${faultOverlay}
 676:             `)
 677:         }
 678:       })
 679:       .on('mousemove', e => tip.style('left', (e.clientX + 16) + 'px').style('top', (e.clientY - 10) + 'px'))
 680:       .on('mouseout',  () => tip.style('opacity', 0))
 681: 
 682:     nodeEnter.append('path').attr('class', 'main-shape')
 683:     nodeEnter.append('text').attr('class', 'icon-text')
 684:       .attr('text-anchor', 'middle').attr('dominant-baseline', 'central')
 685:       .style('pointer-events', 'none')
 686:     nodeEnter.append('text').attr('class', 'label-text')
 687:       .attr('text-anchor', 'middle').attr('dy', 22)
 688:       .style('font-size', '10px').style('font-family', 'JetBrains Mono')
 689:       .style('font-weight', '600').style('fill', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.8)')
 690:       .style('pointer-events', 'none')
 691:       .text(d => d.id)
 692: 
 693:     const nodeMerge = nodeEnter.merge(nodeSel)
 694: 
 695:     nodeMerge
 696:       .style('opacity', d => !selectedNode ? 1 : (connected.has(d.id) ? 1 : 0.18))
 697:       .attr('transform', d => `translate(${d.x},${d.y})`)
 698: 
 699:     nodeMerge.select('.main-shape')
 700:       .attr('d',    d => getShape(d.node_type))
 701:       .attr('fill', d => {
 702:         if ((currentMode === MODES.FAIL_NODE || currentMode === MODES.DELETE_NODE) && !d.is_scada) return '#ff3333'
 703:         if (currentMode === MODES.CONNECT && interactionState.activeSrcNode?.id === d.id) return '#ffaa00'
 704:         if (selectedNode === d.id) return '#33ff33'
 705:         if (d.is_scada) return 'none' // remove background for SCADA node outline
 706:         return getNodeColor(d)
 707:       })
 708:       .attr('fill-opacity', d => d.is_scada ? 0 : 1.0)
 709:       .attr('stroke', d => d.is_scada ? '#33ff33' : '#ffffff')
 710:       .attr('stroke-dasharray', d => d.is_scada ? '4 4' : '0')
 711:       .attr('stroke-width', d => (selectedNode === d.id || d.is_scada) ? 2 : 0)
 712: 
 713:     nodeMerge.select('.icon-text')
 714:       .text(d => getIcon(d.node_type))
 715:       .style('font-size', d => d.node_type === 'substation' ? '14px' : '11px')
 716: 
 717:     // ── Voltage stress ring: physics-only indicator ─────────────────────
 718:     // Shows amber/red pulsing halo when voltage < 0.95 pu (under-voltage stress)
 719:     // This is driven EXCLUSIVELY by node.voltage from the backend physics engine.
 720:     const voltageRingGroup = root.select('.nodes').selectAll('g.voltage-ring')
 721:       .data(nodes.filter(d => !d.failed && !d.isolated && (d.voltage ?? 1.0) > 0 && (d.voltage ?? 1.0) < 0.95), d => d.id)
 722: 
 723:     const voltageRingEnter = voltageRingGroup.enter().append('g').attr('class', 'voltage-ring')
 724:     voltageRingEnter.append('circle')
 725:       .attr('class', 'v-ring')
 726:       .attr('r', 16)
 727:       .attr('fill', 'none')
 728:       .attr('stroke-width', 2)
 729:       .style('pointer-events', 'none')
 730: 
 731:     voltageRingEnter.merge(voltageRingGroup)
 732:       .attr('transform', d => `translate(${d.x},${d.y})`)
 733:       .select('.v-ring')
 734:       .attr('stroke', d => (d.voltage ?? 1.0) < 0.90 ? '#ff4444' : '#ffcc00')
 735:       .attr('stroke-dasharray', '4 3')
 736:       .style('opacity', 0.85)
 737: 
 738:     voltageRingGroup.exit().remove()
 739: 
 740:     // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 741:     // STORAGE VISUALIZATION - Battery level indicator
 742:     // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 743:     const storageGroup = root.select('.nodes').selectAll('g.storage-level')
 744:       .data(nodes.filter(d => d.node_type === 'battery' || d.node_type === 'supercap'), d => d.id)
 745: 
 746:     const storageEnter = storageGroup.enter().append('g')
 747:       .attr('class', 'storage-level')
 748: 
 749:     // Battery level bar background
 750:     storageEnter.append('rect')
 751:       .attr('class', 'storage-bar-bg')
 752:       .attr('x', -18).attr('y', 28)
 753:       .attr('width', 36).attr('height', 5)
 754:       .attr('rx', 2)
 755:       .attr('fill', 'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)')
 756: 
 757:     // Battery level bar fill
 758:     storageEnter.append('rect')
 759:       .attr('class', 'storage-bar-fill')
 760:       .attr('x', -18).attr('y', 28)
 761:       .attr('width', 36).attr('height', 5)
 762:       .attr('rx', 2)
 763: 
 764:     // Storage label (percentage)
 765:     storageEnter.append('text')
 766:       .attr('class', 'storage-text')
 767:       .attr('text-anchor', 'middle')
 768:       .attr('dy', 39)
 769:       .style('font-size', '8px')
 770:       .style('font-family', 'JetBrains Mono')
 771:       .style('fill', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.7)')
 772:       .style('pointer-events', 'none')
 773: 
 774:     const storageMerge = storageEnter.merge(storageGroup)
 775: 
 776:     storageMerge.select('.storage-bar-fill')
 777:       .attr('fill', d => {
 778:         // Get battery level (0-1 range)
 779:         const level = d.battery_level || d.supercap_level || 0.5
 780:         // Color based on level: red (<30%) -> yellow (30-70%) -> green (>70%)
 781:         if (level < 0.3) return '#ff3333'
 782:         if (level < 0.7) return '#ffaa00'
 783:         return '#33ff33'
 784:       })
 785:       .attr('width', d => {
 786:         const level = d.battery_level || d.supercap_level || 0.5
 787:         return 36 * level
 788:       })
 789: 
 790:     storageMerge.select('.storage-text')
 791:       .text(d => {
 792:         const level = d.battery_level || d.supercap_level || 0.5
 793:         return `${Math.round(level * 100)}%`
 794:       })
 795: 
 796:     storageGroup.exit().remove()
 797: 
 798:     // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 799:     // PRIORITY LOAD VISUALIZATION - Hospital badge
 800:     // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 801:     const hospitalGroup = root.select('.nodes').selectAll('g.hospital-priority')
 802:       .data(nodes.filter(d => d.node_type === 'hospital'), d => d.id)
 803: 
 804:     const hospitalEnter = hospitalGroup.enter().append('g')
 805:       .attr('class', 'hospital-priority')
 806: 
 807:     // Priority shield icon
 808:     hospitalEnter.append('text')
 809:       .attr('class', 'priority-badge')
 810:       .attr('text-anchor', 'middle')
 811:       .attr('dy', -20)
 812:       .style('font-size', '10px')
 813:       .style('pointer-events', 'none')
 814:       .text('🛡️ PRI')
 815: 
 816:     const hospitalMerge = hospitalEnter.merge(hospitalGroup)
 817: 
 818:     // Make priority badge pulse when system is under stress
 819:     hospitalMerge.select('.priority-badge')
 820:       .attr('fill', d => {
 821:         // If hospital is cut off, show red; otherwise green
 822:         if (d.failed) return '#ff3333'
 823:         if (d.isolated) return '#ffaa00'
 824:         return '#33ff33'
 825:       })
 826:       .style('filter', d => {
 827:         if (d.failed || d.isolated) return 'drop-shadow(0 0 4px #ff3333)'
 828:         return 'drop-shadow(0 0 3px #33ff33)'
 829:       })
 830: 
 831:     hospitalGroup.exit().remove()
 832: 
 833:     nodeSel.exit().remove()
 834:   }, [gridState, aiState, currentMode, selectedNode, selectedEdge, interactionState, showFlow])
 835: 
 836:   const svgCursor = {
 837:     [MODES.CONNECT]:   'crosshair',
 838:     [MODES.CUT_EDGE]:  'not-allowed',
 839:     [MODES.DELETE_NODE]: 'not-allowed',
 840:     [MODES.ADD_NODE]:  'crosshair',
 841:     [MODES.FAIL_NODE]: 'pointer',
 842:     [MODES.SELECT]:    'default',
 843:   }[currentMode] ?? 'grab'
 844: 
 845:   // Flow status indicator config (BRIGHTENED)
 846:   const flowStatusConfig = {
 847:     flowing:   { color: '#33ff33', icon: '⚡', text: 'FLOWING' },
 848:     stopped:   { color: '#ff3333', icon: '⏹', text: 'STOPPED' },
 849:     rerouting: { color: '#ffaa00', icon: '↻', text: 'REROUTING' },
 850:     'no-flow': { color: '#aaaaaa', icon: '○', text: 'NO FLOW' },
 851:   }
 852:   const status = flowStatusConfig[flowStatus] || flowStatusConfig['no-flow']
 853: 
 854:   return (
 855:     <div style={{ position: 'relative', width: '100%', height: '100%' }}>
 856:       <svg
 857:         ref={svgRef}
 858:         width="100%" height="100%"
 859:         style={{ display: 'block', cursor: svgCursor, position: 'absolute', zIndex: 10 }}
 860:         onContextMenu={e => e.preventDefault()}
 861:       />
 862:       <canvas
 863:         ref={canvasRef}
 864:         style={{ position: 'absolute', top: 0, left: 0, width: '100%', height: '100%', zIndex: 5, pointerEvents: 'none' }}
 865:       />
 866:       {/* Flow Status Indicator */}
 867:       <div style={{
 868:         position: 'absolute',
 869:         top: 12,
 870:         right: 12,
 871:         display: 'flex',
 872:         alignItems: 'center',
 873:         gap: 6,
 874:         padding: '6px 12px',
 875:         background: 'rgba(15,23,42,0.9)',
 876:         border: `1px solid ${status.color}40`,
 877:         borderRadius: 6,
 878:         fontSize: 11,
 879:         fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono, monospace',
 880:         color: status.color,
 881:         boxShadow: `0 0 12px ${status.color}20`,
 882:       }}>
 883:         <span style={{ fontSize: 14 }}>{status.icon}</span>
 884:         <span style={{ fontWeight: 600, letterSpacing: 0.5 }}>{status.text}</span>
 885:       </div>
 886:     </div>
 887:   )
 888: }

   1: /**
   2:  * Dashboard.jsx — Main 3-panel dashboard page.
   3:  *
   4:  * Layout:
   5:  *  [LEFT]  ControlPanel  — 280px fixed

  17:
