  23: import Toolbar, { MODES } from '../components/Toolbar'
  24: 
  25: const POLL_INTERVAL = 2000  // ms
  26: 
  27: const ACTION_BADGE_COLOR_MAP = {
  28:   increase_generation: 'green',
  29:   use_battery:         'blue',
  30:   use_supercapacitor:  'cyan',
  31:   shift_load:          'yellow',
  32:   reroute_energy:      'purple',
  33: }
  34: 
  35: export default function Dashboard() {
  36:   const [gridState, setGridState]   = useState(null)
  37:   const [aiState, setAiState]       = useState({ latest: null, log: [] })
  38:   const [running, setRunning]       = useState(true)
  39:   const [backendOk, setBackendOk]   = useState(null)  // null=checking, true, false
  40:   const [statusMsg, setStatusMsg]   = useState('')
  41:   const [selectedNode, setSelectedNode] = useState('H0')
  42:   const [selectedEdge, setSelectedEdge] = useState(null)
  43: 
  44:   // CAD Mode State
  45:   const [currentMode, setCurrentMode] = useState(MODES.SELECT)
  46:   const [addNodeType, setAddNodeType] = useState('house')
  47:   const [interactionState, setInteractionState] = useState({})
  48:   const [showFlow, setShowFlow] = useState(true)
  49:   const [faultSimMode, setFaultSimMode] = useState(false)
  50:   const [aiAssistMode, setAiAssistMode] = useState(false)
  51: 
  52:   const timerRef = useRef(null)
  53: 
  54:   // ── Load initial state ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  55:   useEffect(() => {
  56:     getState()
  57:       .then(s => { setGridState(s); setBackendOk(true) })
  58:       .catch(() => setBackendOk(false))
  59:   }, [])
  60: 
  61:   // ── AI log updater ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  62:   const pushToLog = useCallback((ai, timestep) => {
  63:     if (!ai?.decision) return
  64:     const entry = {
  65:       timestep,
  66:       text: ai.decision.reasoning,
  67:       color: ai.decision.color,
  68:       time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-GB', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit' }),
  69:     }
  70:     setAiState(prev => ({
  71:       latest: { ...ai },
  72:       log: [...prev.log.slice(-19), entry],
  73:     }))
  74:   }, [])
  75: 
  76:   // ── Simulation step ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  77:   const doStep = useCallback(async () => {
  78:     try {
  79:       if (faultSimMode && Math.random() < 0.15) {
  80:          // Randomly inject a storm/fault during faultSimMode simulation
  81:          await triggerEvent('storm')
  82:       }
  83:       const result = await simulate()
  84:       setGridState(result.grid)
  85:       setBackendOk(true)
  86:       pushToLog(result.ai, result.grid.timestep)
  87:     } catch {
  88:       setBackendOk(false)
  89:     }
  90:   }, [pushToLog, faultSimMode])
  91: 
  92:   // ── Auto-poll ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  93:   useEffect(() => {
  94:     if (!running || !backendOk) {
  95:       clearInterval(timerRef.current)
  96:       return
  97:     }
  98:     timerRef.current = setInterval(doStep, POLL_INTERVAL)
  99:     return () => clearInterval(timerRef.current)
 100:   }, [running, backendOk, doStep])
 101: 
 102:   // ── Handlers from ControlPanel & Graph ─────────────────────────────
 103:   const handleUpdate = useCallback(state => setGridState(state), [])
 104:   const handleMessage = useCallback(msg => {
 105:     setStatusMsg(msg)
 106:     setTimeout(() => setStatusMsg(''), 5000)
 107:   }, [])
 108: 
 109:   const handleFailNode = useCallback(async (nid) => {
 110:     try {
 111:       const result = await triggerEvent('failure', nid)
 112:       setGridState(result.grid)
 113:       handleMessage(result.message)
 114:     } catch (e) {
 115:       handleMessage('❌ Error: ' + (e?.response?.data?.detail || e.message))
 116:     }
 117:   }, [handleMessage])
 118: 
 119:   const handleCutEdge = useCallback(async (u, v) => {
 120:     try {
 121:       const result = await cutEdge(u, v)
 122:       setGridState(result.grid)
 123:       handleMessage(result.message)
 124:       setSelectedEdge(null)
 125:     } catch (e) {
 126:       handleMessage('❌ Error: ' + (e?.response?.data?.detail || e.message))
 127:     }
 128:   }, [handleMessage])
 129: 
 130:   const handleReset = useCallback(async () => {
 131:     try {
 132:       const result = await resetGrid()
 133:       setGridState(result)
 134:       handleMessage('Grid Reset Successfully.')
 135:       setCurrentMode(MODES.SELECT)
 136:       setInteractionState({})
 137:     } catch (e) {
 138:       handleMessage('❌ Reset Error')
 139:     }
 140:   }, [handleMessage])
 141: 
 142:   const handleAddHouse = useCallback(async (node_id) => {
 143:     try {
 144:       const result = await addHouseAPI(node_id)
 145:       setGridState(result.grid)
 146:       handleMessage(result.message)
 147:     } catch (e) {
 148:       handleMessage('❌ Error adding house: ' + (e?.response?.data?.detail || e.message))
 149:     }
 150:   }, [handleMessage])
 151: 
 152:   // ── Failed node count ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 153:   const failedCount = gridState
 154:     ? Object.values(gridState.nodes || {}).filter(n => n.failed || n.isolated).length
 155:     : 0
 156: 
 157:   const storm = gridState?.storm_active
 158: 
 159:   // ── Backend offline screen ─────────────────────────────────────────
 160:   if (backendOk === false) {
 161:     return (
 162:       <div style={{
 163:         display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center',
 164:         justifyContent: 'center', height: '100vh', gap: 20,
 165:         background: 'var(--bg-deep)',
 166:       }}>
 167:         <div style={{ fontSize: 48 }}>⚠️</div>
 168:         <div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--accent-red)' }}>
 169:           Cannot connect to backend
 170:         </div>
 171:         <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', textAlign: 'center', maxWidth: 420 }}>
 172:           Make sure the FastAPI server is running:<br />
 173:           <code style={{ color: 'var(--accent-cyan)', background: 'rgba(0,212,255,0.08)',
 174:             padding: '4px 10px', borderRadius: 6, display: 'inline-block', marginTop: 8 }}>
 175:             cd backend &amp;&amp; python main.py
 176:           </code>
 177:         </div>
 178:         <button
 179:           className="btn btn-cyan"
 180:           onClick={() => {
 181:             setBackendOk(null)
 182:             getState().then(s => { setGridState(s); setBackendOk(true) }).catch(() => setBackendOk(false))
 183:           }}
 184:         >
 185:           🔄 Retry Connection
 186:         </button>
 187:       </div>
 188:     )
 189:   }
 190: 
 191:   return (
 192:     <div style={{
 193:       display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column',
 194:       height: '100vh', overflow: 'hidden',
 195:       background: 'var(--bg-deep)',
 196:     }}>
 197: 
 198:       {/* ── Top Header Bar ─────────────────────────────────────────── */}
 199:       <header style={{
 200:         display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
 201:         padding: '0 24px', height: 52, flexShrink: 0,
 202:         background: 'rgba(5,15,40,0.9)',
 203:         borderBottom: '1px solid rgba(0,212,255,0.12)',
 204:         backdropFilter: 'blur(12px)',
 205:       }}>
 206:         {/* Logo */}
 207:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12 }}>
 208:           <div style={{
 209:             width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 8,
 210:             background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #00d4ff, #00ff88)',
 211:             display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
 212:             fontSize: 18,
 213:           }}>⚡</div>
 214:           <div>
 215:             <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: 0.5, color: 'var(--text-primary)' }}>
 216:               AI Smart Grid
 217:             </div>
 218:             <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-muted)', letterSpacing: 1 }}>
 219:               SELF-HEALING NETWORK
 220:             </div>
 221:           </div>
 222:         </div>
 223: 
 224:         {/* Status badges */}
 225:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>
 226:           {gridState && (
 227:             <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-muted)', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono' }}>
 228:               T:{gridState.timestep}
 229:             </span>
 230:           )}
 231:           {storm && <span className="badge badge-yellow">🌩️ STORM</span>}
 232:           {failedCount > 0 && (
 233:             <span className="badge badge-red pulse-red">⚠️ {failedCount} FAILED</span>
 234:           )}
 235:           {failedCount === 0 && !storm && (
 236:             <span className="badge badge-green">
 237:               <span className="pulse" style={{ width: 6, height: 6, borderRadius: '50%',
 238:                 background: 'var(--accent-green)', display: 'inline-block', marginRight: 5 }} />
 239:               STABLE
 240:             </span>
 241:           )}
 242:           <span className={`badge ${backendOk ? 'badge-cyan' : 'badge-red'}`}>
 243:             {backendOk ? '🟢 ONLINE' : '🔴 OFFLINE'}
 244:           </span>
 245:         </div>
 246: 
 247:         {/* Controls */}
 248:         <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
 249:           <button
 250:             className="btn btn-cyan"
 251:             style={{ padding: '6px 14px', fontSize: 12 }}
 252:             disabled={running}
 253:             onClick={doStep}
 254:           >
 255:             ⏭ Forward Step Sequence
 256:           </button>
 257:         </div>
 258:       </header>
 259: 
 260:       {/* ── Toolbar ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
 261:       <div style={{ padding: '0 16px' }}>
 262:         <Toolbar
 263:           currentMode={currentMode} setCurrentMode={setCurrentMode}
 264:           addNodeType={addNodeType} setAddNodeType={setAddNodeType}
 265:           running={running} setRunning={setRunning}
 266:           showFlow={showFlow} setShowFlow={setShowFlow}
 267:           faultSimMode={faultSimMode} setFaultSimMode={setFaultSimMode}
 268:           aiAssistMode={aiAssistMode} setAiAssistMode={setAiAssistMode}
 269:           onReset={handleReset} loading={!gridState}
 270:         />
 271:       </div>
 272: 
 273:       {/* ── Status Message Toast ───────────────────────────────────── */}
 274:       {statusMsg && (
 275:         <div style={{
 276:           position: 'fixed', top: 64, left: '50%', transform: 'translateX(-50%)',
 277:           background: 'rgba(10,25,55,0.95)', border: '1px solid var(--border)',
 278:           borderRadius: 10, padding: '8px 20px', fontSize: 13,
 279:           color: 'var(--text-primary)', zIndex: 1000, maxWidth: 600,
 280:           backdropFilter: 'blur(12px)',
 281:           animation: 'slide-in 0.3s ease',
 282:         }}>
 283:           {statusMsg}
 284:         </div>
 285:       )}
 286: 
 287:       {/* ── Main 3-Panel Layout ────────────────────────────────────── */}
 288:       <main style={{
 289:         display: 'flex', flex: 1, gap: 0, overflow: 'hidden',
 290:         padding: '12px 16px', paddingTop: 8,
 291:       }}>
 292: 
 293:         {/* LEFT PANEL */}
 294:         <div style={{
 295:           width: 255, flexShrink: 0,
 296:           background: 'var(--bg-panel)',
 297:           border: '1px solid var(--border)',
 298:           borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
 299:           padding: '16px 14px',
 300:           marginRight: 12,
 301:           overflow: 'hidden',
 302:           backdropFilter: 'var(--glass-blur)',
 303:         }}>
 304:           <ControlPanel
 305:             gridState={gridState}
 306:             onUpdate={handleUpdate}
 307:             onMessage={handleMessage}
 308:             selectedNode={selectedNode}
 309:             setSelectedNode={setSelectedNode}
 310:           />
 311:         </div>
 312: 
 313:         {/* CENTER PANEL */}
 314:         <div style={{
 315:           flex: 1,
 316:           background: 'var(--bg-panel)',
 317:           border: `1px solid ${storm ? 'rgba(255,214,0,0.25)' : 'var(--border)'}`,
 318:           borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
 319:           overflow: 'hidden',
 320:           backdropFilter: 'var(--glass-blur)',
 321:           display: 'flex',
 322:           flexDirection: 'column',
 323:           ...(storm ? { boxShadow: '0 0 60px rgba(255,214,0,0.1)' } : {}),
 324:         }}>
 325:           {/* Center header */}
 326:           <div style={{
 327:             padding: '10px 20px',
 328:             borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)',
 329:             display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
 330:           }}>
 331:             <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-muted)', fontWeight: 600, letterSpacing: 1 }}>
 332:               ⚡ LIVE GRID VISUALIZATION
 333:             </span>
 334:             <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 16, fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-muted)', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
 335:               <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 5 }}>
 336:                 <span style={{ width: 18, height: 3, background: 'var(--accent-green)', display: 'inline-block', borderRadius: 2 }} />
 337:                 Healthy Node
 338:               </span>
 339:               <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 5 }}>
 340:                 <span style={{ width: 18, height: 3, background: 'var(--accent-yellow)', display: 'inline-block', borderRadius: 2 }} />
 341:                 Stressed Node
 342:               </span>
 343:               <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 5 }}>
 344:                 <span style={{ width: 18, height: 3, background: 'var(--accent-red)', display: 'inline-block', borderRadius: 2 }} />
 345:                 Failed Node
 346:               </span>
 347:               <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 5 }}>
 348:                 <svg width="18" height="6"><line x1="0" y1="3" x2="18" y2="3" stroke="var(--accent-cyan)" strokeWidth="3"/></svg>
 349:                 ⚡ Power Flow
 350:               </span>
 351:               <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 5 }}>
 352:                 <svg width="18" height="6">
 353:                   <line x1="0" y1="3" x2="18" y2="3" stroke="var(--accent-green)" strokeWidth="2" strokeDasharray="4 3"/>
 354:                 </svg>
 355:                 🧠 Control Signal
 356:               </span>
 357:               <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 5 }}>
 358:                 <svg width="18" height="6"><line x1="0" y1="3" x2="18" y2="3" stroke="var(--accent-red)" strokeWidth="3"/></svg>
 359:                 🔴 Fault Segment
 360:               </span>
 361:             </div>
 362:           </div>
 363: 
 364:           {/* Graph area */}
 365:           <div style={{ flex: 1, position: 'relative', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
 366:             {gridState ? (
 367:               <GridGraph
 368:                 gridState={gridState}
 369:                 aiState={aiState.latest}
 370:                 selectedNode={selectedNode}
 371:                 onSelectNode={setSelectedNode}
 372:                 selectedEdge={selectedEdge}
 373:                 onSelectEdge={setSelectedEdge}
 374:                 onFailNode={handleFailNode}
 375:                 onCutEdge={handleCutEdge}
 376:                 onAddHouse={handleAddHouse}
 377: 
 378:                 // CAD Mode Injection
 379:                 currentMode={currentMode}
 380:                 addNodeType={addNodeType}
 381:                 interactionState={interactionState}
 382:                 setInteractionState={setInteractionState}
 383:                 showFlow={showFlow}
 384:                 aiAssistMode={aiAssistMode}
 385:                 onMessage={handleMessage}
 386:                 onUpdate={handleUpdate}
 387:               />
 388:             ) : (
 389:               <div style={{
 390:                 display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
 391:                 height: '100%', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 12,
 392:               }}>
 393:                 <div style={{ fontSize: 32 }}>⚡</div>
 394:                 <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-muted)', fontSize: 14 }}>
 395:                   Connecting to grid...
 396:                 </div>
 397:               </div>
 398:             )}
 399:           </div>
 400: 
 401:           {/* Status Bar */}
 402:           <div style={{
 403:             height: 28, borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)', background: 'rgba(5,15,40,0.4)',
 404:             display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', padding: '0 16px', gap: 16,
 405:             fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-muted)', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono', flexShrink: 0
 406:           }}>
 407:             <span>Mode: <span style={{ color: 'var(--accent-cyan)' }}>{currentMode}</span></span>
 408:             <span>|</span>
 409:             <span>Selected: <span style={{ color: selectedNode ? 'var(--accent-green)' : 'inherit' }}>{selectedNode || 'NONE'}</span></span>
 410:           </div>
 411:         </div>
 412: 
 413:         {/* RIGHT PANEL */}
 414:         <div style={{
 415:           width: 295, flexShrink: 0,
 416:           background: 'var(--bg-panel)',
 417:           border: '1px solid var(--border)',
 418:           borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
 419:           padding: '16px 14px',
 420:           marginLeft: 12,
 421:           overflow: 'hidden',
 422:           backdropFilter: 'var(--glass-blur)',
 423:         }}>
 424:           <AIDecisionPanel aiState={aiState} gridState={gridState} />
 425:         </div>
 426: 
 427:       </main>
 428:     </div>
 429:   )
 430: }

FILE: frontend\src\services\api.js
================================================================================
   1: /**
   2:  * api.js — Axios service layer for the Smart Grid backend API.
   3:  * Uses Vite proxy to connect to backend (http://localhost:8000)
   4:  */
   5: 
   6: import axios from 'axios'
   7: 
   8: // Use '/api' to route through Vite proxy (defined in vite.config.js)
   9: const BASE_URL = '/api'
  10: 
  11: const api = axios.create({
  12:   baseURL: BASE_URL,
  13:   timeout: 10000,
  14:   headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  15: })
  16: 
  17: // ── Grid operations ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  18: 
  19: /** Get current grid state without stepping the simulation. */
  20: export const getState = () => api.get('/state').then(r => r.data)
  21: 
  22: /**
  23:  * Advance 1 timestep: runs grid physics, LSTM forecast, DQN decision.
  24:  * Returns { grid, ai: { predicted_load, decision, action_result, reward } }
  25:  */
  26: export const simulate = () => api.post('/simulate').then(r => r.data)
  27: 
  28: /** Reset grid to initial state. */
  29: export const resetGrid = () => api.post('/reset').then(r => r.data)
  30: 
  31: // ── User Grid Construction (CAD Modes) ──────────────────────────────────
  32: 
  33: export const addNode = (type, position) => api.post('/add_node', { type, position }).then(r => r.data)
  34: export const addEdge = (u, v) => api.post('/connect', { source: u, target: v }).then(r => r.data)
  35: export const cutEdge = (u, v) => api.post('/cut_edge', { source: u, target: v }).then(r => r.data)
  36: export const failNodeAPI = (node_id) => api.post('/fail_node', { node_id }).then(r => r.data)
  37: export const restoreNodeAPI = (node_id) => api.post('/restore_node', { node_id }).then(r => r.data)
  38: export const moveNodeAPI = (node_id, x, y) => api.put(`/nodes/${node_id}/move`, { x, y }).then(r => r.data)
  39: export const addHouseAPI = (node_id) => api.post('/command/add_house', { node_id }).then(r => r.data)
  40: export const deleteNodeAPI = (node_id) => api.delete(`/nodes/${node_id}`).then(r => r.data)
  41: 
  42: export const getAISuggestions = () => api.get('/ai/suggestions').then(r => r.data)
  43: export const getSuggestParent = (x, y) => api.post('/ai/suggest_parent', { x, y }).then(r => r.data)
  44: export const randomFaultAPI = () => api.post('/random_fault').then(r => r.data)
  45: 
  46: // ── Events ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  47: 
  48: /**
  49:  * Trigger a grid event.
  50:  * @param {string} type - 'failure' | 'storm' | 'clear_storm' | 'demand' | 'generation' | 'restore'
  51:  * @param {string|null} nodeId - required for 'failure' and 'restore'
  52:  * @param {number|null} amount - optional for 'demand' and 'generation'
  53:  */
  54: export const triggerEvent = (type, nodeId = null, amount = null) =>
  55:   api.post('/event', { type, node_id: nodeId, amount }).then(r => r.data)
  56: 
  57: // ── Prediction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  58: 
  59: /** Get LSTM prediction for a specific node. */
  60: export const predict = (nodeId = 'S0') =>
  61:   api.get('/predict', { params: { node_id: nodeId } }).then(r => r.data)
  62: 
  63: // ── Manual action ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  64: 
  65: /** Force a specific RL action by ID (0–4). */
  66: export const forceAction = (actionId) =>
  67:   api.post('/action', { action_id: actionId }).then(r => r.data)
  68: 
  69: // ── Utility ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  70: 
  71: /** Health check. */
  72: export const healthCheck = () =>
  73:   api.get('/health').then(r => r.data).catch(() => null)

================================================================================
FILE: frontend\vite.config.js
================================================================================
   1: import { defineConfig } from 'vite'
   2: import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react'
   3: 
   4: export default defineConfig({
   5:   plugins: [react()],
   6:   server: {
   7:     port: 5173,
   8:     proxy: {
   9:       '/api': {
  10:         target: 'http://localhost:8000',
  11:         changeOrigin: true,
  12:         rewrite: (path) => path.replace(/^\/api/, ''),
  13:       },
  14:     },
  15:   },
  16: })

FILE: index.html
================================================================================
   1: <!DOCTYPE html>
   2: <html lang="en">
   3: <head>
   4:     <meta charset="UTF-8">
   5:     <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
   6:     <title>AI-Powered Self-Healing Grid</title>
   7:     <style>
   8:         * {
   9:             margin: 0;
  10:             padding: 0;
  11:             box-sizing: border-box;
  12:         }
  13: 
  14:         body {
  15:             font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif;
  16:             background: #0a0a0f;
  17:             color: #e0e0e0;
  18:             overflow: hidden;
  19:         }
  20: 
  21:         .container {
  22:             display: flex;
  23:             height: 100vh;
  24:         }
  25:

  28:             flex: 1;
  29:             position: relative;
  30:             background: linear-gradient(135deg, #0d1117 0%, #161b22 100%);
  31:         }
  32: 
  33:         .grid-canvas {
  34:             width: 100%;
  35:             height: 100%;
  36:         }
  37: 
  38:         /* Side Panel - Always Visible */
  39:         .side-panel {
  40:             width: 320px;
  41:             background: #1a1a24;
  42:             border-left: 1px solid #2d2d3a;
  43:             display: flex;
  44:             flex-direction: column;
  45:             overflow: hidden;
  46:         }
  47: 
  48:         .panel-header {
  49:             padding: 16px;
  50:             background: #252532;
  51:             border-bottom: 1px solid #2d2d3a;
  52:         }

 566:     <script>
 567:         // Grid data structure
 568:         const gridData = {
 569:             nodes: [
 570:                 { id: 'SOURCE_1', x: 100, y: 300, type: 'source', label: 'F1' },
 571:                 { id: 'SOURCE_2', x: 700, y: 300, type: 'source', label: 'F2' },
 572:                 { id: 'SW_1', x: 200, y: 300, type: 'switch', label: 'SW1' },
 573:                 { id: 'SW_2', x: 300, y: 300, type: 'switch', label: 'SW2' },
 574:                 { id: 'SW_3', x: 400, y: 300, type: 'switch', label: 'SW3' },
 575:                 { id: 'SW_4', x: 600, y: 300, type: 'switch', label: 'SW4' },
 576:                 { id: 'SW_5', x: 500, y: 300, type: 'switch', label: 'SW5' },
 577:                 { id: 'LOAD_A', x: 300, y: 200, type: 'load', priority: 'critical', label: 'Hospital' },
 578:                 { id: 'LOAD_B', x: 400, y: 400, type: 'load', priority: 'high', label: 'School' },
 579:                 { id: 'LOAD_C', x: 500, y: 200, type: 'load', priority: 'normal', label: 'Residential' }
 580:             ],
 581:             edges: [
 582:                 { from: 'SOURCE_1', to: 'SW_1', isSwitch: true },
 583:                 { from: 'SW_1', to: 'SW_2', isSwitch: true },
 584:                 { from: 'SW_2', to: 'LOAD_A', isSwitch: false },
 585:                 { from: 'SW_2', to: 'SW_3', isSwitch: true },
 586:                 { from: 'SW_3', to: 'LOAD_B', isSwitch: false },
 587:                 { from: 'SOURCE_2', to: 'SW_4', isSwitch: true },
 588:                 { from: 'SW_4', to: 'SW_5', isSwitch: true },
 589:                 { from: 'SW_5', to: 'LOAD_C', isSwitch: false },
 590:                 { from: 'SW_3', to: 'SW_5', isSwitch: true, isTie: true }
 591:             ],
 592:             fault: null,
 593:             restorationPath: null
 594:         };
 595: 
 596:         // Canvas setup
 597:         const canvas = document.getElementById('gridCanvas');
 598:         const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
 599: 
 600:         function resizeCanvas() {
 601:             canvas.width = canvas.parentElement.clientWidth;
 602:             canvas.height = canvas.parentElement.clientHeight;
 603:             drawGrid();
 604:         }
 605: 
 606:         window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas);
 607: 
 608:         function drawGrid() {
 609:             ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
 610: 
 611:             // Draw edges
 612:             gridData.edges.forEach(edge => {
 613:                 const from = gridData.nodes.find(n => n.id === edge.from);
 614:                 const to = gridData.nodes.find(n => n.id === edge.to);
 615: 
 616:                 ctx.beginPath();
 617:                 ctx.moveTo(from.x, from.y);
 618:                 ctx.lineTo(to.x, to.y);
 619: 
 620:                 if (gridData.fault &&
 621:                     ((edge.from === gridData.fault.from && edge.to === gridData.fault.to) ||
 622:                      (edge.from === gridData.fault.to && edge.to === gridData.fault.from))) {
 623:                     // Faulted line
 624:                     ctx.strokeStyle = '#f85149';
 625:                     ctx.lineWidth = 4;
 626:                     ctx.setLineDash([5, 5]);
 627:                 } else if (gridData.restorationPath &&
 628:                     gridData.restorationPath.includes(edge.from) &&
 629:                     gridData.restorationPath.includes(edge.to)) {
 630:                     // Restoration path
 631:                     ctx.strokeStyle = '#3fb950';
 632:                     ctx.lineWidth = 4;
 633:                     ctx.setLineDash([]);
 634:                 } else {
 635:                     // Normal line
 636:                     ctx.strokeStyle = edge.isTie ? '#a371f7' : '#30363d';
 637:                     ctx.lineWidth = edge.isTie ? 3 : 2;
 638:                     ctx.setLineDash(edge.isTie ? [10, 5] : []);
 639:                 }
 640: 
 641:                 ctx.stroke();
 642:                 ctx.setLineDash([]);
 643:             });
 644: 
 645:             // Draw nodes
 646:             gridData.nodes.forEach(node => {
 647:                 ctx.beginPath();
 648:                 ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, 12, 0, Math.PI * 2);
 649: 
 650:                 // Fill based on type
 651:                 switch(node.type) {
 652:                     case 'source':
 653:                         ctx.fillStyle = '#3fb950';
 654:                         break;
 655:                     case 'switch':
 656:                         ctx.fillStyle = '#a371f7';
 657:                         break;
 658:                     case 'load':
 659:                         if (node.priority === 'critical') ctx.fillStyle = '#f85149';
 660:                         else if (node.priority === 'high') ctx.fillStyle = '#d29922';
 661:                         else ctx.fillStyle = '#58a6ff';
 662:                         break;
 663:                 }
 664: 
 665:                 ctx.fill();
 666: 
 667:                 // Border
 668:                 ctx.strokeStyle = '#fff';
 669:                 ctx.lineWidth = 2;
 670:                 ctx.stroke();
 671: 
 672:                 // Label
 673:                 ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
 674:                 ctx.font = '11px sans-serif';
 675:                 ctx.textAlign = 'center';
 676:                 ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
 677:                 ctx.fillText(node.label, node.x, node.y);
 678:             });
 679:         }
 680: 
 681:         let currentFault = null;
 682:         let restorationPlan = null;
 683: 
 684:         function simulateFault() {
 685:             // Simulate fault between SW_2 and LOAD_A
 686:             currentFault = { from: 'SW_2', to: 'LOAD_A' };
 687:             gridData.fault = currentFault;
 688: 
 689:             document.getElementById('systemStatus').textContent = '⚠ FAULT DETECTED';
 690:             document.getElementById('systemStatus').classList.add('fault');
 691: 
 692:             // Generate restoration plan
 693:             generateRestorationPlan();
 694:             drawGrid();
 695: 
 696:             // Show AI overlay
 697:             showAIAssist();
 698:         }
 699: 
 700:         function generateRestorationPlan() {
 701:             // Simulated AI calculation with normalized scoring
 702:             restorationPlan = {
 703:                 faultLocation: 'SW_2 → LOAD_A',
 704:                 isolatedLoads: ['LOAD_A'],
 705:                 restorationPath: ['SOURCE_2', 'SW_4', 'SW_5', 'SW_3', 'SW_2', 'LOAD_A'],
 706:                 sourceFeeder: 'F2',
 707:                 metrics: {
 708:                     R_norm: 0.45,
 709:                     V_norm: 0.32,
 710:                     S_norm: 0.60,
 711:                     P_norm: 1.00,  // Critical hospital priority
 712:                     finalScore: 0.32
 713:                 },
 714:                 switchingSteps: [
 715:                     { action: 'CLOSE', target: 'TIE_1', reason: 'Connect alternate feeder F2 to isolated section' },
 716:                     { action: 'VERIFY', target: 'LOAD_A', reason: 'Confirm hospital power restored' }
 717:                 ],
 718:                 alternatives: 2
 719:             };
 720: 
 721:             gridData.restorationPath = restorationPlan.restorationPath;
 722:         }
 723: 
 724:         function showAIAssist() {
 725:             const overlay = document.getElementById('aiOverlay');
 726:             overlay.classList.add('active');
 727: 
 728:             if (restorationPlan) {
 729:                 const content = document.getElementById('restorationContent');
 730:                 content.innerHTML = `
 731:                     <div style="margin-bottom: 20px;">
 732:                         <h3 style="color: #f85149; margin-bottom: 10px;">⚠ Fault Detected</h3>

================================================================================
FILE: inference.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: inference.py — Multi-Step Agent Inference Script
   3: AI Self-Healing Smart Grid — Submission-Level Agent Loop
   4: 
   5: Runs a [START] → [STEP] × N → [END] agent inference loop
   6: against the simulation environment server (Flask app on port 5000).
   7: 
   8: Fixed Issues:
   9:   ✅ ISSUE 1 — Port corrected to 5000 (matches server/app.py Flask server)
  10:   ✅ ISSUE 2 — workflow_context reads from 'previous_decisions' (correct field)
  11:   ✅ ISSUE 3 — sentiment reads from 'customer_sentiment' (not hardcoded)
  12:   ✅ ISSUE 4 — Duplicate exception handlers removed (single clean block)
  13: 
  14: Usage:
  15:     python inference.py
  16:     OR
  17:     set ENV_URL=http://localhost:5000 && python inference.py
  18: """
  19: 
  20: from __future__ import annotations
  21: 
  22: import os
  23: import json
  24: import time
  25: import random
  26: import requests
  27: from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple
  28: 
  29: 
  30: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  31: # Environment Configuration
  32: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  33: 
  34: def get_environment_config() -> Dict[str, str]:
  35:     """
  36:     Returns environment configuration from env vars with safe defaults.
  37: 
  38:     ISSUE 1 FIX: env_url default changed from :8000 to :5000
  39:     (Flask server in app.py runs on port 5000)
  40:     """
  41:     return {
  42:         "api_base_url": os.getenv("API_BASE_URL", "http://localhost:11434/v1"),
  43:         "model_name":   os.getenv("MODEL_NAME",   "llama2"),
  44:         "hf_token":     os.getenv("HF_TOKEN",      ""),
  45:         "env_url":      os.getenv("ENV_URL",        "http://localhost:5000"),  # ✅ FIX 1
  46:         "api_key":      os.getenv("HF_TOKEN",       "not-needed-for-local"),
  47:     }
  48: 
  49: 
  50: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  51: # Environment Communication
  52: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  53: 
  54: def get_observation(env_url: str, session_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
  55:     """
  56:     Fetches the current observation from the simulation environment.
  57:     Returns None on any network or server error.
  58:     """
  59:     try:
  60:         response = requests.get(
  61:             f"{env_url}/api/grid/state",
  62:             params={"session_id": session_id},
  63:             timeout=10,
  64:         )
  65:         response.raise_for_status()
  66:         return response.json()
  67:     except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
  68:         print(f"  [WARN] Network error fetching observation: {e}")
  69:         return None
  70:     except Exception as e:
  71:         print(f"  [WARN] Unexpected error fetching observation: {e}")
  72:         return None
  73: 
  74: 
  75: def submit_action(env_url: str, session_id: str, action: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
  76:     """
  77:     Submits the chosen action to the simulation environment.
  78:     Returns the step result or None on error.
  79:     """
  80:     try:
  81:         response = requests.post(
  82:             f"{env_url}/api/fault/simulate",
  83:             json={**action, "session_id": session_id},
  84:             timeout=10,
  85:         )
  86:         response.raise_for_status()
  87:         return response.json()
  88:     except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
  89:         print(f"  [WARN] Network error submitting action: {e}")
  90:         return None
  91:     except Exception as e:
  92:         print(f"  [WARN] Unexpected error submitting action: {e}")
  93:         return None
  94: 
  95: 
  96: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  97: # Reward & Scoring
  98: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  99: 
 100: def compute_reward(observation: Dict[str, Any], action: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:
 101:     """
 102:     Computes the reward for the given observation-action pair.
 103: 
 104:     Reward components:
 105:       +2.0  per node close to nominal voltage
 106:       +1.0  per stable frequency
 107:       -5.0  per failed node
 108:       -1.0  per high-stress node
 109:     """
 110:     reward = 0.0
 111:     nodes = observation.get("nodes", {})
 112: 
 113:     for node_id, node in nodes.items():
 114:         node_type = node.get("type", "")
 115:         loads     = node.get("loads", [])
 116: 
 117:         # Voltage stability proxy: fewer critical loads = more stable
 118:         crit = sum(1 for l in loads if l.get("priority") == "CRITICAL")
 119:         norm = sum(1 for l in loads if l.get("priority") != "CRITICAL")
 120: 
 121:         if crit == 0 and norm > 0:
 122:             reward += 2.0   # nominal voltage proxy
 123:         if crit > 0:
 124:             reward -= 5.0   # failed/stressed node penalty
 125: 
 126:     # Action quality bonus (restoring ties is rewarded)
 127:     action_type = action.get("type", "")
 128:     if action_type in ("ADD_TIE_SWITCH", "reroute"):
 129:         reward += 1.0
 130: 
 131:     return round(reward, 2)
 132: 
 133: 
 134: def normalize_score(raw_reward: float,
 135:                     min_r: float = -20.0,
 136:                     max_r: float = 10.0) -> float:
 137:     """
 138:     Normalizes reward to [0, 1] scale for submission scoring.
 139:     Clamps to [min_r, max_r] before normalizing.
 140:     """
 141:     clamped = max(min_r, min(max_r, raw_reward))
 142:     return round((clamped - min_r) / (max_r - min_r), 4)
 143: 
 144: 
 145: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 146: # Strategy & Action Selection
 147: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 148: 
 149: def select_action_llm(observation: Dict[str, Any],
 150:                       workflow_context: Dict[str, Any],
 151:                       sentiment: str,
 152:                       config: Dict[str, str]) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
 153:     """
 154:     Attempts to select an action via local LLM (Ollama / HF endpoint).
 155:     Returns None if LLM is unavailable or returns an invalid response.
 156:     """
 157:     prompt = _build_prompt(observation, workflow_context, sentiment)
 158: 
 159:     try:
 160:         response = requests.post(
 161:             f"{config['api_base_url']}/chat/completions",
 162:             headers={
 163:                 "Authorization": f"Bearer {config['api_key']}",
 164:                 "Content-Type":  "application/json",
 165:             },
 166:             json={
 167:                 "model":       config["model_name"],
 168:                 "messages":    [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
 169:                 "temperature": 0.0,   # deterministic for reproducibility
 170:                 "max_tokens":  256,
 171:             },
 172:             timeout=15,
 173:         )
 174:         response.raise_for_status()
 175:         result    = response.json()
 176:         raw_text  = result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
 177:         action    = json.loads(raw_text)
 178:         return action
 179:     except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
 180:         print(f"  [LLM] Network error: {e} — falling back to heuristic")
 181:         return None
 182:     except Exception as e:
 183:         print(f"  [LLM] Parse/unexpected error: {e} — falling back to heuristic")
 184:         return None
 185: 
 186: 
 187: def select_action_heuristic(observation: Dict[str, Any],
 188:                              workflow_context: Dict[str, Any],
 189:                              sentiment: str,
 190:                              step: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 191:     """
 192:     Deterministic heuristic fallback action selector.
 193: 
 194:     Strategy:
 195:       - If any critical node exists → attempt fault restoration
 196:       - If sentiment is negative    → shift load to reduce stress
 197:       - Default                     → routine monitoring
 198:     """
 199:     nodes    = observation.get("nodes", {})
 200:     edges    = observation.get("edges", [])
 201: 
 202:     has_critical = any(
 203:         any(l.get("priority") == "CRITICAL" for l in n.get("loads", []))
 204:         for n in nodes.values()
 205:     )
 206:     has_tie_available = any(e.get("is_tie", False) and not e.get("is_switch", True)
 207:                             for e in edges)
 208: 
 209:     # Priority 1: restore via tie switch if fault + tie available
 210:     if has_critical and has_tie_available:
 211:         tie_edges = [e for e in edges if e.get("is_tie", False)]
 212:         chosen    = random.choice(tie_edges) if tie_edges else edges[0] if edges else {}
 213:         return {
 214:             "type":       "ADD_TIE_SWITCH",
 215:             "u":          chosen.get("source", "bus1"),
 216:             "v":          chosen.get("target", "bus2"),
 217:             "reason":     "Critical load detected — closing tie switch for restoration",
 218:             "step":       step,
 219:         }
 220: 
 221:     # Priority 2: load shedding on negative sentiment
 222:     if sentiment in ("negative", "very_negative"):
 223:         return {
 224:             "type":   "shift_load",
 225:             "amount": 0.15,
 226:             "reason": f"Negative sentiment ({sentiment}) — deferring non-critical loads",
 227:             "step":   step,
 228:         }
 229: 
 230:     # Default: routine action (round-robin over stable controls)
 231:     actions = ["monitor", "increase_generation", "use_battery"]
 232:     return {
 233:         "type":   actions[step % len(actions)],
 234:         "reason": "Routine grid monitoring and balancing",
 235:         "step":   step,
 236:     }
 237: 
 238: 
 239: def _build_prompt(observation: Dict[str, Any],
 240:                   workflow_context: Dict[str, Any],
 241:                   sentiment: str) -> str:
 242:     """Builds a concise, structured prompt for the LLM action selector."""
 243:     nodes_summary = [
 244:         {"id": n.get("id"), "type": n.get("type"), "loads": len(n.get("loads", []))}
 245:         for n in list(observation.get("nodes", {}).values())[:5]   # limit for token budget
 246:     ]
 247:     return (
 248:         f"You are a smart grid control AI. Your task is to choose the best action.\n\n"
 249:         f"Current Grid State (partial):\n{json.dumps(nodes_summary, indent=2)}\n\n"
 250:         f"Previous Decisions:\n{json.dumps(workflow_context, indent=2)}\n\n"
 251:         f"Customer Sentiment: {sentiment}\n\n"
 252:         f"Respond ONLY with a JSON object like:\n"
 253:         f'{{"type": "ADD_TIE_SWITCH", "u": "bus1", "v": "bus2", "reason": "..."}}\n'
 254:         f"or:\n"
 255:         f'{{"type": "shift_load", "amount": 0.15, "reason": "..."}}'
 256:     )
 257: 
 258: 
 259: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 260: # Escalation Logic
 261: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 262: 
 263: def check_escalation(observation: Dict[str, Any], cumulative_reward: float) -> bool:
 264:     """
 265:     Returns True if the situation requires escalation to human operator.
 266: 
 267:     Escalation triggers:
 268:       - 3+ critical nodes simultaneously
 269:       - Cumulative reward below -10 (system degrading)
 270:     """
 271:     nodes    = observation.get("nodes", {})
 272:     crit_cnt = sum(
 273:         1 for n in nodes.values()
 274:         if any(l.get("priority") == "CRITICAL" for l in n.get("loads", []))
 275:     )
 276:     if crit_cnt >= 3:
 277:         print(f"  [ESCALATE] {crit_cnt} critical nodes — escalating to human operator")
 278:         return True
 279:     if cumulative_reward < -10.0:
 280:         print(f"  [ESCALATE] Cumulative reward {cumulative_reward:.2f} below threshold")
 281:         return True
 282:     return False
 283: 
 284: 
 285: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 286: # Main Inference Loop  [START] → [STEP] × N → [END]
 287: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 288: 
 289: def run_inference(max_steps: int = 5) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 290:     """
 291:     Runs the full multi-step agent inference loop.
 292: 
 293:     Format:
 294:         [START]        — initialise session
 295:         [STEP 1..N]    — observe → decide → act → reward
 296:         [END]          — summarise results
 297: 
 298:     Returns a summary dict with steps, total reward, and normalized score.
 299:     """
 300:     config     = get_environment_config()
 301:     env_url    = config["env_url"]
 302:     session_id = f"session_{int(time.time())}_{random.randint(1000, 9999)}"
 303: 
 304:     print("=" * 60)
 305:     print("  AI Smart Grid — Inference Agent")
 306:     print(f"  Server  : {env_url}")
 307:     print(f"  Session : {session_id}")
 308:     print(f"  Steps   : {max_steps}")
 309:     print("=" * 60)
 310: 
 311:     # ── [START] ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 312:     print("\n[START]")
 313:     print(f"  Connecting to environment at {env_url} ...")
 314: 
 315:     history: list[Dict[str, Any]] = []
 316:     cumulative_reward  = 0.0
 317:     previous_decisions: Dict[str, Any] = {}   # ✅ FIX 2: correct field name
 318: 
 319:     # ── [STEP Loop] ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
 320:     for step in range(1, max_steps + 1):
 321:         print(f"\n[STEP {step}/{max_steps}]")
 322: 
 323:         # 1. Observe
 324:         observation = get_observation(env_url, session_id)
 325:         if observation is None:
 326:             print(f"  [ERROR] Could not fetch observation. Skipping step {step}.")
 327:             time.sleep(1)
 328:             continue
 329: 
 330:         # ── ISSUE 2 FIX: read 'previous_decisions' not 'workflow_context' ──
 331:         workflow_context = observation.get("previous_decisions", {})   # ✅ FIX 2
 332:         if not workflow_context and previous_decisions:
 333:             workflow_context = previous_decisions   # use local memory as fallback
 334: 
 335:         # ── ISSUE 3 FIX: read 'customer_sentiment' not hardcoded 'neutral' ──
 336:         sentiment = observation.get("customer_sentiment", "neutral")   # ✅ FIX 3
 337: 
 338:         print(f"  Nodes       : {len(observation.get('nodes', {}))}")
 339:         print(f"  Sentiment   : {sentiment}")
 340:         print(f"  Prev context: {len(workflow_context)} key(s)")
 341: 
 342:         # 2. Decide (LLM first, heuristic fallback)
 343:         action = select_action_llm(observation, workflow_context, sentiment, config)
 344:         if action is None:
 345:             action = select_action_heuristic(observation, workflow_context, sentiment, step)
 346:             print(f"  Strategy    : HEURISTIC → {action['type']}")
 347:         else:
 348:             print(f"  Strategy    : LLM → {action['type']}")
 349: 
 350:         print(f"  Reason      : {action.get('reason', 'n/a')}")
 351: 
 352:         # 3. Act
 353:         result = submit_action(env_url, session_id, action)
 354:         step_reward = compute_reward(observation, action)
 355:         cumulative_reward += step_reward
 356: 
 357:         # 4. Log step
 358:         step_log = {
 359:             "step":            step,
 360:             "action_type":     action.get("type"),
 361:             "sentiment":       sentiment,
 362:             "reward":          step_reward,
 363:             "cumulative":      round(cumulative_reward, 2),
 364:             "server_response": result.get("status", "no_response") if result else "error",
 365:         }
 366:         history.append(step_log)
 367: 
 368:         # Update local memory of previous decisions
 369:         previous_decisions[f"step_{step}"] = {
 370:             "action": action.get("type"),
 371:             "reward": step_reward,
 372:         }
 373: 
 374:         print(f"  Reward      : {step_reward:+.2f}  (cumulative: {cumulative_reward:+.2f})")
 375: 
 376:         # 5. Escalation check
 377:         if check_escalation(observation, cumulative_reward):
 378:             print("  [ESCALATE] Breaking loop — human intervention required")
 379:             break
 380: 
 381:         time.sleep(0.3)   # small delay between steps
 382: 
 383:     # ── [END] ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 384:     print("\n[END]")
 385:     normalized = normalize_score(cumulative_reward)
 386:     print(f"  Steps completed  : {len(history)}/{max_steps}")
 387:     print(f"  Total reward     : {cumulative_reward:+.2f}")
 388:     print(f"  Normalized score : {normalized:.4f}  (0 = worst, 1 = best)")
 389:     print("=" * 60)
 390: 
 391:     summary = {
 392:         "session_id":       session_id,
 393:         "env_url":          env_url,
 394:         "steps_completed":  len(history),
 395:         "total_reward":     round(cumulative_reward, 2),
 396:         "normalized_score": normalized,
 397:         "history":          history,
 398:     }
 399:     return summary
 400: 
 401: 
 402: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 403: # Entry Point
 404: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 405: 
 406: if __name__ == "__main__":
 407:     result = run_inference(max_steps=5)
 408:     print("\n--- Final Summary (JSON) ---")
 409:     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2))

FILE: main.txt

  97:     visited = set()
  98:     stack = [start]
  99:

 101:         node = stack.pop()
 102: 
 103:         for _, child, data in self.graph.out_edges(node, data=True):
 104:             if not data.get("active", True):
 105:                 continue
 106: 
 107:             if child not in visited:
 108:                 visited.add(child)

 173: ✅ ADD CONTINUOUS FLOW
 174: function drawFlow(ctx, edge, t) {
 175:   if (!edge.active || edge.flow < 0.01) return;
 176: 
 177:   const speed = 0.002 * edge.flow;
 178:   const progress = (t * speed) % 1;
 179: 
 180:   const x = edge.x1 + (edge.x2 - edge.x1) * progress;
 181:   const y = edge.y1 + (edge.y2 - edge.y1) * progress;
 182: 
 183:   ctx.beginPath();
 184:   ctx.moveTo(edge.x1, edge.y1);
 185:   ctx.lineTo(x, y);
 186: 
 187:   ctx.strokeStyle =
 188:     edge.source_type === "solar" ? "#FFD700" :
 189:     edge.source_type === "battery" ? "#FF00FF" :
 190:     edge.source_type === "wind" ? "#00BFFF" :
 191:     "#00FFCC";
 192: 
 193:   ctx.lineWidth = 3;
 194:   ctx.stroke();
 195: }
 196: ✅ ANIMATION LOOP

 198: 
 199: function animate() {
 200:   t += 16;
 201: 
 202:   ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
 203: 
 204:   edges.forEach(edge => drawFlow(ctx, edge, t));
